# 卖出并捆绑买入教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

卖出并捆绑买入功能现已支持 **Pump、PumpSwap、Raydium（AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM)、Bonk、Bonk-USD1 以及 Meteora** 等多种生态，适配不同类型的开盘与做市场景。

*   捆绑支持单地址，但单地址操作建议直接使用市值管理即可。
    
*   捆绑买或卖时地址之间不要留空行，否则会触发报错。
    

circle-check

**这里以 Pump 为例，Pump 卖出并捆绑买入：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/bundled-sell-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/bundled-sell-buy)

circle-info

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#pump-ru-he-mai-chu-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru-jiao-yi-huan-cang)

🧩如何进行卖出并捆绑买入 ？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F7qSZh9MscjxLBADveU9U%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39c106ef-77cd-4e61-8d83-9431f45c5aa3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7eb4aa6e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-2.-da-kai-mai-chu-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru-jie-mian)

**2\. 打开**卖出并捆绑买入**界面**

*   进入对应的卖出并捆绑买入操作页面。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FHBBwqfycnp8m5BOFnIh5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94269604-51f7-4ade-b003-a5ef547a4310&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3193416b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-3.-tian-xie-cao-zuo-xin-xi)

**3\. 填写操作信息**

*   **选择代币**：可选择当前连接钱包中的代币，或手动输入代币合约地址。
    
*   **卖出钱包设置**：
    
    *   手动输入粘贴私钥。
        
    *   设置卖出数量
        
    
    **买入钱包设置**：
    
    *   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
        
    *   刷新导入钱包余额
        
    *   设置买入数量
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FHMYqe9NgP4C9gboiobc2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D817b6e41-af0d-430a-8f6e-3ebac6b6fa2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1a0836c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-4.-she-zhi-jito-wan-cheng-mai-chu-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

**4\. 设置 Jito 完成**卖出并捆绑买入

*   选择适合的速率或自定义金额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FPYPTwq8gQRdxBecD1Iq5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3be5909b-4a70-4306-8e28-eaaa840ba716&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4c6d097&sv=2)

*   点击下方 **卖出并捆绑买入** 按钮即可完成购买。
    

circle-info

任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

⚠️ 注意事项

*   此功能支持多个地址同时捆绑买入，所有费用将由导入的第一个地址统一支付。
    
*   买入所需的 SOL 数量与代币价格直接相关，请确保买入钱包地址中的 SOL 余额充足。如交易失败，可尝试减少买入金额后重新操作。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-mai-chu-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

**1\.** 什么是卖出并捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：是指在同一个区块中完成代币卖出并由新地址立即买入，实现无缝换仓。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-2.-wei-shen-me-yao-yong-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru)

**2\.** 为什么要用新地址买入？

*   check
    
    答：使用新地址可规避链上图谱标记，减少被监控系统识别的风险。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-3.-zhe-zhong-cao-zuo-shi-fou-hui-bei-pan-ding-wei-la-pan-huo-shua-liang)

**3\.** 这种操作是否会被判定为拉盘或刷量？

*   check
    
    答：不会，若控制好节奏和金额，链上数据表现为正常换仓行为。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-4.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-duo-ge-xin-di-zhi-pi-liang-mai-ru)

**4\.** 是否支持多个新地址批量买入？

*   check
    
    答：支持，可指定多个目标地址以提高分散性和隐蔽性。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-5.-shi-yong-ci-gong-neng-shi-fou-xu-yao-pei-zhi-te-shu-can-shu)

**5\.** 使用此功能是否需要配置特殊参数？

*   check
    
    答：无需复杂设置，使用 CiaoTool 可一键捆绑执行，高效完成策略换仓。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# 捆绑买入教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

捆绑买入功能现已支持 **Pump、PumpSwap、Raydium（AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM)、Bonk、Bonk-USD1 以及 Meteora** 等多种生态，适配不同类型的开盘与做市场景。

*   捆绑支持单地址，但单地址操作建议直接使用市值管理即可。
    
*   捆绑买或卖时地址之间不要留空行，否则会触发报错。
    

circle-info

**这里以Raydium为例，Raydium捆绑买入：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/raydium/bundled-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/raydium/bundled-buy)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#pump-ru-he-kun-bang-mai-ru)

🧩 如何进行捆绑买入？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\.** 绑定钱包

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F7qSZh9MscjxLBADveU9U%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39c106ef-77cd-4e61-8d83-9431f45c5aa3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7eb4aa6e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-2.-da-kai-kun-bang-mai-ru-jie-mian)

2\. 打开捆绑买入界面

*   进入对应的捆绑买入操作页面。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FHBBwqfycnp8m5BOFnIh5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94269604-51f7-4ade-b003-a5ef547a4310&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3193416b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-3.-tian-xie-cao-zuo-xin-xi)

3\. 填写操作信息

*   **买入代币**：可选择当前连接钱包中的代币，或手动输入代币合约地址。
    
*   **捆绑买入钱包设置**：
    
    *   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
        
    *   刷新导入钱包余额
        
    *   设置买入数量
        
    *   批量操作删除资金不足的钱包
        
    

circle-exclamation

**注：**选择 **Bonk** 时，捆绑买入钱包设置数量差异。

1.  选择发送类型为 **JITO** 时，每组最多为9个钱包
    
2.  选择发送类型为 **RPC** 时，每组最多为10个钱包
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FQz6LRnu8TmxBY4vdd269%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66eb2a8a-d7a6-42a5-84c6-5139e44d2e71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0b63607&sv=2)

circle-info

**指定钱包地址（可选）**：默认代币会购买到对应钱包地址，**（仅Raydium可用）。**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-4.-she-zhi-jito-wan-cheng-can-shu-she-zhi)

4\. 设置 jito 完成参数设置

*   选择适合的速率或自定义金额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FPYPTwq8gQRdxBecD1Iq5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3be5909b-4a70-4306-8e28-eaaa840ba716&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4c6d097&sv=2)

*   点击下方 **捆绑买入** 按钮即可完成购买。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

⚙️ 注意事项

*   捆绑买入功能支持多个钱包分组同时参与。
    
*   **服务费说明**：所有服务费用由导入的 **第一个钱包** 支付，Jito 交易的小费由 **最后一个钱包** 支付。
    
*   **SOL 余额要求**：请确保你的账户有足够的金额。
    

circle-info

任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-kun-bang-mai-ru)

**1\.** 什么是捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：捆绑买入是指一次性打包多个地址或交易指令，统一发送买入请求，提高效率和优先级。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-2.-kun-bang-mai-ru-he-pu-tong-mai-ru-you-shen-me-qu-bie)

**2\.** 捆绑买入和普通买入有什么区别？

*   check
    
    答：捆绑买入更快、抗滑点能力强，并可借助 Jito 提高抢跑成功率。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-3.-kun-bang-mai-ru-shi-yong-jito-ji-shu-de-zuo-yong-shi-shen-me)

**3\.** 捆绑买入使用 Jito 技术的作用是什么？

*   check
    
    答：Jito 可将交易插入 MEV 优先池，提升确认速度，抢占低价区间。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-4.-shi-fou-xu-yao-duo-ge-qian-bao-cai-neng-kun-bang-mai-ru)

**4\.** 是否需要多个钱包才能捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：不需要多个钱包，也支持单地址多交易批量执行。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-5.-kun-bang-mai-ru-hui-zeng-jia-gas-fei-yong-ma)

**5\.** 捆绑买入会增加 Gas 费用吗？

*   check
    
    答：较普通交易略高，但在抢跑场景中通常成本远低于收益。

# 新地址买入(↑Holders) 教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

**新地址买入(↑Holders)** 功能现已支持 **Pump、PumpSwap、Raydium（AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM)、Bonk、Bonk-USD1 以及 Meteora** 等多种生态，适配不同类型的开盘与做市场景。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-makers-he-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-holders-de-qu-bie-shi-shen-me)

🆚 新地址买入(↑Makers) 和新地址买入(↑Holders)的区别是什么？

类型

主要增加

侧重点

↑ Makers

交易过的地址数

活跃度、成交参与感

↑ Holders

持币地址数

共识分布、长期持有人

circle-check

**这里以Pump为例，Pump 新地址买入(↑Holders)**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/newaddr-buyers-holdersarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/newaddr-buyers-holders)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#ru-he-jin-xing-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-holders)

🧩 **如何进行**新地址买入(↑Holders)**？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FnrnWyNbETFUmW4e6TyfO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D56b12c34-d9aa-4fdb-8139-d2170d78ad27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf65a328&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-2.-da-kai-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-holders-jie-mian)

**2\. 打开**新地址买入 (↑Holders) **界面**

*   进入对应的新地址买入 (↑Holders) 操作页面。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fc1FnYtBeB4vXMlyjR1pJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De52113d0-b25e-42da-9e87-118725c4e71e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46b650ef&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-3.-tian-xie-cao-zuo-xin-xi)

**3\. 填写操作信息**

*   **选择代币**：手动粘贴代币合约地址。
    
*   **设置买入地址数量：**最高可设置1000个钱包买入，可手动输入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fhw8Oslqsh5T5ru6LGHmd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D835d362e-b013-409b-91f3-e8873879ea26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e4324b3&sv=2)

*   **设置买入金额（SOL），**可随机设置区间范围**，**每个新地址的买入金额最少固定为 0.00001。
    
*   **生成钱包数量**：钱包数量为买入地址数量，请保存本地。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FHK3wp2dCOXRzCuRNjUJC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ac00d46-64ff-4bec-b68a-57e59f44cd8a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab09f742&sv=2)

*   **导入主钱包私钥：**检查钱包地址及余额
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FU0NaOj3TFJzVlvvrRffl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc83cbcdb-0254-49f7-b652-cd5cface6ac5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86755b9b&sv=2)

circle-info

1.  买入所产生的链上费用及平台服务费均由**主钱包**统一支付。页面底部会显示所需余额预估，请务必确保主钱包余额**高于预估金额**，否则可能导致交易失败。
    
2.  费用支付钱包为主钱包，但使用功能前仍需先**连接钱包**。当**「主钱包」**与**「已连接钱包」**不一致时，系统将从**主钱包扣费**；若两者一致，则无需额外处理，只需确保余额充足即可。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-4.-she-zhi-jito-mev-xiao-fei)

**4\. 设置Jito MEV 小费**

*   选择适合的线路或自定义金额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FUyZw759vdnYh7xi2en8G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7ecbdb8-fa7b-4cb3-b655-6b2fa3c06df4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71aac06b&sv=2)

*   点击下方 **开始买入** 按钮即可完成购买。
    

triangle-exclamation

**注意事项：**新地址买入的成本主要为Jito小费支出，请根据网络拥堵情况实时调整。功能开启后请勿刷新，刷新将会导致服务中断。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-1.-shen-me-shi-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-holders)

1\. 什么是“新地址买入↑Holders”？

*   check
    
    答： 指通过自动创建多个新钱包地址，并在开盘后为这些地址执行小额真实买入，从而提升链上持币地址数量。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-2.-wei-shen-me-ti-sheng-holder-shu-liang-dui-xiang-mu-you-li)

2\. 为什么提升 Holder 数量对项目有利？

*   check
    
    答： 平台的权重算法中，“持币地址数量”是判断项目热度与排名的重要维度，数量越高越容易被推荐。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-3.-ru-he-pi-liang-chuang-jian-xin-di-zhi)

3\. 如何批量创建新地址？

*   check
    
    答： 在 CiaoTool 中点击“一键生成地址”，可快速生成多个未使用的新钱包地址，并自动配置为买入目标。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-4.-zhe-xie-di-zhi-hui-shi-ji-wan-cheng-jiao-yi-ma)

4\. 这些地址会实际完成交易吗？

*   check
    
    答： 会。系统将为每个地址注入少量 SOL，并发起真实链上买入操作，确保交易可被链上索引和统计。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-5.-wo-ke-yi-kong-zhi-mai-ru-jinehe-di-zhi-shu-liang-ma)

5\. 我可以控制买入金额和地址数量吗？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可以设定每个地址的买入金额（例如 0.0001–0.001 SOL）和地址生成数量，系统将根据设定自动执行。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 市值管理教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

市值管理功能现已支持 **Pump、PumpSwap、Raydium（AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM)、Bonk、Bonk-USD1 以及 Meteora** 等多种生态，适配不同类型的开盘与做市场景。

circle-check

**这里以 Pump 为例，Pump 市值管理**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/market-makingarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/market-making)

circle-info

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#ru-he-jin-xing-shi-zhi-guan-li)

🧩 如何进行市值管理？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#dui-huan-she-zhi)

兑换设置

**价值代币：**

*   **Pump、PumpSwap、Bonk、以及 Meteora** 目前只支持Solana
    
*   **Bonk-USD1** 支持 World Liberty Financial USD
    
*   **Raydium** 支持 Solana、USDT 以及USD Coin
    

**做市代币：**可以选择当前连接钱包下的代币，也可以输入需要做市的代币地址

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252Fay85dITlW46E77AZXmj3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda59ae97-14d9-430d-95a3-78960252a6d8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f0618304&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#zuo-shi-ji-qi-ren-she-zhi)

🤖 【做市机器人设置】

circle-check

提供 **拉盘、砸盘、刷量机器** 这三种模式

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-1.-la-pan)

1\. 拉盘

**持续执行买入行为**

*   **单笔交易量 (SOL)：**每笔交易的买入量，若左右区间相同，则为固定金额，若区间金额不同，则为随机金额
    
*   **条件参数：**提供 【**目标价格、累计最大交易额、运行时长**】这三个条件参数。（若不填将持续进行交易，若填写任一参数，则当满足条件时，会自动停止任务。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F7fUn7NXPj4bn2mlBflGQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ff905f8-c058-41a2-906f-4336a5242625&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=949a3d21&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-2.-za-pan)

2\. 砸盘

**持续执行卖出行为**

*   **单笔交易量 ：**每笔交易的卖出代币量，若左右区间相同，则为固定金额，若区间金额不同，则为随机金额
    
*   **条件参数：**提供 【**目标价格、累计最大交易额、运行时长**】这三个条件参数。若不填将持续进行交易，若填写任一参数，则当满足条件时，会自动停止任务。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FvrbJxXfI4GTPFKUIRFnd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7ee24c67-1fa8-465e-9d99-5093b2770416&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c488ffbd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#tong-yong-can-shu-she-zhi)

3\. 刷量机器

持续执行 **随机买卖**

*   **单笔交易量 ：**每笔交易的买入或卖出的代币量，若左右区间相同，则为固定金额，若区间金额不同，则为随机金额
    
*   **条件参数：**提供【**累计最大交易额(SOL、运行时长**】这二个条件参数。若不填将持续进行交易，若填写任一参数，则当满足条件时，会自动停止任务。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F1O8XA5RgeGOPOQqOY39a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94cbcf4c-7d95-4f35-8502-5aa4f6d49a52&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6042d20&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#tong-yong-can-shu-she-zhi-1)

⚙️ 通用参数设置

*   **任务执行间隔：**每个钱包发起执行交易的间隔时间，为保证成功率，目前最低需设置为 5 秒
    
*   **滑点设置：**如果交易金额不大，同时需要快速交易的话，选择自动即可
    
*   **Jito EVM小费：**Jito 小费可以简单理解为 Solana 链上的另一个打包上链服务商，使用 Jito 打包交易，费用越高，交易上链速度越快。
    
*   如果要降低交易成本或者 Jito 模式成功率低的话，可以选择 **Jito 小费为 0** 走普通交易路线再次尝试。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FaAkRGR5IzmDQkoD4T8ot%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b0f3584-fe2d-40eb-9285-46932f575928&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4f96781b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#cao-zuo-qian-bao-she-zhi)

🔐 操作钱包设置

*   **导入私钥：**批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。导入私钥后，可刷新钱包余额以及排序钱包。
    
*   **实时统计：**任务执行过程中，会实时统计交易结果，也会实时刷新钱包余额
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FN1URocc1IB7diCMJvSVw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De8687300-0ae3-4bc1-95d4-e035cb8f4df5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=190fcb72&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#jiao-yi-ri-zhi)

📜 交易日志

*   整个过程为您**实时呈现交易日志**
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FIL8w3svhIj2qwSA4m0CN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73c87e25-cd02-498b-a7d2-75bbb90d8169&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7695f1e3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-1.-shen-me-shi-shi-zhi-guan-li)

**1\.** 什么是市值管理？

*   check
    
    答：市值管理是通过合理买卖、交易控制等方式维持代币的市场价格和流通表现，避免异常波动。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-2.-wei-shen-me-yao-jin-xing-shi-zhi-guan-li)

**2\.** 为什么要进行市值管理？

*   check
    
    答：防止项目初期价格异常上冲或下跌，有助于维持图表平稳，提升投资者信心。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-3.-ru-he-yong-xin-di-zhi-guan-li-shi-zhi)

**3\.** 如何用新地址管理市值？

*   check
    
    答：可通过多地址轮替买入或卖出，实现真实但分散的交易行为，降低被识别风险。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-4.-shi-fou-ke-yi-pi-liang-zhi-xing-shi-zhi-guan-li-cao-zuo)

**4\.** 是否可以批量执行市值管理操作？

*   check
    
    答：可以，配合 CiaoTool 的批量交易与地址分发功能，可快速完成精细化市值调控。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-5.-shi-zhi-guan-li-shi-fou-she-ji-wei-fa-huo-cao-zong-shi-chang-xing-wei)

**5\.** 市值管理是否涉及违法或操纵市场行为？

*   check
    
    答：仅为控制初期图表平稳、并不误导用户，属于策略性控盘，不构成市场操纵。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# 新地址买入(↑Makers) 教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

**新地址买入(↑Makers)** 功能现已支持 **Pump、PumpSwap、Raydium（AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM)、Bonk、Bonk-USD1 以及 Meteora** 等多种生态，适配不同类型的开盘与做市场景。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-makers-he-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-holders-de-qu-bie-shi-shen-me)

🆚 新地址买入(↑Makers) 和新地址买入(↑Holders)的区别是什么？

类型

主要增加

侧重点

↑ Makers

交易过的地址数量

活跃度、成交参与感

↑ Holders

持币地址数量

共识分布、长期持有人

circle-check

**这里以Pump为例，Pump 新地址买入(↑Makers)**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/newaddr-buyers-markersarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/newaddr-buyers-markers)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#pump-ru-he-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-zeng-jia-du-li-qian-bao-gou-mai-shu-liang)

🆕 如何进行新地址买入(↑Makers)?

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FWUKh7pBaisrclmCvXDVY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68dde481-27b8-491e-a007-402438e68aa1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=271feda2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-2.-da-kai-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-makers-jie-mian)

**2\. 打开**新地址买入 (↑Makers) **界面**

*   进入对应的新地址买入操作页面。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fc1FnYtBeB4vXMlyjR1pJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De52113d0-b25e-42da-9e87-118725c4e71e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46b650ef&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-3.-tian-xie-cao-zuo-xin-xi)

**3\. 填写操作信息**

*   **选择代币**：手动粘贴代币合约地址。
    
*   **设置买入地址数量：**最高可设置1000个钱包买入，可手动输入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fhw8Oslqsh5T5ru6LGHmd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D835d362e-b013-409b-91f3-e8873879ea26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2e4324b3&sv=2)

*   **设置买入金额（SOL），**可随机设置区间范围**，**每个新地址的买入金额最少固定为 0.00001。
    
*   **导入主钱包私钥：**检查钱包地址及余额
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FU0NaOj3TFJzVlvvrRffl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc83cbcdb-0254-49f7-b652-cd5cface6ac5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86755b9b&sv=2)

circle-info

1.  买入所产生的链上费用、SOL账户租金（可退回）及平台服务费均由**主钱包**统一支付。页面底部会显示所需余额预估，请务必确保主钱包余额**高于预估金额**，否则可能导致交易失败。
    
2.  费用支付钱包为主钱包，但使用功能前仍需先**连接钱包**。当**「主钱包」**与**「已连接钱包」**不一致时，系统将从**主钱包扣费**；若两者一致，则无需额外处理，只需确保余额充足即可。
    
3.  **SOL账户租金**每个地址需额外支付 **0.00203928**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-4.-she-zhi-jito-mev-xiao-fei)

**4\. 设置Jito MEV 小费**

*   选择适合的线路或自定义金额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FUyZw759vdnYh7xi2en8G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7ecbdb8-fa7b-4cb3-b655-6b2fa3c06df4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71aac06b&sv=2)

*   点击下方 **开始** 按钮即可完成购买。
    

triangle-exclamation

**注意事项：**新地址买入的成本主要为手续费支出。功能开启后请勿刷新，刷新将会导致服务中断。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#pump-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-jiao-yi-liu-cheng)

🔗 新地址买入运行流程

circle-exclamation

**Raydium 的CPMM和CLMM：**Token-2022 代币由于转账时手续费用会存在于账户内部状态，导致无法进行账户关闭，并回收租金至主钱包地址，请谨慎操作Token-2022代币。

1\. 主钱包向新钱包转账

2\. 新钱包购买代币

3\. 新钱包向主钱包转代币

4\. 新钱包关闭代币账户并回收租金

5\. 新钱包将剩余SOL转回主钱包

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-1.-xin-di-zhi-mai-ru-shi-shen-me-yi-si)

1\. 新地址买入是什么意思？

*   check
    
    答： 指使用全新未使用过的钱包地址，执行首次买入操作，**提升匿名性与图表美观度**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-2.-xin-di-zhi-yao-zen-me-sheng-cheng)

2\. 新地址要怎么生成？

*   check
    
    答： CiaoTool 支持全自动生成多个新地址，或手动导入你准备好的干净地址。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-3.-wei-shen-me-yao-yong-xin-di-zhi-er-bu-shi-jiu-qian-bao)

3\. 为什么要用新地址而不是旧钱包？

*   check
    
    答： 避免将老地址的历史标签带入新图表，**防止图表出现气泡、拉高警惕性**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-4.-ke-yi-she-zhi-duo-ge-xin-di-zhi-yi-qi-mai-ru-ma)

4\. 可以设置多个新地址一起买入吗？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。支持批量生成并配置最多 12 个地址一起进行分散买入操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/bundled-marketcap/new-makers#id-5.-wo-de-si-yao-hui-bei-bao-cun-ma)

5\. 我的私钥会被保存吗？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。CiaoTool 所有签名操作都在浏览器本地完成，**不上传、不存储私钥**，确保资金安全。

# Pump 开盘并买入教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump 开盘并买入**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buy)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#ru-he-jin-xing-kai-pan-bing-mai-ru)

🧩 如何进行开盘并买入？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-tui-jian-shi-yong-phantom-huan-ying-qian-bao)

1\. 绑定钱包 (推荐使用 Phantom-幻影钱包）

*   打开 Pump开盘并买入操作界面 ，
    
*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FFtHO32vs7DNP1xGfBKkt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90fdcd89-489a-4754-b9d2-0af37b9b6470&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5380a245&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-2.-tian-xie-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

**2\. 填写代币基础信息**

*   您可以手动填写代币信息，或者点击 **【克隆】** 按钮，克隆其他代币的信息
    
*   社媒信息为可选项，不是必填项。
    
*   设置当价格上涨超过X％时，自动卖出全部Token.
    

circle-info

如果打开**自动卖出**选项，建议您不要使用开发钱包购买，或在下面填写开发钱包的私钥参与购买。否则，销售时会要求您自动签名，可能会耽误一些时间。支持多达 29 个钱包。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FMAXuMg2CxO6tfPf3ai54%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1366914d-e197-41c3-9188-3720001b3320&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8651bc5b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-3.-zi-ding-yi-he-yue-di-zhi)

**3\. 自定义合约地址**

**两种模式设置自定义合约地址：**

1.  打造你的个性化代币地址，设置代币地址是否以 'pump' 结尾。
    
    *   点击勾选☑️ pump，钱包确认生成
        
    
2.  选择「导入私钥」方式；
    
    *   将你提前生成的私钥粘贴导入（**地址必须要全新地址且没有付过SOL租金**）；
        
    *   系统将使用该地址部署你的代币，确保合约地址与预期一致。
        
    

circle-exclamation

**注：**两种方式任选其一即会立即需要钱包签名并支付平台费用（0.01 SOL)。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fb6Kg1dPWoLk1X3Dnj7Lh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14cdd169-ff1f-4e5a-82e7-f64b4f609215&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8d661f6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-4.-dev-qian-bao-she-zhi)

**4\. Dev 钱包设置**

*   若 dev 钱包未填写购买金额，则免收服务费；否则需支付与其他买入钱包相同的服务费。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252F5fqZOn8DNGY8smp0QUDz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8a55826-cbc3-4bb5-8739-ee0028491331&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46075b1a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-5.-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao-she-zhi)

**5\. 捆绑买入钱包设置**

*   **捆绑买入**钱包采用阶梯定价模式，购买钱包数越多，单个钱包服务费越低。
    
*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型: **Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON）**，或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   设置买入金额：手动输入数量，统一输入金额/百分比/全部，（全部即导入钱包能购买的最大数量）。
    
*   除服务费外，每个新地址需额外支付 **0.00203928** SOL 作为账户租金。
    

circle-exclamation

Pump.fun开盘同时买入请保证买入钱包有足够的买入金额和 GAS，避免买入失败，同时买入最多设置 12 个地址。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FQtObgej64Y2stFbgwfUm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b70beba-a960-4120-a4c9-0f93c642e800&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67448eab&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

**捆绑买入**有个缺点，它有可能会被 pump 平台识别为 Bot。

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FVOX7bUX5ChOCglTEfg12%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0021a906-e957-4277-8b80-01534f386412&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=529d6546&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-6.-ti-qian-sheng-cheng-dai-bi-he-yue)

**6\. 提前生成代币合约**

*   支持提前生成代币合约地址，适用于需要在正式开盘前进行预热或对接的场景。
    

circle-info

**注：**如果自定义合约地址了，就不需要再选择提前生成代币合约。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FuZwQ6IdFqZTvdaatOh47%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db46cf92b-3064-4836-89ba-c5329676aab9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfeae441&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-7.-jito-xiao-fei-she-zhi)

**7\. Jito 小费设置**

*   配置 Jito MEV 小费，用于加速打包交易，提高排序优先级。
    
*   设置完成后点击下方 **Pump开盘并买入** 按钮。
    

triangle-exclamation

此功能实现依赖于 Jito 的捆绑功能。由于网络环境、Jito节点、RPC节点和区块处理引擎的复杂影响，该功能可能面临较高的失败率。

若操作失败，不会开盘成功也不会产生任何费用，请尝试更换RPC节点，区块处理引擎，增加Jito的小费(建议0.01SOL)，并考虑在链上活跃度较低的时段再次尝试。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FrJXkhDkSlXAaURWEHnQQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8eaa3293-f7ca-452f-bf1b-ccc7a8aa0a9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8356c262&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-8.-liu-cheng-zhan-shi)

8\. 流程展示

*   任务开始执行时，会出现日志弹框为您实时更新进度。
    
*   交易成功后，会为您提供交易链接和代币链接，点击可直接查看。
    
*   任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fc44BMj2d21XLJh3ru6TQ%252Ftelegram-cloud-photo-size-5-6161019720581189532-y.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15918fbd-7849-4daf-a1de-4f96bf0b0b58&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1c58e3ff&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-1.-pump-kai-pan-mai-ru-shi-shen-me)

**1\. Pump 开盘买入是什么？**

*   check
    
    答：指在 Pump.fun 开盘瞬间，多个地址同时抢先买入代币，争取低价筹码。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-2.-zui-duo-kun-bang-12-ge-di-zhi-bao-bu-bao-kuo-fa-bi-di-zhi)

**2\. 最多捆绑12个地址，包不包括发币地址？**

*   check
    
    答：不包括，连同发币地址，最多可支持13个地址在开盘时买入代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-3.-pump.fun-fa-bi-hou-hai-neng-xiu-gai-dai-bi-zi-liao-ma)

**3\.** Pump.fun**发币后，还能修改代币资料吗？**

*   check
    
    答：PumpFun发的币是没有任何权限的，不能增发、拉黑以及修改代币资料。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-4.-wo-fa-xing-de-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi-wei-hao-shi-pump-ma)

**4\. 我发行的代币，合约地址尾号是pump吗？**

*   check
    
    答：这个是可选项，取决于你是否勾选以 pump 结尾。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-5.-pump.fun-fa-bi-bu-xu-yao-jia-chi-zi-ma)

**5\.** Pump.fun**发币不需要加池子吗？**

*   check
    
    答：不需要，用户买入后会自动形成一个联合曲线流动性，不需要手动添加。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-6.-pump.fun-fa-bi-man-zu-shen-me-tiao-jian-cai-neng-shang-pumpswap)

**6\.** Pump.fun **发币满足什么条件才能上PumpSwap？**

*   check
    
    答：当联合曲线资金池达到85个sol时，PumpFun会直接将代币发射到**PumpSwap**上面.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-7.-pump.fun-dai-bi-kai-pan-chu-shi-jia-ge-shi-duo-shao)

**7\.** Pump.fun **代币开盘初始价格是多少?**

*   check
    
    答：Pump开盘初始价格默认是0.000000028 SOL.

# Solana Freeze Account Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Freeze Account：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/freeze-accountarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/freeze-account)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#how-to-freeze-account-on-solana)

🧊 **How to Freeze Account on Solana**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can navigate from the **Token Management** page (if you have freeze permissions and have not revoked them, the **Freeze** button will be displayed).
    
2.  Go directly to the **Freeze Account** page, select the token to operate on, enter the wallet address you want to freeze, and click the action button below.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252Fat5iZ1eENyuVJoqzbkDV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2513b46a-8bd0-4f1c-ac9d-ea8241b4eafa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4e1a410&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#freeze-account-transaction-process)

⛓️ **Freeze Account Transaction Process**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   When the task starts, a log popup will appear to update you on the transaction progress in real-time.
    
*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-1.-what-is-the-account-freezing-feature)

1\. What is the account freezing feature?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Freezing an account means temporarily restricting a wallet’s ability to **transfer or trade** specific tokens.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-2.-who-has-the-authority-to-freeze-an-account)

2\. Who has the authority to freeze an account?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Only accounts with the token's **Freeze authority** can perform freezing operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-3.-can-a-frozen-account-still-receive-tokens)

3\. Can a frozen account still receive tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, freezing only restricts **sending and trading**; receiving tokens is still allowed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-4.-how-can-i-unfreeze-a-frozen-account)

4\. How can I unfreeze a frozen account?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** An account with **Freeze authority** can initiate the unfreeze operation at any time.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-5.-does-freezing-an-account-affect-overall-token-circulation)

5\. Does freezing an account affect overall token circulation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, it only affects the **specific frozen wallet**, not the overall circulation of the token.

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)

*   **YouTube:** [https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)

# Solana Revoke Permission Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#solana-revoke-permission-https-ciaotool.io-zh-cn-token-revoke-permission)

Solana Revoke Permission：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/revoke-permissionarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/revoke-permission)



----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#how-to-renounce-token-authority-on-solana)

➕ **How to Renounce Token Authority on Solana**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can access the renouncement feature directly from the **Token Management** page. If any authority has not been renounced, a **Renounce Authority** button will be displayed.
    
2.  You can go directly to the **Renounce Authority** page, select the token, and if any permissions are still active, you can toggle the renouncement switch and click the action button below to proceed.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fc0h3VEhXgep33vrVP6Ut%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8402e73-e6f1-4011-af3f-81fbd40ad3ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86e29790&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#renouncement-transaction-process)

🔄 **Renouncement Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-1.-what-permissions-are-required-to-mint-more-tokens)

1\. What permissions are required to mint more tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You must retain the **Mint authority** to perform any token minting operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-2.-will-the-total-supply-update-immediately-after-minting)

2\. Will the total supply update immediately after minting?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, the change is reflected **instantly on-chain**, and updates will appear in your wallet and on block explorers.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-3.-will-minting-more-tokens-affect-the-token-price)

3\. Will minting more tokens affect the token price?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Minting increases the total supply, which may **impact market price and liquidity** — proceed with caution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-4.-how-can-i-mint-tokens-using-ciaotool)

4\. How can I mint tokens using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Go to the **Token Management** section in CiaoTool, select **Mint**, enter the amount, and confirm the signature.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-5.-is-token-minting-safe)

5\. Is token minting safe?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** As long as your **private key is secure** and permissions are properly managed, minting is a **safe and controlled** process.

# Solana Unfreeze Account Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Unfreeze Account：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/unfreeze-accountarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/unfreeze-account)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#how-to-unfreeze-account-on-solana)

❄️ **How to Unfreeze Account on Solana**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can navigate from the **Token Management** page (if you have unfreeze permissions and have not revoked them, the **Unfreeze** button will be displayed).
    
2.  Go directly to the **Unfreeze Account** page, select the token to operate on, enter the wallet address you want to unfreeze, and click the action button below.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FRTftXTzUbEQYGXimFTuV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0416a3f-cddd-4d3a-bac4-d41611fbac80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=827a500b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#unfreeze-account-transaction-process)

⛓️ **Unfreeze Account Transaction Process**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-1.-what-permission-is-required-to-unfreeze-an-account)

1\. What permission is required to unfreeze an account?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Only an account with **Freeze authority** can perform the unfreeze operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-2.-can-the-account-trade-immediately-after-being-unfrozen)

2\. Can the account trade immediately after being unfrozen?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, once unfrozen, the account’s **transfer and trading rights** are instantly restored.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-3.-does-unfreezing-an-account-incur-a-transaction-fee)

3\. Does unfreezing an account incur a transaction fee?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, the unfreeze action incurs a **standard on-chain transaction fee**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-4.-can-the-unfreeze-action-be-reversed)

4\. Can the unfreeze action be reversed?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, once completed, the **account permissions are immediately restored** and cannot be undone.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-5.-how-do-i-unfreeze-an-account-using-ciaotool)

5\. How do I unfreeze an account using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Go to the **Token Management** page, select the frozen account, click **Unfreeze**, and sign the transaction.

# Pump 微量刷单教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump 微量刷单：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/micro-tradingarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/micro-trading)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#ru-he-jin-xing-pump-wei-liang-shua-dan)

🧩 如何进行Pump 微量刷单？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FXyfjYF0onrS0ZXOBR65W%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad766661-4081-43f9-af1c-03a6e7e18718&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f1765346&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-2.-da-kai-pump-wei-liang-shua-dan-jie-mian)

**2\. 打开** Pump 微量刷单**界面**

*   进入对应的Pump 微量刷单操作页面。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-3.-tian-xie-cao-zuo-xin-xi)

**3\. 填写操作信息**

*   **选择刷单代币**：手动输入代币合约地址。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FuvnLYb1hdEg4dGLCZWzE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9db1b466-7133-493e-b3bb-1ae5be78039c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=407862ce&sv=2)

*   **刷单钱包设置**：
    
    *   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
        
    *   刷新导入钱包余额及Token 余额。
        
    *   操作删除资金不足的钱包。
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FXF4va3dHC4Pksd2byaur%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D676ac21f-2f7e-456a-a7c2-1ccd35a31dd6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ec736c63&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-4.-shua-dan-she-zhi)

**4\. 刷单设置**

*   **单次买卖金额设置：**Pump首页展示的订单最小交易金额为 0.01 SOL，交易额越大展示概率越高。
    
*   **任务执行间隔**：随机和指定时间两种模式（秒）
    
*   **钱包执行顺序**：顺序执行/随机执行
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FrGf96LPIOFlFXh5M0LRJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3a327bef-77de-4b9e-8214-f4b4c2e2f024&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6fa65343&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-5.-jito-xiao-fei-she-zhi)

**5\. Jito 小费设置**

*   配置 Jito MEV 小费，用于加速打包交易，提高排序优先级。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fdq2bOisY21kMysog1Lyj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D100cfefc-f064-422d-b115-1974829dcbdd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=31720c3e&sv=2)

*   点击下方 **开始刷单** 按钮即可完成购买。
    

circle-exclamation

**注：**买卖一笔为一次刷单，买和卖将分别收取服务费，服务费以刷单页下方展示为准。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#pump-wei-liang-shua-dan-jiao-yi-liu-cheng)

🔗 Pump 微量刷单交易流程

*   任务开始执行时，会出现日志弹框为您实时更新进度。交易成功后，会为您提供交易链接，点击可直接查看
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FbyZJ24N1DgkjpOIfCL5T%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ffe6c57-8638-4294-9b68-5a6758ef3046&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1a811d8c&sv=2)

*   任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FQMygCpwqLzcBDSTw53Qg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa9f7004-cee0-4670-9bd5-6480a5615ceb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4cdaf2f7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-1.-shen-me-shi-pump-wei-liang-shua-dan)

1\. 什么是 Pump 微量刷单？

*   check
    
    答： 微量刷单是指使用极小金额的买卖交易，在不显著影响代币价格的前提下，持续保持项目在 Pump 首页曝光。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-2.-wei-liang-shua-dan-you-shen-me-yong)

2\. 微量刷单有什么用？

*   check
    
    答： 刷单能提升项目的活跃度指标，增加项目在首页或热门列表中的可见性，**吸引更多真实用户点击和关注**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-3.-shua-dan-jinehui-ying-xiang-xiao-guo-ma)

3\. 刷单金额会影响效果吗？

*   check
    
    答： 一般建议使用 0.01–0.02 SOL 的小额买卖，多次频繁执行能达到较好的刷量效果，系统会读取交易频率而非金额总量。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-4.-hui-bu-hui-dao-zhi-tu-biao-yi-chang-huo-ying-xiang-shi-chang)

4\. 会不会导致图表异常或影响市场？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。CiaoTool 已做过优化，微量刷单默认开启「隐藏图表影响」模式，不会出现明显价格波动或成交尖刺。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-5.-ke-yi-pi-liang-she-zhi-duo-ge-di-zhi-jin-xing-shua-dan-ma)

5\. 可以批量设置多个地址进行刷单吗？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。支持批量导入多个钱包地址，系统将自动轮询执行小额买卖，**提升自然度与抗检测能力**。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# Solana Burn Token Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Burn Token：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/burnarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/burn)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#how-to-burn-token-on-solana)

🔥 **How to Burn Token on Solana**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can navigate from the **Token Management** page (if you have a token balance, the **Burn** button will be displayed).
    
2.  Go directly to the **Burn Token** page, select the token you want to burn, enter the burn amount, and click the action button below.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FQlH3SUug1SuIf051znwU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904b04d9-3ba2-43c9-bcac-65026a822135&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fae3ace7&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#token-burn-transaction-process)

⛓️ **Token Burn Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   When the task starts, a log popup will appear to update you on the transaction progress in real-time.
    
*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-1.-what-is-token-burning)

1\. What is token burning?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Token burning refers to **permanently destroying** a certain amount of tokens to reduce the circulating supply.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-2.-how-does-burning-tokens-impact-a-project)

2\. How does burning tokens impact a project?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Burning increases **token scarcity**, which can boost market confidence and perceived project value.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-3.-can-a-burn-operation-be-reversed)

3\. Can a burn operation be reversed?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** **No**, once burned, tokens are **permanently removed** and cannot be recovered.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-4.-how-do-i-burn-tokens-using-ciaotool)

4\. How do I burn tokens using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Use the **Token Management** feature, enter the burn amount, and **sign the transaction** to complete the process.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-5.-does-burning-tokens-incur-a-fee)

5\. Does burning tokens incur a fee?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, burning tokens incurs a **standard on-chain transaction fee**.

# Solana Token Management Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Token Management：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/managementarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/management)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#tokens-are-categorized-into-the-following-four-types)

Tokens are categorized into the following **four types**:

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#standard-tokens)

💰 **Standard Tokens：**

The most common type of SPL token, used for standard transfers and transactions.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FFx4pMZnggIpCb9OaScI2%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De23b776d-435a-42ca-9888-3bc27760b4da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcb5e20f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#pump-tokens)

🎯 **Pump Tokens：**

Tokens created via Pump. You can perform token burning operations.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252Fnl8J2OhK4BGlU5jldNrG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20a65685-dd94-453e-a706-b68370c4b556&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d11c578&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#nft-tokens)

🖼️ **NFT Tokens：**

Displays the list of NFT tokens you own.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FAm0AerJnAHnQ5keeMfjt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2c4843b-1b31-4217-a835-5da14364070d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=541ff03e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#stable-tokens)

💵 **Stable Tokens：**

Displays the balance of USDT and USDC.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FjbDReAXof54KdV8qeVI3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b70a9b7-6c78-4ec6-897e-af246eb11678&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e40a4ae9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-1.-can-i-change-the-total-supply-of-a-standard-token)

1\. Can I change the total supply of a standard token?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, if you’ve retained the **Mint authority**, you can increase or reduce the supply through minting or burning; otherwise, the supply cannot be changed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-2.-do-i-have-to-revoke-permissions-for-pump-tokens)

2\. Do I have to revoke permissions for Pump tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It's strongly recommended to **revoke permissions early** to avoid concerns about potential minting or freezing, and to build community trust.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-3.-whats-the-core-difference-between-nfts-and-regular-tokens)

3\. What’s the core difference between NFTs and regular tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** **NFTs are unique, non-fungible assets** (usually based on the Metaplex standard), while standard tokens are **fungible and divisible**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-4.-how-do-stablecoins-maintain-price-stability)

4\. How do stablecoins maintain price stability?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Stablecoins typically rely on **reserves, pegging mechanisms,** or **algorithms** to maintain a 1:1 ratio with fiat currencies like USD.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-5.-can-pump-tokens-or-nfts-be-managed-as-standard-tokens)

5\. Can Pump tokens or NFTs be managed as standard tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Not recommended. NFTs and some Pump tokens have **different structures**, and their **permission controls and trading behavior** may not follow standard token rules.

# Before Token Launch: How Should Token Liquidity Be Allocated? | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Create Token：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/create)

**Pump：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buy)

**Bonk：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buy)

circle-check

**BSC Create Token：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**Fourmeme：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buy)

**Flap：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**Base Create Token：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#why-is-liquidity-so-important)

🔑 Why Is Liquidity So Important?

*   **Trading Smoothness**: Liquidity directly affects slippage. The lower the liquidity, the greater the price impact of a single trade, resulting in a less smooth trading experience.
    
*   **Price Stability**: Higher liquidity can better absorb buy and sell pressure, improving price stability, but it also comes with higher capital lock-up costs.
    
*   **Manipulation Risk & Fit**: When liquidity is insufficient, pools become easier to manipulate. However, more liquidity is not always better—excessive liquidity can increase potential impermanent loss. The key is whether the liquidity configuration matches the project’s current stage.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#first-define-your-liquidity-tier)

📊 First, Define Your Liquidity Tier

Regardless of which blockchain you launch on, you should first identify your project’s liquidity tier. This choice directly affects investor perception and price behavior.

*   **Very Low Liquidity**: Experimental projects or low-budget memes; high slippage and extremely vulnerable to bots.
    
*   **Low Liquidity**: Early-stage projects with a small community; price stability is still limited.
    
*   **Moderate Liquidity**: Projects with a growing user base and regular trading activity; prices are more controlled.
    
*   **High Liquidity**: Mature-stage projects; market confidence improves significantly.
    
*   **Very High Liquidity**: Well-funded or proven projects; manipulation becomes difficult.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#liquidity-reference-ranges-by-blockchain)

🔗 Liquidity Reference Ranges by Blockchain

The table below summarizes commonly observed liquidity ranges based on real market conditions. These are **reference benchmarks**, not strict rules.

Liquidity Tier

SOL (Raydium)

SOL (PumpSwap)

BSC (BNB)

Base

Very Low

1 – 100 SOL

1 – 25 SOL

0.15 – 15 BNB

0.1 – 5 WETH

Low

101 – 500 SOL

26 – 125 SOL

15 – 75 BNB

6 – 25 WETH

Moderate

501 – 2,000 SOL

126 – 500 SOL

75 – 300 BNB

26 – 100 WETH

High

2,001 – 10,000 SOL

501 – 2,500 SOL

300 – 1,500 BNB

101 – 500 WETH

Very High

\>10,000 SOL

\>2,500 SOL

\>1,500 BNB

\>500 WETH

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F6YLTtIJTDr0AhxOybYP3%252F79699.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61ed9f51-35f1-4c7b-919e-c4d27a4bd4fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb25c37d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#what-problems-does-insufficient-liquidity-cause)

⚠️ What Problems Does Insufficient Liquidity Cause?

*   **Impact of Insufficient Liquidity**: When liquidity is low, slippage increases significantly, directly degrading the trading experience. At the same time, liquidity pools become more vulnerable to bot front-running and pump-and-dump attacks, raising overall market risk.
    
*   **The Need for Active Liquidity Management**: While increasing liquidity can help mitigate these issues to some extent, impermanent loss must still be considered—especially during periods of high price volatility. Therefore, liquidity should be managed dynamically rather than deployed as a one-time allocation.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#should-you-allocate-100-of-tokens-to-the-liquidity-pool)

🔎 Should You Allocate 100% of Tokens to the Liquidity Pool?

*   Generally, no. A healthier approach is to allocate **40%–70%** of the total token supply to liquidity, while reserving the remainder for **staking incentives, ecosystem rewards, community growth, or future airdrops**.
    
*   This structure ensures sufficient market depth while preserving long-term flexibility for the project.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FWh9C92NlDq23PXzBgdxE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70abd2d1-f248-489a-9c89-32f4a5fb279f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed83faef&sv=2)

*   Liquidity is core infrastructure for any token. Although specific ranges vary across blockchains, the underlying principle remains the same:
    

> **Adequate liquidity = more stable prices + stronger market confidence + lower manipulation risk**

Carefully planning your liquidity tier and token allocation is one of the most important steps to avoid failing at the very beginning.

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Jito 捆绑包教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/jito#shen-me-shi-jito-kun-bang-bao)

**什么是 Jito 捆绑包？**

Jito Bundle 代表了 Solana 生态系统中的一项突破性功能，为交易者提供了一种无缝执行多个交易的简化方法。这些捆绑包是精心设计的交易列表，可确保顺序和原子执行，从而提高交易操作的效率和可靠性。

通俗来讲，就是如果 交易 A + 交易 B 两笔交易构成一个 jito 捆绑包，那么交易 A 和 交易 B会在链上一起执行。如果 A 和 B 两笔交易有任何一笔交易失败，那么两笔交易都不会上链成功。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/jito#ta-ru-he-zhi-chi-ciaotool)

**它如何支持 CiaoTool？**

Jito Bundle 为 CiaoTool 用户提供宝贵的支持，提供一系列功能来优化交易策略：

1.  **给验证器小费**：借助 Jito Bundle，交易者可以通过给验证器小费来确定交易的优先级，确保及时执行并最大化交易机会。
    
2.  **交易优化**：通过批量 DeFi 操作并利用原子套利机会，交易者可以准确轻松地利用市场低效率。
    

将 Jito Bundle 纳入 CiaoTool 的工具包，使交易者能够自信、高效、敏捷地驾驭加密货币市场，确保在不断发展的数字资产交易环境中保持竞争优势。

**了解有关 Jito Bundle 的更多信息：**[https://jito-labs.gitbook.io/mev/searcher-resources/bundlesarrow-up-right](https://jito-labs.gitbook.io/mev/searcher-resources/bundles)

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)

# Solana 租金回收教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

Solana 租金回收：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/reclaim-rentarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#shi-yong-bu-zhou)

📝 使用步骤

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-1.-xuan-ze-cao-zuo-qian-bao-dang-qian-huo-dao-ru)

1\. 选择操作钱包（当前或导入）。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-2.-sao-miao-qian-bao-nei-suo-you-spl-token-nft-zhang-hu)

2\. 扫描钱包内所有 SPL Token / NFT 账户。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-3.-gou-xuan-xu-hui-shou-de-zhang-hu-lei-xing)

3\. 勾选需回收的账户类型：

*   空账户
    
*   有余额但可烧毁的代币账户
    
*   NFT（支持批量）
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-4.-dian-ji-yi-jian-hui-shou-bing-qian-ming-que-ren-jiao-yi)

4\. 点击【一键回收】并签名确认交易。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-5.-cheng-gong-hou-ke-cha-kan-shi-fang-de-sol-shu-liang)

5\. 成功后，可查看释放的 SOL 数量

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FCjXrEM2E6ne6jScheVV4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91ea94be-c03f-45fc-9bfa-a051c1a143af&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86a6489b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-1.-shen-me-shi-zu-jin-hui-shou-wei-shen-me-yao-cao-zuo)

1\. 什么是租金回收？为什么要操作？

*   check
    
    答： 租金回收是关闭不再使用的账户，释放已支付的 SOL 租金，**可降低账户维护成本并提升钱包整洁度**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/rent-recovery#id-2.-shao-hui-dai-bi-huo-nft-hui-yong-jiu-shi-xiao-ma)

2\. 烧毁代币或 NFT 会永久失效吗？

*   check
    
    答： 是的。执行烧毁操作会**永久销毁资产并关闭账户**，请确保目标代币或 NFT 无后续用途再进行操作。

# Solana Mint Token Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#solana-mint-token-https-ciaotool.io-en-us-token-mint)

Solana Mint Token：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/mintarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/mint)



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#how-to-mint-token-on-solana)

🔓 **How to Mint Token on Solana**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can access the minting feature directly from the **Token Management** page. If you have the necessary minting permissions and have not renounced them, a **Mint** button will be displayed.
    
2.  You can go directly to the **Token Minting** page, select a token or enter the token address to search. If the **Mint Authority** is still active, you can proceed with minting. Simply enter the desired amount and click the **Mint** button.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FDWx0u0qq0ggslaHt0lLR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2539c5f7-b2c0-4ffd-8e9a-00577824d410&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d7170cce&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#minting-transaction-process)

🔁 **Minting Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-1.-can-token-permissions-be-restored-after-revocation)

1\. Can token permissions be restored after revocation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. Once permissions are revoked, the action is **permanent and cannot be undone**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-2.-why-should-i-revoke-token-permissions)

2\. Why should I revoke token permissions?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Revoking permissions **increases project transparency**, strengthens community trust, and attracts more investors.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-3.-is-the-revocation-process-complicated)

3\. Is the revocation process complicated?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Not at all. With **CiaoTool**, it’s a **one-click operation** — no coding required.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-4.-which-permissions-are-most-important-to-revoke)

4\. Which permissions are most important to revoke?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Typically, the **Mint** (minting) and **Freeze** (account freezing) permissions are key to ensuring supply integrity and operational safety.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-5.-will-revoking-permissions-affect-token-trading)

5\. Will revoking permissions affect token trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. **Regular transfers and trading** of the token will remain unaffected.

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
