# Wallet Security Guidelines | CiaoTool

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#web3-wallet-private-keys-are-crucial)

🔐 **Web3 Wallet Private Keys Are Crucial**

Once a private key falls into the wrong hands, your assets can be completely drained. However, executing batch operations often requires using the private key, as it is impossible to sign multiple wallets simultaneously without it.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#to-address-such-needs-there-are-two-widely-used-types-of-tool-in-the-market)

To address such needs, there are two widely used types of tool in the market:

1.  **Telegram Bots (TG BOT):** TG BOTs inherently require access to private keys to sign transactions, making them a common choice for batch operations.
    
2.  Another approach involves using certain web-based tools that execute transactions on the backend after obtaining the user’s private key, but this method carries extremely high risk.
    
    *   **Trust:** The platform must be highly trustworthy.
        
    *   **Security:** The platform must have robust measures to protect private keys (e.g., the dexx server hack is a typical risk example).
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#how-does-ciaotool-keep-your-private-keys-safe)

✅ **How Does CiaoTool Keep Your Private Keys Safe?**

CiaoTool uses a **client-side signing mechanism**, meaning your private key is **never uploaded or stored on any server**. All transactions are signed locally within your browser, ensuring that the platform is **technically incapable of accessing or stealing your private key**. For users who perform frequent operations, we also offer an **optional local encrypted storage** feature — balancing convenience with maximum security.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#how-to-ensure-private-keys-are-only-used-for-local-signing)

🛡️ **How to Ensure Private Keys Are Only Used for Local Signing**

Any frontend tool that wants to access a private key must make an HTTPS request to send the key to a backend server. To verify this, you can inspect the tool's network activity:

1.  Open **Chrome Browser**.
    
2.  Right-click and select **Inspect**.
    
3.  Navigate to **Network** -> **Fetch/XHR**.
    
4.  Check if any requests send your private key to the backend (excluding third-party RPC interfaces like Helius for on-chain data).
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252Fo4l39JAI7EGjKGuAlap0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe938640-f827-4d93-bdcd-ea9e50926773&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67473b61&sv=2)

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FAxjjRJUeSmBNcusHJeBX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d9694dd-48d9-436f-bfef-63752dba0b1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=125cb9c6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#how-to-operate-private-keys-safely-and-conveniently)

🔐 **How to Operate Private Keys Safely and Conveniently**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#ciaotool-offers-three-methods-for-managing-private-keys)

CiaoTool offers **three methods** for managing private keys:

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252F2oA9a8EoIJ2nWxSSqDAp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8165f14-1692-4832-8650-3561f5aaa132&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf95d4be&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-1.-manual-input)

**1\. Manual Input**

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FuGb1vOoQwpMQlOfNFwRq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f6f4fb8-d67a-4ebd-be10-a8a3aeb79ee1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6315174&sv=2)

This method requires you to manage your private keys yourself and paste them into an input field. CiaoTool will use your private key for local signing.

**⚠️ Security Precautions** :

*   Prevent malicious clipboard plugins on your computer from stealing your private key.
    
*   Ensure your private key isn’t stored in plain text on your device. Secure your device to prevent theft.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-2.-import-private-key-file)

**2\. Import Private Key File**

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FkCjGk5RGWKgnxLSIl2um%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71edfaad-5c27-4bc2-ac76-8b340b2b9c6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1898dc6&sv=2)

CiaoTool supports importing private keys in **Excel**, **CSV**, **JSON**, or **TXT** formats. Compared to manual input, this method improves efficiency.

*   **Instructions**:
    
    *   **For existing wallets:** download the \[template file\] from the top left, paste your private keys into it, and import.
        
    *   **For new wallets:** use the **Multi Sender** feature to create new wallets, perform batch transfers, and export them in one go. Then, import the exported file.
        
    
*   **⚠️ Security Precautions** :
    
    *   Prevent malicious clipboard plugins from stealing your private key.
        
    *   Ensure your private key isn’t stored in plain text on your device. Secure your device to prevent theft.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-3.-local-encrypted-storage-recommended)

**3\. Local Encrypted Storage (Recommended 👍)**

CiaoTool offers a **local encrypted storage** feature that uses AES encryption. Your private key is encrypted with a password you set (known only to you) and stored locally.

*   **Storage Location**: Chrome Browser -> Right-click -> Inspect -> Application.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FYTrC8jXxUIDjBChDBs8Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D213269a2-b35b-425b-822c-b15be6895d1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26bfa93d&sv=2)

*   **Advantages**:
    
    *   Compared to manual input or file upload, private keys are not stored in plain text on your device.
        
    *   It allows for easy wallet balance viewing and streamlined batch operations.
        
    
*   **Important Note**:
    
    *   Remember your encryption password. If lost, CiaoTool cannot recover your data. You’ll need to delete local data and start over.
        
    

**Instructions**:

*   **For existing wallets:** After enabling wallet management, click **\[Import Bulk Wallets\]** in the top left and import your private keys. You can then select them directly for batch operations.
    
*   **For new wallets:** After creating new wallets, import them into local wallet management with one click.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FwtVNr9ny6e3FQwdlS4D0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a669b22-e2fd-4587-be15-cf8e924fc987&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=713892d&sv=2)

**⚠️Security Precautions** :

*   Be cautious of malicious clipboard plugins when importing private keys into local management.
    
*   Ensure the security of your local device and encryption password.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions（FAQ）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-1.-how-can-i-keep-my-seed-phrase-secure)

1\. How can I keep my seed phrase secure?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Write it down with pen and paper and store it offline. Never save it as a screenshot, in cloud notes, or chat history.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-2.-why-shouldnt-i-save-my-wallet-using-screenshots)

2\. Why shouldn't I save my wallet using screenshots?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Screenshots can be accessed by malware or synced to the cloud, posing serious security risks.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-3.-will-clearing-my-browser-cache-affect-my-wallet)

3\. Will clearing my browser cache affect my wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. Non-custodial wallet private keys are not stored in browser cache, but make sure you have backed up your seed phrase beforehand.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-4.-what-are-the-risks-of-using-browser-extension-wallets)

4\. What are the risks of using browser extension wallets?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Extension wallets can be exploited by fake websites or malicious approvals — always double-check every interaction and signature.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-5.-how-do-i-know-if-an-airdrop-or-link-is-safe)

5\. How do I know if an airdrop or link is safe?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Avoid clicking on unknown links or approving suspicious transactions — especially those claiming “free airdrops.”
    

###

# 批量创建钱包教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**批量创建钱包：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/my-wallets/create-walletsarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/my-wallets/create-wallets)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程，手把手演示如何一鍵生成上百錢包!

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 **操作步骤**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#id-1.-shu-ru-chuang-jian-shu-liang-dian-ji-chuang-jian-ji-ke-sheng-cheng-pi-liang-qian-bao)

1\. 输入创建数量，点击创建即可生成批量钱包。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#id-2.-sheng-cheng-wan-nin-hai-ke-yi-xuan-ze-dao-ru-dao-pi-liang-qian-bao-guan-li-zhe-jiang-da-da-ti-gao)

2\. 生成完您还可以选择导入到批量钱包管理，这将大大提高您批量操作私钥的效率

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fy2t1zgCvnxRszVfZlLb8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a0abee9-7015-48c8-b814-a1fb3d2ea3d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1ce4b9b4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#id-1.-yi-ci-zui-duo-ke-yi-chuang-jian-duo-shao-ge-qian-bao-di-zhi)

1\. 一次最多可以创建多少个钱包地址？

*   check
    
    答： CiaoTool 支持一键生成最多 **500 个钱包地址**，可根据需求自定义数量。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#id-2.-chuang-jian-de-qian-bao-shi-fou-dai-you-si-yao-ru-he-dao-chu)

2\. 创建的钱包是否带有私钥？如何导出？

*   check
    
    答： 是的。每个钱包都会自动生成对应私钥，可在操作完成后导出为 **CSV 文件或 JSON 文件**，用于备份或后续操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/create-wallets#id-3.-zhe-xie-qian-bao-an-quan-ma-shi-fou-hui-shang-chuan-si-yao)

3\. 这些钱包安全吗？是否会上传私钥？

*   check
    
    答： 安全。**所有钱包生成与私钥处理均在本地浏览器执行**，平台不会上传、保存或访问用户的任何私钥信息。

# Bonk 创建并买入教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Bonk 创建并买入**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/launch-and-buy)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#ru-he-jin-xing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

🧩 如何进行Bonk 创建并买入？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-tui-jian-shi-yong-phantom-huan-ying-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包 (推荐使用 Phantom-幻影钱包）**

*   打开 Bonk 创建并买入操作界面 ，
    
*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FFtHO32vs7DNP1xGfBKkt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90fdcd89-489a-4754-b9d2-0af37b9b6470&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5380a245&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-2.-tian-xie-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

**2\. 填写代币基础信息**

*   您可以手动填写代币信息，或者点击 **【克隆】** 按钮，克隆其他代币的信息
    
*   社媒信息为可选项，不是必填项。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FDpHq0F25piEzieXKskDH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddeb0c424-cf89-402d-bfa9-ddd624d6080a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4a41fb44&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-3.-zi-ding-yi-he-yue-di-zhi)

**3\. 自定义合约地址**

*   打造你的个性化代币地址，
    
*   将你提前生成的私钥粘贴导入（请务必保密保存）；
    
*   系统将使用该地址部署你的代币，确保合约地址与预期一致。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FXTU3zfhl5SWiAdgQAxpr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82417176-1b93-46e7-9b16-2165c0942ecc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c41305c8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-4.-dev-qian-bao-she-zhi)

**4\. Dev 钱包设置**

*   若 dev 钱包未填写购买金额，则免收服务费；否则需支付与其他买入钱包相同的服务费。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252F5fqZOn8DNGY8smp0QUDz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8a55826-cbc3-4bb5-8739-ee0028491331&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46075b1a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-5.-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao-she-zhi-zui-duo-8-ge-qian-bao)

**5\. 捆绑买入钱包设置（最多8个钱包）**

*   **捆绑买入**钱包采用阶梯定价模式，购买钱包数越多，单个钱包服务费越低。
    
*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型: **Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON）**，或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   设置买入金额：手动输入数量，统一输入金额/百分比/全部，（全部即导入钱包能购买的最大数量）。
    
*   除服务费外，每个新地址需额外支付 **0.00203928** SOL 作为账户租金。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FNrKeDYuU9O8MsTSfwcNc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7809d2f-9c7e-4a45-bfdc-b5c2a293bc89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df07a5d8&sv=2)

*   **捆绑买入**有个缺点，它有可能会被 pump 平台识别为 Bot。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FVOX7bUX5ChOCglTEfg12%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0021a906-e957-4277-8b80-01534f386412&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=529d6546&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-6.-ti-qian-sheng-cheng-dai-bi-he-yue)

**6\. 提前生成代币合约**

*   支持提前生成代币合约地址，适用于需要在正式开盘前进行预热或对接的场景。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FuZwQ6IdFqZTvdaatOh47%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db46cf92b-3064-4836-89ba-c5329676aab9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfeae441&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-7.-jito-xiao-fei-she-zhi)

**7\. Jito 小费设置**

*   配置 Jito MEV 小费，用于加速打包交易，提高排序优先级。
    
*   设置完成后点击下方 **Bonk开盘并买入** 按钮。
    

circle-info

此功能实现依赖于 Jito 的捆绑功能。由于网络环境、Jito节点、RPC节点和区块处理引擎的复杂影响，该功能可能面临较高的失败率。

若操作失败，不会开盘成功也不会产生任何费用，请尝试更换RPC节点，区块处理引擎，增加Jito的小费(建议0.01SOL)，并考虑在链上活跃度较低的时段再次尝试。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FrJXkhDkSlXAaURWEHnQQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8eaa3293-f7ca-452f-bf1b-ccc7a8aa0a9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8356c262&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-8.-liu-cheng-zhan-shi)

**8\. 流程展示**

*   任务开始执行时，会出现日志弹框为您实时更新进度。
    
*   交易成功后，会为您提供交易链接和代币链接，点击可直接查看。
    
*   任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-1.-shen-me-shi-bonk-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru-gong-neng)

**1\.** 什么是 Bonk 创建并买入功能？

*   check
    
    答：这是一个一键工具，可在 Lets Bonk 上快速创建并自动买入新代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-2.-shi-fou-xu-yao-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**2\.** 是否需要连接钱包？

*   check
    
    答：是的，您需要连接 Solana 钱包并准备好足够 SOL 支付费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-3.-chuang-jian-dai-bi-hou-ke-yi-xiu-gai-xin-xi-ma)

**3\.** 创建代币后可以修改信息吗？

*   check
    
    答：一旦代币创建完成，名称、符号和供应量等基本参数将无法修改。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-4.-gou-mai-dai-bi-hou-zai-na-li-cha-kan)

**4\.** 购买代币后在哪里查看？

*   check
    
    答：创建成功后，代币会自动转入您的钱包，可在钱包或 Solana 区块浏览器中查看。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/create#id-5.-wo-xu-yao-dong-dai-ma-cai-neng-shi-yong-ma)

**5\.** 我需要懂代码才能使用吗？

*   check
    
    答：不需要，整个流程为无代码操作，适合所有用户快速启动代币项目。

# 批量转账(多对多)教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**批量转账（ 多对多）**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/multi-to-multiarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/multi-to-multi)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#ru-he-jin-xing-duo-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang)

🧩 **如何进行多**对多转账？

triangle-exclamation

转出钱包数量需要和目标钱包数量一致！

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FQTahwSsW0pTtmEPYxTYs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc1b154a-9dba-48dc-886b-6b77e17c102b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30363db0&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-2.-da-kai-yi-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang-cao-zuo-ye)

**2\. 打开一对多转账操作页**

*   导入私钥，系统自动刷新SOL余额与Token余额，请保证钱包中有充足的 SOL。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-3.-xuan-ze-fa-song-dai-bi)

**3\. 选择发送代币**

*   既可以选择 SOL，又可以选择当前钱包 Token.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fer2ljGeKRhRL3wtzFc5I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61ce2021-4fc2-4cd5-822c-c45dcefdf06c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89c1751a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-4.-dao-ru-zhuan-zhang-qian-bao)

4\. 导入转账钱包

**导入钱包设置**：

*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   刷新导入钱包余额
    
*   设置转账数量，支持统一金额或随机范围。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FEm5BJjAkiC1ruYTTMHMJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9c0f26d2-bb0b-40f6-a933-76e149715d39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34806013&sv=2)

*   批量操作删除资金不足的钱包
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FHTwWSIqoua8tJ0tkpAUe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0dcaeca4-68aa-49c8-8c56-5db8e7d26c9e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f437aeaf&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-5.-dao-ru-jie-shou-di-zhi)

5\. 导入接收地址

**导入钱包设置**：

*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   刷新导入钱包余额，查看地址接收数量。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-6.-que-ren-xin-xi)

6\. 确认信息

*   检查无误后，点击下方 **确认转账** 按钮即可完成操作。
    

circle-exclamation

注：所有转账的手续费均由当前转账的钱包支付。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-dui-duo-pi-liang-zhuan-zhang)

1\. 什么是多对多批量转账？

*   check
    
    答： 多对多批量转账是指从多个来源地址向多个目标地址转账，**适合大规模资金分发**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-2.-zhuan-zhang-di-zhi-he-jie-shou-di-zhi-zen-me-dao-ru)

2\. 转账地址和接收地址怎么导入？

*   check
    
    答： 支持通过文件上传或手动粘贴导入，支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-3.-shi-fou-ke-yi-she-zhi-mei-yi-dui-de-zhuan-zhang-jine)

3\. 是否可以设置每一对的转账金额？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可以为每对地址配置不同的转账金额，或设定统一金额让系统批量执行。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-4.-cao-zuo-shi-fou-an-quan-hui-bao-cun-wo-de-si-yao-ma)

4\. 操作是否安全？会保存我的私钥吗？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。所有私钥只用于本地签名交易，**不会上传或保存至任何服务器**，保障用户资产安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-5.-duo-dui-duo-shi-yong-yu-na-xie-chang-jing)

5\. 多对多适用于哪些场景？

*   check
    
    答： 适用于项目方或机构在多个地址中发放薪资、空投、分红、批量返还等复杂资产分发场景。

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)

# Pump 捆绑买入并狙击教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#kun-bang-mai-ru-bing-ju-ji-httpsciaotool.iozhcnpumpsnipebundledbuysnipe)

捆绑买入并狙击： [https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/snipe/bundled-buy-snipearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/snipe/bundled-buy-snipe)



-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   捆绑支持单地址，但单地址操作建议直接使用市值管理即可。
    
*   捆绑买或卖时地址之间不要留空行，否则会触发报错。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#ru-he-jin-xing-pump-kun-bang-mai-ru-bing-ju-ji)

🧩 如何进行 Pump 捆绑买入并狙击？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-tui-jian-shi-yong-phantom-huan-ying-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包 (推荐使用 Phantom-幻影钱包）**

*   打开 Pump 捆绑买入并狙击 操作界面 ，
    
*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F86XqXzw7moOCoDNvZYrW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c98b774-d882-48e5-abaa-48ed649fc415&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f7cc166&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-xuan-ze-mu-biao-dai-bi)

**2\. 选择目标代币**

*   输入或粘贴 Pump.fun 上待开盘项目的代币地址。
    
*   系统将自动获取该代币的曲线信息（建议准备充足的 SOL 余额以满足预估买入需求）。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FXMfLfnVLggFv6jmcqSRO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da66c3059-160f-4026-a171-2435a31c8ee4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a0ac64e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao-she-zhi-zui-duo-12-ge)

**3\. 捆绑买入钱包设置（最多 12个）**

你有三种方式导入捆绑钱包地址：

*   **手动输入**：逐一粘贴钱包私钥。
    
*   **上传文件**：支持 CSV/JSON 格式批量导入私钥。
    
*   **自动生成**：使用 CiaoTool 一键生成钱包地址（推荐提前保存私钥备份）。
    

> 💡提示：钱包越多，抢跑成功率越高；但请注意 SOL 余额分配要充足。

*   除服务费外，每个新地址需额外支付 **0.00203928** SOL 作为账户租金。
    

circle-info

请保证买入钱包有足够的买入金额和 GAS，避免买入失败，同时买入最多设置 12 个地址。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fd2iJIzJTmrGwxAGq2pu0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25e45299-af71-4a58-ae09-9bd1c8992037&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d3bca85&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-she-zhi-swap-mai-ru-qian-bao)

**4\. 设置 Swap 买入钱包**

*   导入单个私钥
    
*   输入该钱包预计使用的 SOL 数量（**\* 具体买入的数量与需要买入的比例关联**）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FEORaMwam8ArWfYbqFgNy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D853f9e97-4ce0-4f3d-82ee-627497d0f608&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cad37e0b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-jito-xiao-fei-she-zhi-ke-xuan)

**5\.** Jito 小费**设置（可选）**

*   配置 Jito MEV 小费，用于加速打包交易，提高排序优先级。
    
*   设置完成后选择下方的 **捆绑买入并狙击** 按钮
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FZ4oX1Nb2zTnFWvqFIV4V%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9823dee8-fa9a-437d-b660-a71ef829d67e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5132dc2d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题（FAQ）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-shen-me-shi-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao-zu)

1\. 什么是捆绑买入钱包组？

*   check
    
    **答：**指在 Pump.fun 项目开盘时，最多可设置 12 个钱包同步执行买入操作，这些钱包将通过同一笔打包交易完成买入，提高效率并降低被抢跑风险。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-swap-mai-ru-qian-bao-de-zuo-yong-shi-shen-me)

2\. Swap 买入钱包的作用是什么？

*   check
    
    **答：**Swap 买入钱包是用于开盘后进行市场买入操作的钱包，适用于后续控盘、补仓、做市等用途，通常作为主力地址使用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-jito-xiao-fei-bi-xu-yao-she-zhi-ma)

3\. Jito 小费必须要设置吗？

*   check
    
    **答：**不是必须，但强烈推荐开启。Jito 技术可将交易送入优先排序池，极大提升抢跑成功率，避免被夹单或抢跑失败。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-si-yao-shi-fou-hui-bei-ciaotool-shang-chuan-huo-bao-cun)

4\. 私钥是否会被 CiaoTool 上传或保存？

*   check
    
    **答：**不会。所有私钥仅用于本地浏览器签名，CiaoTool 不会上传、保存或接触任何私钥数据，确保资产安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-ru-guo-kun-bang-mai-ru-shi-bai-le-zen-me-ban)

5\. 如果捆绑买入失败了怎么办？

*   check
    
    **答：**如果失败，资金仍保留在原钱包中。你可以重新尝试操作，并适当调整滑点或提高 Jito 小费，提升成功率。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Bonk-USD1 创建并买入教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Bonk USD1 创建并买入**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/USD1/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/USD1/launch-and-buy)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#ru-he-jin-xing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

🧩 如何进行 Bonk USD1 创建并买入？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-tui-jian-shi-yong-phantom-huan-ying-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包 (推荐使用 Phantom-幻影钱包）**

*   打开 Bonk USD1 创建并买入操作界面 ，
    
*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FFtHO32vs7DNP1xGfBKkt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90fdcd89-489a-4754-b9d2-0af37b9b6470&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5380a245&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-2.-tian-xie-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

**2\. 填写代币基础信息**

*   您可以手动填写代币信息，或者点击 **【克隆】** 按钮，克隆其他代币的信息
    
*   社媒信息为可选项，不是必填项。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FNtyo70grPmihx4syK51d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D66165dc4-acb0-42de-be68-8c8689440d57&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=697f7482&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-3.-zi-ding-yi-he-yue-di-zhi)

**3\. 自定义合约地址**

*   打造你的个性化代币地址，
    
*   将你提前生成的私钥粘贴导入（请务必保密保存）；
    
*   系统将使用该地址部署你的代币，确保合约地址与预期一致。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FXTU3zfhl5SWiAdgQAxpr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82417176-1b93-46e7-9b16-2165c0942ecc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c41305c8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-4.-dev-qian-bao-she-zhi)

**4\. Dev 钱包设置**

*   若 dev 钱包未填写购买金额，则免收服务费；否则需支付与其他买入钱包相同的服务费。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252F5fqZOn8DNGY8smp0QUDz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8a55826-cbc3-4bb5-8739-ee0028491331&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46075b1a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-5.-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao-she-zhi-zui-duo-8-ge-qian-bao)

**5\. 捆绑买入钱包设置（最多8个钱包）**

*   **捆绑买入**钱包采用阶梯定价模式，购买钱包数越多，单个钱包服务费越低。
    
*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型: **Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON）**，或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   设置买入金额：手动输入数量，统一输入金额/百分比/全部，（全部即导入钱包能购买的最大数量）。
    
*   除服务费外，每个新地址需额外支付 **0.00203928** SOL 作为账户租金。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FNrKeDYuU9O8MsTSfwcNc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7809d2f-9c7e-4a45-bfdc-b5c2a293bc89&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=df07a5d8&sv=2)

*   **捆绑买入**有个缺点，它有可能会被 pump 平台识别为 Bot。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FVOX7bUX5ChOCglTEfg12%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0021a906-e957-4277-8b80-01534f386412&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=529d6546&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-6.-ti-qian-sheng-cheng-dai-bi-he-yue)

**6\. 提前生成代币合约**

*   支持提前生成代币合约地址，适用于需要在正式开盘前进行预热或对接的场景。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FuZwQ6IdFqZTvdaatOh47%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db46cf92b-3064-4836-89ba-c5329676aab9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfeae441&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-7.-jito-xiao-fei-she-zhi)

**7\. Jito 小费设置**

*   配置 Jito MEV 小费，用于加速打包交易，提高排序优先级。
    
*   设置完成后点击下方 **Bonk USD1 创建并买入** 按钮。
    

circle-info

此功能实现依赖于 Jito 的捆绑功能。由于网络环境、Jito节点、RPC节点和区块处理引擎的复杂影响，该功能可能面临较高的失败率。

若操作失败，不会开盘成功也不会产生任何费用，请尝试更换RPC节点，区块处理引擎，增加Jito的小费(建议0.01SOL)，并考虑在链上活跃度较低的时段再次尝试。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FrJXkhDkSlXAaURWEHnQQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8eaa3293-f7ca-452f-bf1b-ccc7a8aa0a9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8356c262&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-8.-liu-cheng-zhan-shi)

**8\. 流程展示**

*   任务开始执行时，会出现日志弹框为您实时更新进度。
    
*   交易成功后，会为您提供交易链接和代币链接，点击可直接查看。
    
*   任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-1.-shen-me-shi-bonkusd1-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru-gong-neng)

**1\.** 什么是 Bonk-USD1 创建并买入功能？

*   check
    
    答：这是一个一键工具，可在 Lets Bonk-USD1 上快速创建并自动买入新代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-2.-shi-fou-xu-yao-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**2\.** 是否需要连接钱包？

*   check
    
    答：是的，您需要连接 Solana 钱包并准备好足够 SOL 支付费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-3.-chuang-jian-dai-bi-hou-ke-yi-xiu-gai-xin-xi-ma)

**3\.** 创建代币后可以修改信息吗？

*   check
    
    答：一旦代币创建完成，名称、符号和供应量等基本参数将无法修改。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-4.-gou-mai-dai-bi-hou-zai-na-li-cha-kan)

**4\.** 购买代币后在哪里查看？

*   check
    
    答：创建成功后，代币会自动转入您的钱包，可在钱包或 Solana 区块浏览器中查看。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/usd1-create#id-5.-wo-xu-yao-dong-dai-ma-cai-neng-shi-yong-ma)

**5\.** 我需要懂代码才能使用吗？

*   check
    
    答：不需要，整个流程为无代码操作，适合所有用户快速启动代币项目。

# 准备 SOL 与 Solana 租金说明 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/sol-rent#shen-me-shi-sol)

🪙 什么是 SOL？

*   SOL 是 Solana 区块链的原生代币，用于支付交易费用，同时也可用于其他功能，例如通过质押参与网络安全维护。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/sol-rent#solana-jiao-yi-fei-yong)

💸 **Solana 交易费用**

*   在 Solana 上进行任何链上操作都需要用 SOL 支付手续费。也就是说，每次在 CiaoTool 发起交易时，你的钱包里都必须有足够的 SOL 来覆盖费用。
    

circle-check

**小贴士：**0.000000001 SOL = 1 lamport（SOL 的十亿分之一）

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/sol-rent#solana-zu-jin)

💰 **Solana 租金**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/sol-rent#solana-qu-kuai-lian-zhi-suo-yi-neng-gao-xiao-cun-chu-shu-ju-qi-zhong-yi-ge-guan-jian-yuan-yin-shi-qi)

🏗️ Solana 区块链之所以能高效存储数据，其中一个关键原因是其独特的**“租金”**机制。

*   在 Solana 上，每个用户的钱包地址、代币转移记录以及其他程序化交易都会占用区块链存储资源。为了 使用这些资源，系统会收取一定的租金。
    

📝 **SOL 是 Solana 的原生代币，用于支付创建和维护每个账户所需的租金。租金的多少取决于该账户占用的存储资源量。**

*   例如，当你第一次在钱包中收到新代币时，系统会自动为该代币创建关联账户（ATA），并收取相应的 SOL 租金。
    
*   大多数情况下，这部分租金是可退的。如果账户被关闭，所占用的存储资源会被释放，租金会退回到账户所有者的地址。
    
*   你可以通过 **CiaoTool** 的 [**「钱包管理 → 租金回收」**arrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent)
    页面，一键退还代币账户的租金。
    

triangle-exclamation

CiaoTool 致力于提供便捷的工具服务，但不构成任何投资建议。平台内容可能根据产品迭代进行调整，敬请用户自行判断并留意更新。

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

[上一页Web3 钱包与安全指南chevron-left](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet)
[下一页Solana 地址与优先费用指南chevron-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/address-and-fee)

# Solana Token Creation Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#solana-create-token-https-ciaotool.io-en-us-token-create)

Solana Create Token：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/create)



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#how-to-create-a-token-on-solana)

🪙 **How to Create a Token on Solana**

1.  **Open the Solana One-Click Token Creation** interface: [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/create)
    
2.  **Fill in Basic Information：**The token **decimals** define how small the token can be divided. The maximum precision for SPL tokens is **9**, with common settings being **6** (for utility tokens) and **9** (for high-precision applications).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FKTbHfxZDpph3EuDolsU8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4e1a1e1-5db6-4dce-bd65-9eca5b231249&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c46b5ea&sv=2)

1.  **(Optional) Add Contact Information**
    

If you want users to join your community or learn more about your project, this is the most direct way to provide that information.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FDtDEcGy4wucGTAbUjw6O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D886032f3-044c-4771-9e01-e0e3438306ca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61433598&sv=2)

1.  **Custom Contract Address:** Create a personalized token address and stand out from the start — **all for just 0.01 SOL.**
    

*   In the tool, select the “Import Private Key” option;
    
*   Paste your pre-generated private key (make sure to store it securely);
    
*   The system will deploy your token from this address, ensuring the contract address matches your expectations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F3JY3dfcRL4kNwKUn1Rxd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d9e7e32-3a8b-43d2-b838-81e2ab39d122&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12767dd2&sv=2)

1.  **(Optional) Set Permissions**
    

*   Generally, for tokens that need to be added to **Raydium**, it is recommended to **revoke the freeze and mint permissions**.
    
*   The metadata update permission can be chosen at your discretion.
    
*   If the metadata update permission is revoked, the **token name and logo** can no longer be updated.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F4yeE69wMipnjFeiWFiRb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e075cac-f841-491f-b9dc-36e2814f2324&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ceec98b8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#token-creation-transaction-process)

🔁 **Token Creation Transaction Process**

*   When the process starts, a **log popup** will appear to update you on the progress in real time.
    
*   Once the transaction is successful, you will receive **transaction and token links**, which you can click to view directly.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FbX1Xk530gARy7TfZsV0w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35fa2967-8bc0-46c9-a17c-911effa622d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fad18960&sv=2)

*   If anything goes wrong during the process, we will provide **clear feedback** on the issue, **No fees** will be charged for failed transactions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions（FAQ）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-1.-what-wallet-do-i-need-to-create-a-token)

1\. What wallet do I need to create a token?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** We recommend using Solana-compatible browser extension wallets such as **Phantom** or **Backpack**, and ensuring the wallet is properly connected.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-2.-how-much-sol-is-required-for-one-click-token-creation)

2\. How much SOL is required for one-click token creation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Typically around **0.1–0.3 SOL** is needed to create the token account and complete the initialization transaction (may vary slightly based on network congestion).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-3.-why-is-nothing-happening-after-i-click-create)

3\. Why is nothing happening after I click "Create"?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Please check if your wallet is prompting for a signature. If not, try refreshing the page and reconnecting your wallet.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-4.-where-can-i-view-my-token-after-its-created)

4\. Where can I view my token after it's created?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You can view the token details on a Solana block explorer such as **Solscan** by entering the token address, or import the token into your wallet to display it.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-5.-can-i-change-the-token-name-or-symbol-after-creation)

5\. Can I change the token name or symbol after creation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, **SPL tokens** allow you to modify the name and symbol even after the token has been created.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Batch Create Wallets Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Batch Create Wallets：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/my-wallets/create-walletsarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/my-wallets/create-wallets)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through video, feel free to watch this tutorial — it walks you through how to generate hundreds of wallets in just one click!

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#steps-to-create-batch-wallets)

🔗 **Steps to Create Batch Wallets**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Enter the Quantity**: Input the number of wallets you want to create.
    
2.  **Click Create**: Click the **Create** button to generate the wallets.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FUZvaUrR5r2dab5B2fcEn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1093d07b-dca7-4939-86ab-e23eef50a429&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c8f82dc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#frequently-asked-questions)

❓Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#id-1.-how-many-wallet-addresses-can-i-create-at-once)

1\. How many wallet addresses can I create at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** CiaoTool supports generating up to 500 wallet addresses in one click. You can customize the quantity as needed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#id-2.-do-the-created-wallets-include-private-keys-how-can-i-export-them)

2\. Do the created wallets include private keys? How can I export them?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. Each wallet is generated with a corresponding private key, which can be exported as a CSV or JSON file after the operation for backup or later use.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#id-3.-are-these-wallets-secure-will-my-private-keys-be-uploaded)

3\. Are these wallets secure? Will my private keys be uploaded?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, they are secure. All wallet generation and private key handling are performed locally in your browser. The platform does not upload, store, or access any private key data.

*   平台集成了包括代币**一键发射、批量转账、冷分仓、狙击保护、流动性控制**等核心功能，涵盖从代币创建、部署、分发到管理的完整流程，用户无需编写任何代码，即可高效完成复杂的链上操作。

2️⃣ **PancakeSwap 深度整合：**支持一键创建、添加与撤销流动性，实时显示价格、滑点与池子状态，让流动性管理更清晰可控。

3️⃣ **批量与自动化工具：**提供中转转账、批量归集与发送、批量一转多等功能，大幅提升多地址操作效率。

4️⃣ **多链多场景支持：**覆盖 BSC（Four.meme、Flap、Binance Alpha）、IoTeX（Robot Pump）以及 Base、X Layer 等主流网络，满足多样化发币与运营需求。

# Web3 钱包与安全指南 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

![Page cover](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F0mlm4xi9H01DyLOiUfIP%252F1234.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07206d46-19e4-433b-8ae4-85a9ae15854d&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b717f573&sv=2)

circle-check

[**安全、稳定，为 Solana 生态提供最好用的全能工具集。**arrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#shen-me-shi-web3-qian-bao)

什么是 Web3 钱包？

Web3 钱包是一种管理链上资产的工具，可用于存储、发送和接收加密货币与 NFT，并且能够连接区块链和各种去中心化应用（DApps）。它是进入 Web3 世界的“访问钥匙”。

与 Web2 的中心化账户系统不同，Web3 钱包强调**自我主权**：

*   资产不保存在某家公司，而是记录在区块链上；
    
*   没有中心化机构替你保管，私钥在你自己手里；
    
*   钱包只是你读取链上资产的界面，不能移动或干预你的资金。
    

也正因为如此，只要私钥掌握在你自己手中，即便更换钱包应用，你的资产依然存在链上不会丢失。

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#web3-qian-bao-an-quan-zhi-nan)

Web3 钱包安全指南

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#si-yao-bao-hu)

🔐 私钥保护

*   **本地签名**：CiaoTool 的签名过程完全在本地执行，私钥不会上传或存储。
    
*   **官方绝不索要私钥**：任何要求提供私钥的人或账号都是诈骗。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#xiaoeqian-bao-jian-yi)

🪙 小额钱包建议

如果有可能暴露私钥的操作场景（如复制到剪贴板、跨设备传输等），请使用小额钱包处理，避免风险扩大。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#si-yao-fu-zhi-ji-qiao)

📄 私钥复制技巧

复制私钥时，可采用“打乱顺序、分段复制”方式，降低被剪贴板恶意程序偷窥的概率。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#bao-chi-gao-du-jing-ti)

🚨 保持高度警惕

*   谨防钓鱼链接、未知程序下载。
    
*   团队不会给你私聊，不会让你加“另一个官方群”。
    
*   不要向任何人展示你的私钥、助记词或截图。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/web3-wallet#qian-bao-xie-lou-zen-me-ban)

🆘 钱包泄露怎么办？

如果你觉得私钥已经暴露，请立即将所有资产转移到一个全新的钱包地址。

triangle-exclamation

**温馨提醒：**去中心化钱包若丢失或被盗，在没有私钥或助记词备份的情况下无法找回。请务必安全保存并正确备份您的私钥或助记词。

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 幻影钱包Phantom安装教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/phantom#mu-qian-phantom-yi-cheng-wei-yong-hu-can-yu-solana-qu-kuai-lian-shi-de-shou-xuan-qian-bao)

目前，Phantom 已成为用户参与 Solana 区块链时的首选钱包。

1.  如果你想使用 CiaoTool 工具发行代币，可以先安装 Phantom 钱包，下面给大家介绍一下安装教程：
    
2.  访问 [https://phantom.app/downloadarrow-up-right](https://phantom.app/download)
     并选择您的浏览器类型。
    
3.  按照相应扩展程序商店中的步骤将 Phantom 添加到您的浏览器。安装后，您可以浏览器插件中看到 Phantom。
    
4.  如果您是新用户，请选择“**创建新钱包**”并创建密码。
    
5.  如果您已有 Solana 钱包，只需单击**“我已有钱包”**并输入助记词即可恢复钱包。 输入密码后，选择“继续”
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FRWTmZ2b9qBTN84xn84WY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De1f18845-e50a-4e73-a1f7-5b2a6336be72&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d20f5a4&sv=2)

1.  将您的“**助记词**”存放在安全可靠的位置，这是恢复您的钱包的唯一方法。 **任何人、任何人、任何人**绝不会向您询问助记词。任何有权访问此助记词的人都可以访问您的资金。
    
2.  安全保存您的助记词后选择“继续”。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FAAyBOFAlJuWqyAVRhDKu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2dc8d92-20da-4acc-ab89-d43c02f83017&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c624121d&sv=2)

1.  安装完成后，你可以通过浏览器右上角的插件图标，找到你的钱包
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FvIVZgXRAji3dXZeGoc6j%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f7482ce-2ea1-4244-8c65-bfd260067be0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7eefcb6c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/phantom#app)

APP

*   访问 [https://phantom.app/downloadarrow-up-right](https://phantom.app/download)
     并根据您的设备类型（iOS/Android）选择应用程序市场。
    
*   您将被重定向到设备应用程序商店中的 Phantom 应用程序，按照步骤在设备上下载并安装该应用程序。
    
*   安装后，打开应用程序，您应该会看到 Phantom 入门屏幕以设置新钱包。
    
*   如果您是全新用户，请选择“**创建新钱包**”并启用设备验证（可能会根据设备类型而有所不同），以保护您的钱包免遭未经授权的访问。
    
*   如果您已有 Solana 钱包，您可以选择“**我已有钱包**”并输入您的助记词来恢复您的钱包。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252Fx8YTgv5YuDKRGeA3udcY%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De00255f3-0d03-445c-9851-119442711acb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85ab7248&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/phantom#zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

**注意事项：**

*   Phantom 钱包不仅支持 Sol 链，也支持以太坊、马蹄链，所以创建钱包之后会有 3 个地址。
    
*   提币或者转账，一定要选择复制 Solana 地址，不要选错了。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)

# Pump 开盘买入并狙击教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**开盘买入并狙击**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/snipe/launch-buy-snipearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/snipe/launch-buy-snipe)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程，手把手演示如何在 Solana 上完成开盘买入与一键狙击操作。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#ru-he-jin-xing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

🧩 如何进行开盘买入并狙击？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-tui-jian-shi-yong-phantom-huan-ying-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包 (推荐使用 Phantom-幻影钱包）**

*   打开 **Pump开盘买入并狙击** 操作界面 ，
    
*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FFtHO32vs7DNP1xGfBKkt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90fdcd89-489a-4754-b9d2-0af37b9b6470&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5380a245&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-2.-tian-xie-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

**2\. 填写代币基础信息**

*   您可以手动填写代币信息，或者点击 **【克隆】** 按钮，克隆其他代币的信息
    
*   社媒信息为可选项，不是必填项。
    
*   设置当价格上涨超过X％时，自动卖出全部Token.
    

circle-info

如果打开**自动卖出**选项，建议您不要使用开发钱包购买，或在下面填写开发钱包的私钥参与购买。否则，销售时会要求您自动签名，可能会耽误一些时间。支持多达 29 个钱包。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FMAXuMg2CxO6tfPf3ai54%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1366914d-e197-41c3-9188-3720001b3320&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8651bc5b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-3.-zi-ding-yi-he-yue-di-zhi)

**3\. 自定义合约地址**

**两种模式设置自定义合约地址：**

1.  打造你的个性化代币地址，设置代币地址是否以 'pump' 结尾。
    
    *   点击勾选☑️ pump，钱包确认生成
        
    
2.  选择「导入私钥」方式；
    
    *   将你提前生成的私钥粘贴导入（**地址必须要全新地址且没有付过SOL租金**）；
        
    *   系统将使用该地址部署你的代币，确保合约地址与预期一致。
        
    

circle-exclamation

**注：**两种方式任选其一即会立即需要钱包签名并支付平台费用（0.01 SOL)。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fb6Kg1dPWoLk1X3Dnj7Lh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14cdd169-ff1f-4e5a-82e7-f64b4f609215&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8d661f6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-4.-dev-qian-bao-she-zhi)

**4\. Dev 钱包设置**

*   若 dev 钱包未填写购买金额，则免收服务费；否则需支付与其他买入钱包相同的服务费。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252F5fqZOn8DNGY8smp0QUDz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8a55826-cbc3-4bb5-8739-ee0028491331&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46075b1a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-5.-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao-she-zhi)

**5\. 捆绑买入钱包设置**

*   **捆绑买入**钱包采用阶梯定价模式，购买钱包数越多，单个钱包服务费越低。
    
*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型: **Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON）**，或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   设置买入金额：手动输入数量，统一输入金额/百分比/全部，（全部即导入钱包能购买的最大数量）。
    
*   除服务费外，每个新地址需额外支付 **0.00203928** SOL 作为账户租金。
    

circle-info

Pump.fun开盘同时买入请保证买入钱包有足够的买入金额和 GAS，避免买入失败，同时买入最多设置 9 个地址。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F4M6Dvn6DMVb04E9FZlaG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D239d1298-d6dc-4d83-8f09-a21e6f8e7d9c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1468431e&sv=2)

circle-info

**捆绑买入**有个缺点，它有可能会被 pump 平台识别为 Bot。

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FVOX7bUX5ChOCglTEfg12%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0021a906-e957-4277-8b80-01534f386412&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=529d6546&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-6.-swap-mai-ru-qian-bao)

**6\.** Swap 买入钱包

这是后续进行 swap 操作的钱包。设置方式：

*   导入单个私钥
    
*   输入该钱包预计使用的 SOL 数量（\*具体买入的数量与需要买入的比例关联）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F53Ln5YphH4YHgDtv4S4b%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dae883599-38cb-426a-9ca4-1dabe87302ee&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4d87e2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-7.-ti-qian-sheng-cheng-dai-bi-he-yue)

**7\. 提前生成代币合约**

*   支持提前生成代币合约地址，适用于需要在正式开盘前进行预热或对接的场景。
    

circle-info

**注：**如果自定义合约地址了，就不需要再选择提前生成代币合约。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FuZwQ6IdFqZTvdaatOh47%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db46cf92b-3064-4836-89ba-c5329676aab9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cfeae441&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-8.-jito-xiao-fei-she-zhi)

**8\. Jito 小费设置**

*   配置 Jito MEV 小费，用于加速打包交易，提高排序优先级。
    
*   设置完成后点击下方 **Pump开盘买入并狙击** 按钮。
    

circle-info

此功能实现依赖于 Jito 的捆绑功能。由于网络环境、Jito节点、RPC节点和区块处理引擎的复杂影响，该功能可能面临较高的失败率。

若操作失败，不会开盘成功也不会产生任何费用，请尝试更换RPC节点，区块处理引擎，增加Jito的小费(建议0.01SOL)，并考虑在链上活跃度较低的时段再次尝试。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FrJXkhDkSlXAaURWEHnQQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8eaa3293-f7ca-452f-bf1b-ccc7a8aa0a9f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8356c262&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-9.-zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

**9\. 注意事项**

*   狙击交易存在失败风险，建议分散资金、设置合理滑点
    
*   所提供的私钥仅用于本地签名，**CiaoTool 不会上传或保存任何私钥**
    
*   开盘后如遇卡顿或链拥堵，可手动中止或刷新任务
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-1.-shen-me-shi-kun-bang-mai-ru-qian-bao)

1\. 什么是捆绑买入钱包？

*   check
    
    答：这是用于在 Pump 项目开盘时同步执行买入交易的钱包群，可最多设置 12 个。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-2.-dev-qian-bao-he-swap-qian-bao-you-shen-me-qu-bie)

2\. Dev 钱包和 Swap 钱包有什么区别？

*   check
    
    答：Dev 钱包用于部署代币合约；Swap 钱包则用于开盘后参与市场买入（通常用于控盘、流动性管理等）。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-3.-ti-qian-sheng-cheng-dai-bi-he-yue-you-shen-me-you-shi)

3\. 提前生成代币合约有什么优势？

*   check
    
    答：可节省部署等待时间，确保狙击逻辑更连贯不掉链，特别适用于短线机会。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-4.-jito-xiao-fei-bi-xu-zhi-fu-ma)

4\. Jito 小费必须支付吗？

*   check
    
    答：不是必须，但开启后可极大提高交易优先级，**防止被其他用户夹单或错过开盘**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/ecosystem/launch-buy-snipe#id-5.-xi-tong-hui-bao-cun-wo-de-si-yao-ma)

5\. 系统会保存我的私钥吗？

*   check
    
    答：不会。CiaoTool 所有签名过程都在用户本地完成，私钥不会上传服务器，确保安全性。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# Solana Update Token Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Update Token：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/updatearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/update)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#how-to-update-token-metadata-on-solana)

🖋️ **How to Update Token Metadata on Solana**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can access the update feature directly from the **Token Management** page. If the token has update permissions, an **Update** button will be displayed.
    
2.  You can go directly to the **Token Update** page, select the token, and if the authority has not been renounced, you can proceed with the update.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FGkhXrOa85S5BJHypVVHP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04689105-1edc-4275-ab3f-64471ef46117&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbd96dd2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#token-update-transaction-process)

🔄 **Token Update Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-1.-what-token-information-can-be-updated-using-ciaotool)

1\. What token information can be updated using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You can update **token metadata**, as well as adjust **mint** and **freeze authorities**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-2.-how-much-does-it-cost-to-update-token-info)

2\. How much does it cost to update token info?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** A fee is charged as marked by CiaoTool, currently **0.0375 SOL**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-3.-do-permission-updates-take-effect-immediately)

3\. Do permission updates take effect immediately?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, changes are **instantly synchronized on-chain**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-4.-can-permissions-be-restored-after-revocation)

4\. Can permissions be restored after revocation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** **No**, revoking permissions is an **irreversible action**, so proceed with caution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-5.-is-it-safe-to-update-token-information)

5\. Is it safe to update token information?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes — as long as you're using a **secure wallet for signing**, the process is safe.

# Phantom Wallet Installation Guide Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-info

Phantom is the most popular wallet for Solana users—install it first to use CiaoTool for token issuance.

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/phantom-wallet-installation-guide-tutorial#browser-extension)

**Browser Extension**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Visit the Official Website**:
    

Navigate to [https://phantom.app/downloadarrow-up-right](https://phantom.app/download)
 and select your browser type.

1.  **Add Phantom to Your Browser**: Follow the steps in your browser's extension store to add Phantom. Once installed, you will see Phantom in your browser extensions.
    
2.  **Set Up Your Wallet**:
    
    *   If you're a new user, select **"Create New Wallet"** and set up a password.
        
    *   If you already have a Solana wallet, click **"I Already Have a Wallet"** and input your recovery phrase to restore the wallet.
        
    *   After entering your password, click **"Continue"**.
        
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2F9iqHQqbiXfCNBbAGmcE4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19c84caa&sv=2)

1.  **Secure Your Recovery Phrase**:
    

*   Store your recovery phrase in a secure location. It is the only way to recover your wallet.
    
*   **Important**: Never share your recovery phrase with anyone. Anyone with access to this phrase can access your funds.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2F8grY8PuEQS6uiRtz6Qjy%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9cae362&sv=2)

1.  **Complete Installation**:
    

*   Once the installation is complete, you can find your wallet via the browser extension icon in the top-right corner.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2Fbrkq1nXEbwGr9kSHIu8q%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8efe1d04&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/phantom-wallet-installation-guide-tutorial#mobile-app)

**Mobile App**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Visit the Official Website**: Navigate to [https://phantom.app/downloadarrow-up-right](https://phantom.app/download)
     and choose the appropriate app store for your device (iOS/Android).
    
2.  **Install the Phantom App**: You will be redirected to the app store. Follow the instructions to download and install the Phantom app on your device.
    
3.  **Set Up Your Wallet**:
    
    *   If you're a new user, select **"Create New Wallet"** and enable device verification (varies by device type) to protect your wallet from unauthorized access.
        
    *   If you already have a Solana wallet, select **"I Already Have a Wallet"** and input your recovery phrase to restore the wallet.
        
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2FRoGrwHczsml7g6aeIoAu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1c04638&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/phantom-wallet-installation-guide-tutorial#important-notes)

**Important Notes**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Phantom wallet supports Solana, Ethereum, and Polygon chains. After creating a wallet, you will have three separate addresses.
    
*   When withdrawing or transferring tokens, **always copy the Solana address**. Ensure you select the correct address to avoid errors.

# Solana Batch Rent Recovery Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Batch Rent Recovery：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent-batcharrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent-batch)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#steps-to-operate)

🔗 Steps to Operate


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#step-1-import-wallets)

Step 1: Import Wallets

*   You can manually enter private keys or upload a CSV file containing multiple private keys.
    
*   The system will scan the account usage under each wallet.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#step-2-select-reclamation-type)

Step 2: Select Reclamation Type

*   ✅ Reclaim Empty Accounts Only: Automatically identifies and closes accounts with zero balance.
    
*   🔁 Reclaim All Accounts: Includes burnable token and NFT accounts; assets are burned before closing the accounts.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FRzrm4HCpgtv6OhOzoshq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba14b0c8-25b8-4353-bb36-7f526e9111c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a39fcab9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#step-3-configure-sol-reclamation-address)

Step 3: Configure SOL Reclamation Address

*   By default, the released SOL is returned to the original accounts.
    
*   You can also manually specify a single unified address to centrally manage the reclaimed rent.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#step-4-payer-settings-optional)

Step 4: Payer Settings (Optional)

*   Supports one wallet paying GAS (fees) on behalf of other addresses, useful for airdrop addresses or accounts without leftover SOL.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fc4fG8frzaSEGAzxhtE9g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5f69f02-39f9-465c-bda2-56363bb9329d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=98624e52&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#step-5-execute-reclamation)

Step 5: Execute Reclamation

*   Click \[Start Reclamation\], and the system will automatically initiate batch transactions, each signed locally.
    
*   You can monitor the processing status and amount of SOL released in real time.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#frequently-asked-questions)

❓Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-1.-what-types-of-accounts-can-be-reclaimed)

1\. What types of accounts can be reclaimed?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** SPL Token accounts, NFT accounts, and zero-balance accounts can all be reclaimed to release the associated rent if no longer needed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-2.-can-all-reclaimed-sol-be-sent-to-a-single-address)

2\. Can all reclaimed SOL be sent to a single address?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. You can manually set a single collection address, and all released SOL will be transferred there for centralized management.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-3.-can-wallets-without-gas-sol-still-perform-reclamation)

3\. Can wallets without GAS (SOL) still perform reclamation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. By enabling the "Fee Payer" feature, the system will use a designated wallet to cover gas fees for other wallets, allowing for low-cost batch operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-batch-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-4.-is-batch-processing-of-multiple-addresses-supported)

4\. Is batch processing of multiple addresses supported?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. You can import multiple wallets (via private keys or JSON files) and perform unified account scanning and reclamation in one go.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# Solana 一键清仓教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana 一键清仓：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/one-click-clearancearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/one-click-clearance)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#ru-he-shi-yong-yi-jian-qing-cang)

🧩 如何使用一键清仓？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1\. 连接钱包**

*   点击 **连接钱包**，完成钱包授权。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F3RQT1KjVgijVDHJcZ7Mo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89ac695e-0acb-4876-b56f-aaffce2ad4f9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8259d66&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-2.-xuan-ze-qian-bao-qing-cang-mo-shi)

**2\. 选择钱包清仓模式**

*   选择需要进行清仓操作的钱包：
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F565AP0gskJyVwPyziJRU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De639a2cb-c94c-4e29-9cc5-2636591baada&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=976ce2b8&sv=2)

*   **当前绑定钱包**：直接清理当前已连接的钱包资产
    
*   **其他钱包**：通过导入私钥清理其他钱包资产
    

circle-exclamation

⚠️ **注意：**钱包中需要有一定数量的 **SOL**，用于支付**操作费用和Gas 费用**，否则可能导致交易失败。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-3.-xuan-ze-xu-yao-qing-cang-de-token)

**3\. 选择需要清仓的 Token**

*   系统会自动检测钱包中的代币列表，选择需要卖出的 Token。
    
*   如果没有检测到代币，可以点击 **刷新** 重新扫描。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FkQL508NoutltA912bSIA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5222d804-7055-468a-b26e-332b9011d328&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30d24455&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-4.-kai-shi-qing-cang)

**4\. 开始清仓**

*   查看费用预估详情
    
*   确认信息后点击 **一键清仓**，系统将自动执行卖出操作。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#chang-jian-wen-ti)

**❓常见问题**

**1\. 一键清仓会卖出钱包中的所有代币吗？**

*   check
    
    答：系统会检测钱包中的代币列表，您可以选择需要清仓的 Token，确认后才会执行卖出操作。
    

**2\. 为什么清仓前需要保留一定数量的 SOL？**

*   check
    
    答：每笔交易都需要支付 **Gas 费用**，同时还需要支付平台服务费，因此钱包中需要保留一定的 **SOL** 才能完成清仓交易。
    

**3\. 如果没有检测到代币怎么办？**

*   check
    
    答：可以点击 **刷新** 按钮重新扫描钱包资产。如果仍未检测到，可能是该代币暂未被系统识别或没有可交易流动性。
    

**4\. 清仓过程中如果交易失败会扣费吗？**

*   check
    
    答：如果交易未成功执行，平台不会收取服务费，但链上交易产生的 **Gas 费用** 仍可能产生。
    

**5\. 一键清仓支持多个钱包吗？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。您可以选择**当前连接钱包**，也可以通过**导入其他钱包私钥**的方式，对不同钱包进行清仓操作。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

triangle-exclamation
