# 批量归集(多对一)教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

批量归集(多对一)：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/batch-collectionarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/batch-collection)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#ru-he-jin-xing-pi-liang-gui-ji-duo-dui-yi)

🧩 **如何进行**批量归集 (多对一) ？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FQTahwSsW0pTtmEPYxTYs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc1b154a-9dba-48dc-886b-6b77e17c102b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30363db0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-2.-xuan-ze-gui-ji-dai-bi)

**2\. 选择归集代币**

选择需要归集的代币，可下拉选择也可手动粘贴代币地址

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F5KyvMhH3ryA9Dbizyjaq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D004d0a4d-2759-4a45-b287-a02848ea590c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=34101b17&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-3.-dao-ru-dai-gui-ji-qian-bao)

**3\. 导入待归集钱包**

**导入钱包设置**：

*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   刷新导入钱包余额
    
*   设置归集数量，支持全部、固定归集数量、保留数量三种设置。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FBVzcIItqU4isRnRGjz3A%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8f73c88-865b-4ab4-b683-04de1a644c25&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4f25c5&sv=2)

*   批量操作删除错误项
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FYnmLG6klh6QpauX1kmat%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff70a436-f3e1-4135-86c3-aef3804e5222&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7b2352d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-4.-she-zhi-shou-xu-fei-qian-bao)

**4\. 设置手续费钱包**

私钥导入支付手续费的钱包，请确保钱包余额充足。

*   所有的服务费、gas 费、jito 小费都将由当前手续费钱包支付
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-5.-she-zhi-jie-shou-qian-bao)

5\. 设置接收钱包

导入归集到的接收地址，可选择当前钱包。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-6.-que-ren-xin-xi)

**6\. 确认信息**

*   检查无误后，点击下方 **开始归集** 按钮即可完成操作。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-1.-shen-me-shi-pi-liang-gui-ji)

1\. 什么是批量归集？

*   check
    
    答： 批量归集指将多个钱包地址中持有的代币统一转入一个主地址，**便于集中管理资产、统一调配资金**。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-2.-ru-he-dao-ru-duo-ge-di-zhi)

2\. 如何导入多个地址？

*   check
    
    答： 可通过粘贴私钥、上传文件（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON）导入多个地址。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-3.-ke-yi-gui-ji-na-xie-zi-chan-lei-xing)

3\. 可以归集哪些资产类型？

*   check
    
    答： 支持归集 Solana 主链的 SPL 标准代币（包含 Token2022）及 SOL 主币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-4.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-gui-ji-shi-zi-ding-yi-zhu-zhang-hu-di-zhi)

4\. 是否支持归集时自定义主账户地址？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可手动输入目标主地址，或选择当前已连接钱包作为归集接收方。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/multi-to-one#id-5.-shi-fou-ke-yi-zhi-gui-ji-yueda-yu-mou-ge-shu-zhi-de-qian-bao)

5\. 是否可以只归集余额大于某个数值的钱包？

*   check
    
    答： 可以设置最小余额门槛（如：仅归集余额 > 1 SOL 的地址），**避免浪费资源归集“尘埃资产”**。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Token Snapshot Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Token Snapshot:** [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/tokenTool/snapshot-token-holdersarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/tokenTool/snapshot-token-holders)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#common-use-cases)

✅ Common Use Cases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Pre-airdrop targeting for active users
    
*   Analyze whales for market cap control
    
*   Identify loyal holders for community rewards
    
*   Support for data-driven marketing campaigns
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#step-1-select-a-token)

🪙 Step 1: Select a Token


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the target token address manually, or choose from tokens held in your connected wallet.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZWMnlSC6ZKFY1ZpUxSHw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90f1900e-1fb8-487b-9acb-fd51ff6403f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fea1e043&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#step-2-set-filter-options)

📊 Step 2: Set Filter Options


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#top-holder-filter-optional)

✅ Top Holder Filter (Optional)

Choose from preset ranges to fetch top holders:

*   Top 100 / 500 / 1000 / 2000 / 5000 / 10000 This will retrieve wallets with the highest token balances.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#minimum-holding-amount-optional)

✅ Minimum Holding Amount (Optional)

Set a minimum token amount (e.g., 1000 tokens) to exclude low-balance or dust wallets from the snapshot.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FUCLyIsKw4N1UGi4rIJss%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De40d755e-91a9-4f18-918e-25782206d7b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b28b308f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#step-3-generate-and-export-snapshot)

🧾 Step 3: Generate & Export Snapshot


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click **“Token Snapshot”** to fetch on-chain data. Once completed, export your results in one of the following formats:

*   **CSV** – ideal for airdrop distribution
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FcNYJ587qfhIS3vVOurjd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8624b559-86e2-4bd2-888d-c73645346d91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2f24e93&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#frequently-asked-questions)

❓Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#id-1.-what-types-of-tokens-are-supported)

**1\. What types of tokens are supported?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** All SPL-standard tokens are supported, including both standard tokens and Token2022 types.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#id-2.-what-addresses-can-be-filtered-in-a-snapshot)

**2\. What addresses can be filtered in a snapshot?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You can filter Top 100 to Top 10,000 holders or set a custom minimum token balance to target specific users.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#id-3.-can-i-export-the-snapshot-results)

**3\. Can I export the snapshot results?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, results can be exported in CSV or JSON format for airdrop planning or market analysis.

# SOL Relay Transfer Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**SOL Relay Transfer:** [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/relay-transferarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/relay-transfer)

circle-exclamation

**Note**

*   The number of **sending wallets** must be the same as the number of **recipient wallets**.
    
*   Relay Transfer only supports **SOL transfers**. Please make sure to **save the generated relay address information** before starting the transfer.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#how-to-use-solana-relay-transfer)

🧩 How to Use Solana Relay Transfer？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-1.-connect-wallet)

1\. Connect Wallet

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, choose your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fk6uyv7QEAdoKL4wiUrmy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5fc2e69-1acf-46c8-8c0c-265886434da1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=929f88ba&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-2.-select-wallet-clearance-mode)

2\. Select Wallet Clearance Mode

*   Relay Transfer only supports **SOL transfers**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-3.-select-sending-wallets)

**3\. Select Sending Wallets**

You can import multiple wallets in two ways:

*   Manually paste **multiple private keys**
    
*   Upload a file containing private keys (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FyY1qRRDsSiuVHordqOvO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09912c85-a9a5-41e8-80f5-2ece8168e2fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2935f0c&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

⚠️ **Note:** Ensure the sending wallets have sufficient **SOL**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-4.-select-recipient-addresses)

**4\. Select Recipient Addresses**

*   Enter the **target wallet addresses**.
    
*   The number of recipient addresses **must match** the number of sending wallets.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FXgUBwjzNjH43tAcvhyse%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd3356b17-3805-4d25-99b3-71f398ebea2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=554cbf88&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-5.-set-relay-amount-per-address)

**5\. Set Relay Amount per Address**

Choose how the relay amount is allocated:

*   **Fixed value** (e.g., each address transfers **1 / 4 / 10**), or **custom input** for address
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FosdyFjuzdV2RESucHaLf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D89b09d1a-a582-4fc8-87c3-016af9092687&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2fdd2650&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-6.-generate-relay-wallets)

**6\. Generate Relay Wallets**

*   The system will automatically generate **intermediate relay addresses** used to route the transactions and obscure the transfer path.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-7.-confirm-transfer)

**7\. Confirm Transfer**

*   After verifying the details, click **“Confirm Transfer.”**
    
*   The system will execute the relay process sequentially and complete the fund distribution.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#faq)

❓FAQ

**1\. What is the difference between Relay Transfer and a normal transfer?**

*   check
    
    **A:** Relay Transfer inserts a set of intermediate wallets between the sender and receiver, creating multiple transfer paths to enhance privacy and reduce on-chain traceability.
    

**2\. Why must the number of sending addresses match the number of receiving addresses?**

*   check
    
    **A:** Each sending address is mapped to one target address. Maintaining a one-to-one mapping ensures accurate fund distribution and correct execution of the transfer logic.
    

**3\. Do I need to prepare SOL for each relay wallet?**

*   check
    
    **A:** No. The system automatically generates relay wallets and executes the transfers. However, your **fee-paying wallet** must have enough SOL to cover the transaction fees for each transfer.
    

**4\. Is the relay process safe? Can I control the relay wallets?**

*   check
    
    **A:** The private keys of all relay wallets will be provided for you to save. The entire process runs locally or in a trusted environment, and **CiaoTool does not store user keys**, ensuring security and control.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Solana One-Click Clearance Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana One-Click Clearance:** [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/one-click-clearancearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/one-click-clearance)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#how-to-use-solana-one-click-clearance)

🧩 How to Use Solana One-Click Clearance？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-1.-connect-wallet)

1\. Connect Wallet

*   Click **Select Wallet** and complete the wallet authorization.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fk6uyv7QEAdoKL4wiUrmy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df5fc2e69-1acf-46c8-8c0c-265886434da1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=929f88ba&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-2.-select-wallet-clearance-mode)

2\. Select Wallet Clearance Mode

Choose the wallet you want to clear:

*   **Current Connected Wallet:** Directly clear assets from the currently connected wallet.
    
*   **Other Wallet:** Import a private key to clear assets from another wallet.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FCIOLkLXhGjMb4isYs646%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c25defc-a767-4756-ab00-5b0c0a264afc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64bad4a5&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

⚠️ **Note:** The wallet must contain a certain amount of **SOL** to cover **operation fees and gas fees**, otherwise the transaction may fail.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-3.-select-tokens-to-clear)

3\. Select Tokens to Clear

*   The system will automatically detect the tokens in your wallet. Select the tokens you want to sell.
    
*   If no tokens are detected, click **Refresh** to scan again.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F9FvPTlhl5HHTWjeIsv4z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ce7f39a-f151-4912-a203-39e2cad67e51&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e6a7050&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#id-4.-start-clearance)

4\. Start Clearance

*   Review the **estimated fee details**, then click **One-Click Clearance** to execute the sell orders automatically.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fg2ZVer6Unf78CSNSdFty%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19dfb324-90fa-451c-bd1e-399338805235&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d34ec16&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-click-clearance#faq)

❓FAQ

**1\. Will One-Click Clearance sell all tokens in the wallet?**

*   check
    
    **A:** The system will detect the token list in your wallet. You can select which tokens to clear, and the sale will only be executed after confirmation.
    

**2\. Why do I need to keep some SOL before clearance?**

*   check
    
    **A:** Each transaction requires **gas fees**, and platform service fees also apply. Therefore, the wallet must have sufficient **SOL** to complete the clearance process.
    

**3\. What should I do if no tokens are detected?**

*   check
    
    **A:** Click the **Refresh** button to rescan the wallet assets. If tokens still do not appear, the token may not be recognized by the system or may lack tradable liquidity.
    

**4\. Will I be charged if the clearance transaction fails?**

*   check
    
    **A:** If the transaction fails, the platform will not charge a service fee. However, **on-chain gas fees** may still apply.
    

**5\. Does One-Click Clearance support multiple wallets?**

*   check
    
    **A:** Yes. You can clear the **currently connected wallet** or import **other wallet private keys** to clear assets from different wallets.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Blog**: [https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blog)
    
*   **Medium:** [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **YouTube:** [https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp：**[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Volume Bot Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The Volume Bot feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

circle-check

Here’s an example using **Pump** with the **Volume Bot：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/multi-swaparrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/multi-swap)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#how-to-use-the-volume-bot)

🧩 **How to Use the Volume Bot？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve the authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Ffgnd09X7ZtGR2lviXN5B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6aba1db7-e8d7-429b-b19f-2c6bd57bf55f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a6907b8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-2.-open-the-volume-bot-interface)

**2\. Open the Volume Bot Interface**

*   Navigate to the **Volume Bot** operation page.
    

circle-info

When selecting **Meteora**, this also applies to **Bags** and **Believe**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FrSOvEmb4gcggsjk9ys2w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D740c048e-5afd-4b40-9a94-8a649096e631&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0cf5f12&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

*   **Select Trade Direction:** The first token is fixed as the **value token**. Click the middle switch button to change the trade direction, and manually enter the second token contract address.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FxhAEX9uxEefTlhkkR1a2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d41f924-f319-4423-ba0c-a32e4c02ce1e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c454ca4&sv=2)

*   **Trading Wallet Setup:**
    
    *   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
        
    *   Refresh imported wallet balances
        
    *   Set buy amount
        
    *   Batch set trade amount mode: **All Amount**, **Fixed Amount**, **Random Amount**, or **Random Percentage**
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F80j5UKtXWAEzVUEyaEpy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32912b7d-cb2d-4218-9100-998f2b8073fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8956fed&sv=2)

*   **Other Trading Parameters:** Set the task interval and slippage.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FjnS5ZCfQlkWS2mmTsmUH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8ab3704-aecb-4c5f-a435-6e5c147fe432&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c9b429a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-4.-set-jito-mev-tip)

**4\. Set Jito MEV Tip**

*   Choose a suitable route or enter a custom tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F23u1IlBphw6M4vYfeguV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da01e8ddf-afb5-42c4-8a6d-452700498771&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78963f85&sv=2)

*   Click **“Start Batch Transactions”** to execute.
    

circle-info

⚠️ **Note:** It is recommended to enable **Auto Slippage** for best results.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-1.-what-is-pump-batch-trading)

1\. What is Pump batch trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Batch trading refers to presetting multiple wallet transaction instructions, which the system will automatically execute at specified times or triggered conditions, improving trading efficiency and enabling unified operations across multiple addresses.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-2.-what-operations-can-be-executed-in-batch)

2\. What operations can be executed in batch?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Supports batch buying, selling, swapping, bundled buying, and more, distributing tasks to multiple wallets with one click, suitable for market making, controlling supply, and volume boosting strategies.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-3.-how-to-import-batch-wallets)

3\. How to import batch wallets?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Wallets can be imported in bulk by pasting addresses and private keys or uploading CSV files, and the system also supports one-click automatic wallet generation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-4.-will-batch-trades-be-sent-simultaneously)

4\. Will batch trades be sent simultaneously?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, the system initiates all transaction requests synchronously within the same round and can leverage Jito priority channels to improve packaging efficiency and avoid missing market opportunities.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/batch-trading#id-5.-is-interval-or-polling-execution-supported)

5\. Is interval or polling execution supported?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, you can set trading frequency and interval between rounds; the system will automatically execute volume boosting, chart manipulation, or strategy rotation without manual intervention.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# 批量转账(一对多)教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**批量转账(一对多)：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/one-to-multiarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/one-to-multi)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#ru-he-jin-xing-yi-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang)

🧩 **如何进行**一对多转账？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

1\. 绑定钱包

*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FQTahwSsW0pTtmEPYxTYs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc1b154a-9dba-48dc-886b-6b77e17c102b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=30363db0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-2.-da-kai-yi-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang-cao-zuo-ye)

2\. 打开一对多转账操作页

*   导入私钥，系统自动刷新SOL余额与Token余额，请保证钱包中有充足的 SOL。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-3.-xuan-ze-fa-song-dai-bi)

3\. 选择发送代币

*   既可以选择 SOL，又可以选择当前钱包 Token.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fer2ljGeKRhRL3wtzFc5I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61ce2021-4fc2-4cd5-822c-c45dcefdf06c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89c1751a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-4.-dao-ru-jie-shou-di-zhi)

4\. 导入接收地址

**导入钱包设置**：

*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   刷新导入钱包余额
    
*   设置转账数量，支持统一金额或随机范围。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fk2pvskV4njBicN67CWBi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68454f44-bc2d-4368-8dcd-9f0c37c7a2d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d90ad74&sv=2)

*   批量操作删除资金不足的钱包
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FaGuuQsnX2WaCRBAEc42Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D916f9a6e-2332-4eb9-9cd5-f7929430d3a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=559dadc7&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**注：**在慢速一对多转账中可设置任务执行间隔时间（固定时间或随机）

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FRdjdB5e2bovl6R8DermM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2e6126c-e81d-4414-b86d-eed6114019eb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ad2e3b36&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-5.-que-ren-xin-xi)

5\. 确认信息

*   检查无误后，点击下方 **确认转账** 按钮即可完成操作。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-1.-shen-me-shi-yi-dui-duo-pi-liang-zhuan-zhang)

1\. 什么是一对多批量转账？

*   check
    
    答： 一对多批量转账是指从一个钱包地址，向多个目标地址**同时发送代币**的操作，常用于空投、奖励发放、资产分发等场景。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-2.-ru-he-dao-ru-jie-shou-di-zhi)

2\. 如何导入接收地址？

*   check
    
    答： 你可以手动输入地址，也可以上传 CSV 文件导入目标地址列表（支持地址+金额格式），系统会自动识别并展示预览。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-3.-mei-ge-di-zhi-ke-yi-zhuan-bu-tong-shu-liang-ma)

3\. 每个地址可以转不同数量吗？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可以为每个地址设置不同的转账数量，也可以设置统一的金额分发给所有目标地址。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-4.-ke-yi-tong-shi-zhuan-duo-ge-dai-bi-ma)

4\. 可以同时转多个代币吗？

*   check
    
    答： 当前版本支持选择单一 SPL 代币或 SOL 进行批量转账；如需多种资产分发，可多次执行操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-5.-qian-ming-he-guang-bo-jiao-yi-shi-zi-dong-de-ma)

5\. 签名和广播交易是自动的吗？

*   check
    
    答： 是的。CiaoTool 将自动打包所有交易请求，并通过本地钱包签名后统一广播，无需逐条确认，**极大提升转账效率**。

# Anti-MEV Volume Bot Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The Anti-MEV Volume Bot feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

circle-check

**Here’s an example using Pump for a Anti-MEV Volume Bot**：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/anti-mevarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/anti-mev)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#how-to-run-anti-mev-volume-bot)

🛡️ How to Run Anti-MEV Volume Bot？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve the authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F90zr2wczTd1Ia8AtbbYn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea75e5c5-e0c5-4a8e-86c5-dc0d51ddc410&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a9944dda&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-2.-open-the-anti-mev-volume-bot-interface)

**2\. Open the** Anti-MEV Volume Bot **Interface**

*   Navigate to the **Anti-MEV Volume Bot** operation page.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F8FwOcvu9dBg276rDloVu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb821a35-98ee-43d9-ae34-22c4d1681633&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=423cb2bf&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

*   **Select Token:** Choose a token from the connected wallet or manually enter the token contract address.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FrQxTgDaHxtVCtxI27pzM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24101064-806d-4cbf-a855-49e7d948db3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ca9684e&sv=2)

*   **Brush Volume Wallet Setup:** Supports two modes (Import wallets via private keys、Use the current wallet）
    

circle-info

Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fjb6Jc2Yy8PJV9lspblB9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D391f0dbc-f861-4804-bcbd-75a7a998f68d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=46803689&sv=2)

*   **Volume Parameters:**
    
    *   Set volume amount (randomization supported)
        
    *   Set task interval (seconds)
        
    *   Set number of runs (**1 buy + 1 sell = 1 cycle**)
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FaEaXivGY37UfbJQMwBa8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78a066e2-b5a7-4f48-ba43-5e7b1e1c5fa7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c9b8a14d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-4.-configure-jito-and-execute)

**4\. Configure Jito and Execute**

*   Choose a suitable route or enter a custom tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FDW7Q2lNv9GQDIBk7ONGM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad1a0659-bf57-4512-83dd-9ae0c35abe14&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a82dbfb&sv=2)

*   Click **“Start Volume Brushing”** to begin.
    

circle-info

⚠️ **Note:** Do **not refresh the page** after starting. Refreshing will interrupt the volume task.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-1.-what-is-a-mev-volume)

1\. What is a “MEV Volume”?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** A MEV Volume refers to inserting disruptive transactions between the buy and sell addresses, causing disorder in the transaction queue and affecting the intended execution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-2.-how-does-a-mev-volume-affect-project-teams)

2\. How does a MEV Volume affect project teams?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It disrupts the strategy execution order, disturbs market rhythm, and may even lead to failures in market making or token distribution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-3.-how-to-use-ciaotool-to-prevent-mev-volume)

3\. How to use CiaoTool to prevent MEV Volume?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** By setting the buy/sell order within the same address and defining slippage tolerance, CiaoTool ensures transaction atomicity and execution priority.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-4.-what-role-does-jito-technology-play-in-preventing-mev-volume)

4\. What role does Jito technology play in preventing MEV Volume?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Jito can bundle key transactions and send them to the priority pool, enhancing on-chain processing order and preventing queue insertion.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/anti-mev-volume#id-5.-does-it-support-multi-address-mev-volume-protection-execution)

5\. Does it support multi-address MEV volume protection execution?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, it can be combined with batch trading tools to implement multi-address strategy execution and order protection.

# Bundled Sell Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The bundled sell feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

*   Bundling supports single-address operations, but for a single address, it’s recommended to use the market-making feature instead.
    
*   When performing bundled buys or sells, do not leave blank lines between addresses, as this may trigger an error.
    

circle-check

**Here’s an example using Raydium for a Bundled Sell:** [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/raydium/bundled-sellarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/raydium/bundled-sell)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#how-to-perform-a-bundled-sell)

🧩 How to Perform a Bundled Sell？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve the authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fzwc3Q4KOtFaj42ofZA0Y%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfef4f2cc-7f5d-4ee9-97da-8d40471a0388&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=154e2c0f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-2.-open-the-bundled-sell-interface)

**2\. Open the Bundled Sell Interface**

*   Navigate to the bundled sell operation page for your selected platform.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FaGwYowat5Uwkf3MIxj6G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deda94c4b-22c7-4389-be80-04728e0dbc4f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2d47a07&sv=2)

circle-info

When selecting **Meteora**, this also applies to **Bags** and **Believe**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

**Token to Sell:** You can choose a token from the currently connected wallet or manually enter the token contract address.

*   **Bundled Sell Wallet Setup:**
    
    *   Batch import wallets (supported formats: **Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
        
    *   Refresh imported wallet balances
        
    *   Set sell amounts
        
    *   Batch remove wallets with insufficient f
        
    

circle-exclamation

**Note:** When selecting **Bonk**, the wallet quantity rules for bundled selling differ.

*   If **Send Type = JITO** → Maximum **9 wallets per group**
    
*   If **Send Type = RPC** → Maximum **10 wallets per group**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fp5VY7nlYLKNBS8hPvZ4d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2bf56d3-152c-4c57-b68f-f93fd4f5c453&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f522e9c6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-4.-configure-jito-parameters)

**4\. Configure Jito Parameters**

*   Choose a recommended speed setting or customize the tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FRy7aetEXvyx5HzKmfw0f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0d9d77f-0530-4885-a827-446c0a77038f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f6ac893&sv=2)

*   Click the **“Bundled Sell”** button at the bottom to execute the purchase.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#important-notes)

**⚙️ Important Notes**

*   Bundled selling supports multiple wallet groups participating simultaneously.
    
*   **Service Fee:** Paid by the **first imported wallet**.
    
*   **Jito Tip:** Paid by the **last wallet in the group**.
    
*   **SOL Balance Requirement:** Ensure all participating wallets have sufficient SOL.
    

circle-info

If any step fails, clear feedback will be provided. **No fees are charged for failed transactions.**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-1.-what-is-bundled-selling)

1\. What is bundled selling?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** bundled selling refers to **sending multiple sell instructions or addresses in a single transaction** to improve efficiency and execution priority.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-2.-what-are-the-benefits-of-bundled-selling)

2\. What are the benefits of bundled selling?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It increases **execution speed**, reduces **slippage**, and helps avoid missing the best selling window due to manual delays.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-3.-what-role-does-jito-play-in-bundled-selling)

3\. What role does Jito play in bundled selling?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Jito **prioritizes bundled transactions**, making it easier to complete sales during peak congestion.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-4.-can-i-bundle-sells-from-multiple-addresses)

4\. Can I bundle sells from multiple addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes — you can **combine multiple wallets** and sell in one batch with a single click.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-sell#id-5.-is-there-a-risk-of-failure-in-bundled-selling)

5\. Is there a risk of failure in bundled selling?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes — issues like **network congestion** or **insufficient balance** may still cause failure, so it's best to double-check conditions and slippage settings in advance.

# One To Multi Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana One To Multi：** [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/one-to-multiarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/one-to-multi)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#how-to-perform-one-to-multi-transfer)

🧩 **How to Perform One To Multi Transfer？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-1.-connect-wallet)

**1\. Connect Wallet**

*   Click **“Connect Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FEbVbu5l57Ns7Imk97Rjq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07772cf2-1994-4010-9205-aa7f1e278872&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f6d34dae&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-2.-open-the-one-to-multi-transfer-page)

**2\. Open the One To Multi Transfer Page**

*   Import the private key. The system will automatically refresh the **SOL balance** and **token balances**.
    
*   Please ensure the wallet has sufficient **SOL**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-3.-select-token-to-send)

**3\. Select Token to Send**

*   You can choose to send **SOL** or any **token from the current wallet**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FYd4b8rZhTimYK2KffYIh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8ad60ce-6ce3-46b9-8af1-6da2263efc09&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1dcad31&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-4.-import-recipient-addresses)

**4\. Import Recipient Addresses**

**Wallet Import Options:**

*   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**)，or manually paste addresses/private keys
    
*   Refresh imported wallet balances
    
*   Set transfer amounts (**fixed amount or random range**)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fp5dszS3tbXvqljOd9L0v%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9df4d52-6d29-4fdd-a4e2-c746ee31cbb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed16f3e6&sv=2)

*   Batch remove wallets with insufficient funds.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FH1ypS6iQ4gZKVYbYM7Qw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De4c66868-432f-4070-94e1-2084243d308a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=236afcd9&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note:** In **One To Multi Slow**, you can set the **task execution interval** (fixed time or random).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FlnKmOy4drjbIRQW6Sr6a%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78f3c353-6b17-4354-9875-080cdb0804ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81d38dbd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-5.-confirm-information)

**5\. Confirm Information**

*   After reviewing the details, click **“Confirm Transfer”** to complete the operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#successful-operation-case)

☑️ **Successful Operation Case**

*   When the task starts executing, a log pop-up will appear to update the transaction progress in real time.
    
*   After the transaction is successful, a transaction link will be provided, which you can click to view details directly.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FhY8LI7HWDhSszclnoYno%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4b0d9f4-39f5-490b-bdd6-2b3f8daca020&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95599eb9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#failed-operation-case)

❗️Failed Operation Case

*   If any issues arise during the process, we will clearly inform you. No fees will be charged for failed operations.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FAqYeeYn7ohWrJVkZpLX2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81da612d-ed9b-44cc-bb04-b884c73feab1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f1ea523&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#frequently-asked-questions)

❓Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-1.-what-is-a-one-to-many-batch-transfer)

1\. What is a one-to-many batch transfer?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Sending tokens from one wallet to many addresses at once.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-2.-how-do-i-import-addresses)

2\. How do I import addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Manually enter or upload a CSV file.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-3.-can-each-address-get-a-different-amount)

3\. Can each address get a different amount?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, supports custom or equal amounts.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-4.-can-i-transfer-multiple-tokens-at-once)

4\. Can I transfer multiple tokens at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, only one token per batch.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/one-to-multi#id-5.-is-the-process-automatic)

5\. Is the process automatic?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, signing and broadcasting are handled automatically.

# Solana 地址与优先费用指南 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/address-and-fee#solana-di-zhi-shi-yong-zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

🔑 Solana 地址使用注意事项

*   创建 Solana 钱包时，会生成长度为 43 或 44 的地址，这些地址都是可用的。但如果在使用过程中错误地修改了地址——例如删掉 44 位地址中的一位，或给 43 位地址多加一位——虽然得到的新地址依然符合 43/44 位格式，但它**不再对应原来的私钥或助记词**，属于“黑洞地址”，资产将无法找回。
    
*   Solana 地址采用无校验位的 Base58 编码，仅能验证字符和长度，无法检测地址是否被篡改。相比之下，TRON（波场）也使用 Base58，但包含校验位，一旦地址修改会立即报错。因此，在转账时请务必核对收款地址的完整性，确保资金安全。
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/other/address-and-fee#solana-you-xian-ji-fei-yong-zhi-nan)

⚡ Solana 优先级费用指南

Solana 区块链允许用户通过支付额外费用来提高交易在网络中的处理优先级。支付更高费用的交易会比低费用交易更快被验证者确认，就像以太坊的 Gas 机制一样。

CiaoTool 根据网络情况设置了三档优先级费用：

*   **低优先级**：单笔交易费用 ≤ 0.0001 SOL
    
*   **高优先级**：单笔交易费用 ≤ 0.003 SOL
    

用户可根据交易紧急程度选择合适的优先级，以实现更快的交易确认速度。

# Sell Bundled Buy Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The sell and bundled buy feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

*   Bundling supports single-address operations, but for a single address, it’s recommended to use the market-making feature instead.
    
*   When performing bundled buys or sells, do not leave blank lines between addresses, as this may trigger an error.
    

circle-check

**Here’s an example using Pump for a Sell and Bundled Buy：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/bundled-sell-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/bundled-sell-buy)

circle-info

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#how-to-sell-and-perform-a-bundled-buy)

🧩 **How to Sell and Perform a Bundled Buy？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Connect Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve the authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F3IHza56EJHQau54mFBPb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86fb364d-a9c1-40d7-9688-0c569ca2d459&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be33cf64&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-2.-open-the-sell--bundled-buy-interface)

**2\. Open the Sell + Bundled Buy Interface**

*   Go to the **Sell and Bundled Buy** operation page.
    

circle-info

When selecting **Meteora**, this also applies to **Bags** and **Believe**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fi2KsIy3w7788uwCAhJJK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3cf3332b-131c-4643-981d-0e561fe50de8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be8607e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

**Select Token:** Choose a token from the connected wallet or manually enter the token contract address.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FyAt8iD2WA0FEYwhLUGef%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4c46c4a-37c7-4e9f-b63a-3be82da68658&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bf8f8fff&sv=2)

**Sell Wallet Setup:**

*   Manually paste the private key
    
*   Set the sell amount
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FqX4CwrSvB7k2KsrAzxLB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D68704510-0f70-4a91-90e2-c7b00bcd97c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1193ba6f&sv=2)

**Buy Wallet Setup:**

*   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
    
*   Refresh imported wallet balances
    
*   Set buy amounts
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FRA3w1Rru7m2WutCzGBAN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77903715-6156-4b5d-94b3-e1affdd526fb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=da1e33f0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-4.-configure-jito-and-execute)

**4\. Configure Jito and Execute**

*   Choose a recommended speed or enter a custom tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F0dkY576Fe0emEjg0n4Q0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D48adf1c6-eaed-443a-8bae-ddae66ad5b78&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22397371&sv=2)

*   Click **“Sell and Bundled Buy”** to execute the transaction.
    

If any step fails, clear feedback will be provided. **No fees are charged for failed transactions.**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#important-notes)

⚠️ **Important Notes**

*   This feature supports multiple addresses participating in the bundled buy simultaneously.
    
*   **All service fees are paid by the first imported wallet.**
    
*   The required **SOL amount** depends on the token price. Make sure buy wallets have sufficient SOL balance.
    

circle-info

If a transaction fails, try reducing the buy amount and resubmitting.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-1.-what-is-sell-and-bundled-buy)

1\. What is "Sell and Bundled Buy"?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It refers to **selling tokens and immediately buying them back with a new address** in the same block, enabling seamless position switching.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-2.-why-use-a-new-address-to-buy)

2\. Why use a new address to buy?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Using a new address helps **avoid on-chain tagging**, reducing the risk of detection by monitoring systems.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-3.-will-this-operation-be-flagged-as-price-manipulation-or-wash-trading)

3\. Will this operation be flagged as price manipulation or wash trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No — as long as the **timing and amount are controlled**, it appears as a normal position switch on-chain.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-4.-can-i-use-multiple-new-addresses-for-the-buyback)

4\. Can I use multiple new addresses for the buyback?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes — you can specify **multiple target addresses** to enhance distribution and stealth.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/sell-bundled-buy#id-5.-does-this-function-require-special-configuration)

5\. Does this function require special configuration?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No — with **CiaoTool**, you can execute the entire strategy in one click without complex setup.

# Solana 批量租金回收教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana 批量租金回收：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent-batcharrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent-batch)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 操作步骤

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#di-1-bu-dao-ru-qian-bao)

第 1 步：导入钱包

*   可选择手动输入私钥或上传包含多个私钥的 CSV 文件。
    
*   系统将扫描每个钱包下的账户使用情况。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#di-2-bu-xuan-ze-hui-shou-lei-xing)

第 2 步：选择回收类型

*   ✅ **仅回收空账户**：自动识别余额为零的账户并关闭。
    
*   🔁 **回收所有账户**：包括可销毁的代币和 NFT 账户，将资产烧毁后关闭账户。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fg7S4GJzMnsSsAahvstgF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da81687f1-045e-4bb9-b8fc-dd4cb9d5f186&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29cb84ee&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#di-3-bu-pei-zhi-sol-hui-shou-di-zhi)

第 3 步：配置 SOL 回收地址

*   默认将释放的 SOL 回收到原账户。
    
*   也可手动指定一个**统一接收地址**，用于集中管理回收的租金。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#di-4-bu-dai-fu-she-zhi-ke-xuan)

第 4 步：代付设置（可选）

*   支持由一个钱包为其他地址支付 GAS（手续费），适用于空投地址或未留 SOL 的账号回收。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FPpQiTDbBNp8aCC43OuCJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D534451ed-2654-4be5-a21d-054703452029&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44474a6e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#di-5-bu-zhi-xing-hui-shou-cao-zuo)

第 5 步：执行回收操作

*   点击【开始回收】，系统将自动发起批量交易，每笔交易均由本地签名完成。
    
*   可实时查看处理状态与释放的 SOL 数量。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#id-1.-ke-yi-hui-shou-na-xie-zhang-hu-lei-xing)

1\. 可以回收哪些账户类型？

*   check
    
    答： 包括 SPL Token 账户、NFT 账户、空余额账户，只要不再使用都可以释放对应租金。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#id-2.-shi-fou-ke-yi-jiang-suo-you-sol-tong-yi-hui-shou-dao-yi-ge-di-zhi)

2\. 是否可以将所有 SOL 统一回收到一个地址？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可以手动设定一个回收地址，所有释放的 SOL 将集中转入该地址，便于统一管理。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#id-3.-dao-ru-de-qian-bao-mei-you-gassol-hai-neng-hui-shou-ma)

3\. 导入的钱包没有 GAS（SOL）还能回收吗？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。如果开启“代付功能”，系统会使用你指定的钱包为其他钱包代付手续费，实现低成本批量操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/batch-rent-recovery#id-4.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-pi-liang-chu-li-duo-ge-di-zhi-de-zhang-hu)

4\. 是否支持批量处理多个地址的账户？

*   check
    
    答： 支持。你可以批量导入多个钱包（私钥/JSON），统一执行账户扫描和回收操作。

# Solana Rent Recovery Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Rent Recovery：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/reclaim-rentarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/reclaim-rent)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#steps-to-use)

📝 Steps to Use


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-1.-select-the-operating-wallet-current-or-imported)

1\. Select the operating wallet (current or imported).

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-2.-scan-all-spl-token-nft-accounts-within-the-wallet)

2\. Scan all SPL Token / NFT accounts within the wallet.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-3.-check-the-account-types-to-reclaim)

3\. Check the account types to reclaim:

*   Empty accounts
    
*   Token accounts with balance that can be burned
    
*   NFTs (supports batch processing)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-4.-click-one-click-reclaim-and-sign-to-confirm-the-transaction)

4\. Click \[One-Click Reclaim\] and sign to confirm the transaction.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-5.-after-success-view-the-amount-of-sol-released)

5\. After success, view the amount of SOL released.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FUYWZEnkbHEUAyQWYkhwW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1558c65-2dae-4c00-90b1-6b454aa7f16f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ae3ab686&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-1.-what-is-rent-reclamation-and-why-is-it-necessary)

1\. What is rent reclamation and why is it necessary?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Rent reclamation means closing unused accounts to release the SOL rent paid, reducing account maintenance costs and keeping the wallet organized.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/solana-rent-recovery-tutorial#id-2.-does-burning-tokens-or-nfts-permanently-invalidate-them)

2\. Does burning tokens or NFTs permanently invalidate them?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. Burning permanently destroys the assets and closes the accounts. Please ensure the tokens or NFTs have no further use before proceeding.

# Jito Bundle Tutorial | CiaoTool

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/jito-bundle-tutorial#what-is-the-jito-bundle)

What Is the Jito Bundle ？


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The Jito Bundle is a feature within the Solana blockchain ecosystem designed to enable the efficient execution of multiple transactions.
    
*   By bundling transactions together, it ensures they are processed sequentially and atomically—either all transactions succeed or none do.
    
*   This structure allows traders to leverage opportunities like arbitrage, batching decentralized finance (DeFi) operations, and liquidating positions, among other use cases.
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/jito-bundle-tutorial#key-features-include)

Key features include:


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Sequential Execution**: Transactions are executed in the order specified.
    
2.  **Atomic Execution**: All transactions must succeed; if one fails, none of the bundled transactions are committed to the blockchain.
    
3.  **Prioritization through Tips**: Traders can incentivize validators by tipping them to prioritize their bundles for quicker processing.
    

Simply put, if transaction A and transaction B form a Jito bundle, they will both be executed together on the blockchain. If either transaction A or transaction B fails, neither transaction will be successfully recorded on-chain.

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/jito-bundle-tutorial#how-can-it-support-soltradingbot)

**How Can it Support CiaoTool?**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Jito Bundle provides invaluable support to **CiaoTool** users by offering a suite of features that optimize trading strategies:

*   **Tipping Validators**: With Jito Bundle, traders can prioritize their transactions by tipping validators, ensuring timely execution and maximizing trading opportunities.
    
*   **Transaction Optimization**: By batching DeFi operations and leveraging atomic arbitrage opportunities, traders can efficiently exploit market inefficiencies. For instance, creating liquidity pools and swap tokens can be executed together, preventing sniper arbitrage bots.
    

Incorporating Jito Bundle into the **CiaoTool** toolkit enables traders to navigate the crypto market confidently, efficiently, and swiftly, ensuring a competitive edge in the rapidly evolving digital asset trading landscape.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/jito-bundle-tutorial#learn-more-about-jito-bundle-https-jito-labs.gitbook.io-mev-searcher-resources-bundles)

**Learn more about Jito Bundle:** [https://jito-labs.gitbook.io/mev/searcher-resources/bundlesarrow-up-right](https://jito-labs.gitbook.io/mev/searcher-resources/bundles)

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Blog**: [https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blog)
    
*   **Medium:** [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **YouTube:** [https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp：**[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Batch Collection Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Batch Collection：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/batch-collectionarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/batch-collection)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#how-to-perform-batch-collection-multi-to-one-transfer)

🧩 **How to Perform Batch Collection (Multi To One Transfer) ？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-1.-connect-wallet)

**1\. Connect Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FxUQxUCQ6n0O70Iok5Dhj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc23894f4-b5f9-42c1-867c-13fc0f8fbb2b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9bfc7a3f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-2.-select-token-to-collect)

**2\. Select Token to Collect**

*   Choose the token you want to collect.
    
*   You can either **select from the dropdown list** or **manually paste the token contract address**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F8dXkOc5xNX5w7BCWRtwl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D450361d6-1ae3-42a0-a0ac-48446a3cda6f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed89d873&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-3.-import-source-wallets)

**3\. Import Source Wallets**

**Wallet Import Options:**

*   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**)，or manually paste private keys
    
*   Refresh imported wallet balances
    
*   Set collection amount: **All**, **Fixed Amount**, or **Keep Balance**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZ46in6U6bdnNJYSmxbdc%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8895c87c-d92c-4197-aa14-8a0b691dde34&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f28adb8&sv=2)

*   Batch operations allow you to **remove invalid entries**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FwpOCGbEy6JcdyiUzyjlL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa13842d-849a-42da-a6bb-70d8c9a849eb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7d9c4db&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-4.-set-fee-paying-wallet)

**4\. Set Fee-Paying Wallet**

*   Import the private key of the wallet that will **pay the transaction fees**. Ensure the wallet has sufficient balance.
    
*   All **service fees, gas fees, and Jito tips** will be paid by this **fee-paying wallet**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-5.-set-receiving-wallet)

**5\. Set Receiving Wallet**

*   Enter the **receiving address** for the collected tokens.
    
*   You may also choose the **currently connected wallet**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-6.-confirm-information)

**6\. Confirm Information**

*   After verifying the details, click **“Start Collection”** to complete the operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#successful-operation-case)

☑️ **Successful Operation Case**

*   When the task starts executing, a log pop-up will appear to update the transaction progress in real time.
    
*   After the transaction is successful, a transaction link will be provided, which you can click to view details directly.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FkZCjLy3WOOSMyz4SMsVh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc22b234b-7388-40ac-b9ea-f1118ea0ba7b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=798a2bad&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#failed-operation-case)

❗️Failed Operation Case

*   If any issues arise during the process, we will clearly inform you. No fees will be charged for failed operations.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FE8Fpnok494vjLkMW6iiK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D525ca919-a311-4420-ab33-997d7c5a5810&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1099da9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-1.-what-is-batch-consolidation)

1\. What is batch consolidation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It means transferring tokens from multiple wallets into one main address for easier asset management.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-2.-how-to-import-multiple-source-wallets)

2\. How to import multiple source wallets?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Paste private keys, upload a CSV, or connect local wallets for bulk import.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-3.-what-assets-can-be-consolidated)

3\. What assets can be consolidated?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** SOL and all SPL tokens on Solana, including Token2022 types.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-4.-can-i-set-a-custom-main-address)

4\. Can I set a custom main address?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, you can input any target address or use the connected wallet.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-collection#id-5.-can-i-filter-by-minimum-balance)

5\. Can I filter by minimum balance?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, set a threshold to skip wallets with low balances (e.g., < 1 SOL).

# 「一转多」教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**Base：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**X Layer：**[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**IoTeX：**[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#shi-pin-jiao-cheng)

📹 视频教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#yi-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang-jiao-cheng-onetomany-transfer)

🧾 一对多转账教程（One-to-Many Transfer）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-bang-ding-zhi-chi-bsc-lian-de-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包：绑定支持BSC链的钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FNh1hoNxgVQrp3ioqC92a%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0241f23&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-2.-xuan-ze-bang-ding-qian-bao-qian-bao)

**2\. 选择绑定钱包钱包**

*   可使用当前连接的钱包，或导入其他钱包私钥。
    

circle-info

**自用钱包**：接收钱包地址数量有 200 个限制

**其他钱包**：接收钱包地址数量无限制，可自由添加

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPq0bsgnFDpjfX76aiNhX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18c43c44&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-3.-xuan-ze-jinemo-shi-zhi-chi-xiang-tong-shu-liang-zhuan-zhang-huo-wei-mei-ge-di-zhi-she-zhi-zi-ding)

**3\. 选择金额模式：**支持「相同数量转账」或为每个地址设置「自定义数量」，自定义数量如下图格式。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FMqIfkNNzxhG44ol4ndR3%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2aaa2dd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-4.-shu-ru-dai-bi-di-zhi-xuan-ze-dai-bi-li-ru-busdusdt-huo-shou-dong-shu-ru-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi)

**4\. 输入代币地址：**选择代币（例如 BUSD、USDT），或手动输入代币合约地址。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fl0ln02x60ycvSE9uBjol%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bb67ec7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-5.-tian-jia-jie-shou-di-zhi-ke-shou-dong-nian-tie-huo-shang-chuan-di-zhi-lie-biao-wen-jian-xlsxlsx-g)

**5\. 添加接收地址：**可手动粘贴或上传地址列表文件（xls、xlsx格式）。

1.  **选择相同数量转账，即需要设置相同转账金额** 输入每个接收地址的代币数量，或上传带金额的地址文件。
    
2.  **发送** 确认后签名，一键完成批量发送。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FEfUu9GN5YYKtjFd2ubG4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=268fb47d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-1.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-bu-tong-di-zhi-zhuan-bu-tong-shu-liang)

1\. 是否支持不同地址转不同数量？

*   check
    
    答：支持。可上传自定义金额的 xls、xlsx格式文件，精细控制每笔转账。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-2.-cao-zuo-shi-fou-an-quan)

2\. 操作是否安全？

*   check
    
    答：安全。私钥仅用于本地签名，系统不保存任何钱包数据。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-3.-zhuan-zhang-shi-bai-zen-me-ban)

3\. 转账失败怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请检查地址是否有效、余额是否充足，并适当提高 Gas 限额重试。
