# New Address Buy (↑Makers) Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The New Address Buy (↑Makers) feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

🆚 **Difference Between New Wallet Buys (↑Makers) and New Wallet Buys (↑Holders)**

Type

Main Increase

Focus

**↑ Makers**

Number of active trading addresses

Activity and trading engagement

**↑ Holders**

Number of holding addresses

Distribution consensus and long-term holders

circle-check

**Taking Pump as an example, Pump New Address Buy (↑Makers)：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/newaddr-buyers-markersarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/newaddr-buyers-markers)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#how-to-perform-a-new-address-buy-makers)

🆕 **How to Perform a New Address Buy (↑Makers)**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FMS1BUizmvLMYRGsjZJAu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db53252d8-83c7-43a2-9db4-4513466eeb3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6dbac29&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-2.-open-the-new-address-buy-makers-interface)

**2\. Open the New Address Buy (↑Makers) Interface**

*   Navigate to the **New Address Buy** operation page.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FMPviCmLDgkYi5OkZGmQ2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e1edf0e-a69f-4332-ac67-1390b1e02a61&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19b9b6a5&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

*   **Select Token:** Manually paste the token contract address.
    
*   **Set Number of Buy Addresses:** Up to 1,000 new wallets; can be entered manually.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FHFBj2EoquPUu05hDtLFB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D626f1b8d-a732-4fcb-bf36-aa36ff8cd39d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a7fd459&sv=2)

*   **Set Buy Amount (SOL):** Can set a random range; minimum per address is **0.00001 SOL**.
    
*   **Import Main Wallet Private Key:** Check wallet addresses and balances.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FuSMOl8dypttYdeLxFNMW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6690d26b-7909-4422-a9ee-a87d9e053893&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=711a7591&sv=2)

> 1.  All on-chain fees, SOL account rent (refundable), and platform service fees are paid by the **main wallet**. The estimated total balance is displayed at the bottom—ensure the main wallet has sufficient funds to avoid transaction failure.
>     
> 2.  The payment wallet is the main wallet. If it differs from the connected wallet, the system will deduct fees from the main wallet. If both are the same, simply ensure sufficient balance.
>     
> 3.  SOL account rent per new address: **0.00203928 SOL**.
>     

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-4.-set-jito-mev-tip)

**4\. Set Jito MEV Tip**

*   Choose a recommended route or enter a custom tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FdTYyK0fa5rdTw8dQtBr6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd11b1b26-1720-44fe-bec8-ee8cea0420e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95ff08d3&sv=2)

circle-info

Click **“Start”** to execute the purchase.

triangle-exclamation

⚠️ **Note:**

*   The main cost for a New Address Buy is **transaction fees**.
    
*   Do **not refresh** the page after starting; refreshing will interrupt the service.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#new-address-buy-workflow)

🔗 **New Address Buy Workflow**

circle-info

**For Raydium CPMM and CLMM (Token-2022 tokens):** Be cautious—transfer fees remain in the account state, preventing account closure and rent recovery to the main wallet.

1.  Main wallet transfers SOL to new wallets
    
2.  New wallets purchase the token
    
3.  New wallets transfer tokens back to the main wallet
    
4.  New wallets close token accounts and recover rent
    
5.  Remaining SOL in new wallets is returned to the main wallet
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-1.-what-does-buying-with-new-addresses-mean)

1\. What does buying with new addresses mean?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It means using completely new, unused wallet addresses to perform the first-time purchase, enhancing anonymity and improving chart aesthetics.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-2.-how-to-generate-new-addresses)

2\. How to generate new addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** CiaoTool supports one-click automatic generation of multiple new addresses or manual import of your own clean addresses.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-3.-why-use-new-addresses-instead-of-old-wallets)

3\. Why use new addresses instead of old wallets?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** To avoid carrying over historical labels from old addresses to new charts, preventing bubbles and raising suspicion on the chart.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-4.-can-multiple-new-addresses-be-set-to-buy-simultaneously)

4\. Can multiple new addresses be set to buy simultaneously?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, you can batch-generate and configure up to 12 addresses for dispersed simultaneous purchases.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-markers#id-5.-will-my-private-keys-be-saved)

5\. Will my private keys be saved?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. All signing operations in CiaoTool are completed locally in the browser; private keys are neither uploaded nor stored, ensuring fund security.

# Multi-to-Multi Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Multi-to-Multi**：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/multi-to-multiarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/manage/multi-to-multi)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#how-to-perform-multi-to-multi-transfer)

🧩 **How to Perform Multi-to-Multi Transfer?**

circle-exclamation

⚠️ The number of **sending wallets** must be the same as the number of **recipient wallets**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-1.-connect-wallet)

**1\. Connect Wallet**

*   Click **“Connect Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZelO1E9ScIxLwBWenTli%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D233d5daa-175c-4b33-bbfc-e9fba89b8c90&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8307c7d4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-2.-open-the-multi-to-multi-transfer-page)

**2\. Open the Multi-to-Multi Transfer Page**

*   Import private keys. The system will automatically refresh **SOL balances** and **token balances**.
    
*   Please ensure the wallets contain sufficient **SOL**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-3.-select-token-to-send)

**3\. Select Token to Send**

You can choose to transfer **SOL** or any **token from the current wallet**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F7FtlsVSYk8sRcbQnfQ5i%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2aa61f0f-ac49-4dc6-a7ca-914bd3f6f584&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2dfb1dce&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-4.-import-sending-wallets)

**4\. Import Sending Wallets**

**Wallet Import Options:**

*   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**)，or manually paste private keys
    
*   Refresh imported wallet balances
    
*   Set transfer amounts (**fixed amount or random range**)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F4caPJjJZRpdV4TIZtmQ8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2f6a041b-0866-4433-a98b-4fc6564929e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35533f8e&sv=2)

*   Batch remove wallets with insufficient funds
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fk8i0GcmkN9OgEqvFEJus%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74d846a2-ad86-4840-aab5-44097673096e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=770067d6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-5.-import-recipient-addresses)

**5\. Import Recipient Addresses**

**Address Import Options:**

*   Batch import addresses (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**),or manually paste addresses/private keys
    
*   You can refresh imported wallet balances to **view the receiving amounts for each address**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F7m4FGpRVGOgONFWTno09%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4280ab58-ecd5-4177-9c76-7d5baad0e28f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6b93e92&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-6.-confirm-information)

**6\. Confirm Information**

*   After reviewing the details, click **“Confirm Transfer”** to complete the operation.
    

circle-exclamation

⚠️ **Note:** All transfer fees are paid by the **sending wallets involved in the transaction**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#successful-operation-case)

☑️ **Successful Operation Case**

*   When the task starts executing, a log pop-up will appear to update the transaction progress in real time.
    
*   After the transaction is successful, a transaction link will be provided, which you can click to view details directly.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FhY8LI7HWDhSszclnoYno%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4b0d9f4-39f5-490b-bdd6-2b3f8daca020&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95599eb9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#failed-operation-case)

❗️Failed Operation Case

*   If any issues arise during the process, we will clearly inform you. No fees will be charged for failed operations.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FAqYeeYn7ohWrJVkZpLX2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81da612d-ed9b-44cc-bb04-b884c73feab1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2f1ea523&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-1.-what-is-a-many-to-many-batch-transfer)

1\. What is a many-to-many batch transfer?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It’s a transfer from multiple source wallets to multiple target wallets, ideal for mass fund distribution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-2.-how-to-import-source-and-target-addresses)

2\. How to import source and target addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Upload source addresses with private keys and a target address list via CSV; the system auto-matches and processes transfers.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-3.-can-i-set-different-amounts-for-each-pair)

3\. Can I set different amounts for each pair?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, you can set custom amounts per pair or apply a uniform amount to all.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-4.-is-it-safe-will-my-private-key-be-saved)

4\. Is it safe? Will my private key be saved?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It’s safe. All signing happens locally; your keys are never uploaded or stored.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/multi-to-multi#id-5.-what-is-this-used-for)

5\. What is this used for?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Great for airdrops, payroll, rewards, or mass refunds across many wallets.

# Bonk Launch And Buy Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Bonk** **Launch And Buy：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/letsbonkZone/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/letsbonkZone/launch-and-buy)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#how-to-create-and-buy-on-bonk)

🧩 How to Create and Buy on Bonk？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-1.-connect-your-wallet-phantom-recommended)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet (Phantom Recommended)**

*   Open the **Bonk Create & Buy** interface.
    
*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FrwrIEV6xCqF0r662GXtD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da22504e8-a2ec-4437-8eae-46b39330658c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67f54a81&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-2.-fill-in-basic-token-information)

**2\. Fill in Basic Token Information**

*   You may manually enter token details or click **“Clone”** to copy information from another token.
    
*   Social media links are optional.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F4JiJdrOtR0UFcL1EUMby%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78b104f7-8d5b-471e-b8eb-9f116e5e4011&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b6ab742b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-3.-customize-contract-address)

**3\. Customize Contract Address**

*   Create your personalized token address.
    
*   Paste your pre-generated private key (store it securely).
    
*   The system will deploy the token using this address to ensure the contract matches your expectation.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FYeU3SJNe3sziibTG1oWO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D287cf45b-70f7-4236-8dc3-9f4209775403&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=841313a9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-4.-dev-wallet-settings)

**4\. Dev Wallet Settings**

*   If the dev wallet does **not** set a buy amount, no service fee is charged.
    
*   If it participates in buying, the same service fee as other buy wallets applies.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FqAvoElfLZBllwcp3pp6r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f13e46a-744a-4fea-9395-d62a2bbbc057&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe19a35a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-5.-bundled-buy-wallet-setup-up-to-8-wallets)

**5\. Bundled Buy Wallet Setup (Up to 8 Wallets)**

*   Bundled buy follows a **tiered pricing model**—the more wallets you use, the lower the service fee per wallet.
    
*   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
    
*   Set buy amount: fixed amount / percentage / all (maximum purchasable amount per wallet)
    
*   In addition to service fees, each new address requires **0.00203928 SOL** as account rent.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FINxEUGv37q7QUpsAv2kG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da383b392-82e4-444d-bd8d-4d84f14b4afb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=896f07ce&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note:** Bundled buys may be identified as bots by the platform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-6.-pre-generate-token-contract)

**6\. Pre-Generate Token Contract**

*   Supports generating the token contract address in advance—useful for pre-launch marketing or integrations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F9CAtru4q5As70Ikszuae%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a3dba4f-f246-45d2-b7b5-eceb5401eff5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac47946&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** If you have customized the contract address, there is no need to pre-generate the token contract again.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-7.-jito-tip-settings)

**7\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the **Jito MEV tip** to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority.
    
*   After configuration, click **“Bonk Launch & Buy.”**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F1ylg2iNKFPtS1Rm44txe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58a8fbc4-782a-4563-83c5-c6298b47ae10&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=429adcc1&sv=2)

circle-info

This feature relies on **Jito bundling**. Due to network conditions, Jito nodes, RPC nodes, and block engine factors, the failure rate may be relatively high.

If the operation fails:

*   The launch will not succeed
    
*   No fees will be charged
    

You may try switching RPC nodes or block engines, increasing the Jito tip (**recommended: 0.01 SOL**), or retrying during lower on-chain activity periods.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-8.-process-display)

**8\. Process Display**

*   Once the task begins, a log pop-up will provide real-time progress updates.
    
*   After a successful transaction, you will receive both the **transaction link** and **token link** for direct viewing.
    
*   If any issue occurs at any stage, clear feedback will be provided. **No fees will be charged for failed operations.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-1.-what-is-the-bonk-create-and-buy-feature)

1\. What is the Bonk “Create and Buy” feature?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It’s a one-click tool that allows you to quickly create and automatically buy a new token on Lets Bonk.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-2.-do-i-need-to-connect-a-wallet)

2\. Do I need to connect a wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, you need to connect your Solana wallet and have enough SOL to cover the fees.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-3.-can-i-modify-the-token-information-after-creation)

3\. Can I modify the token information after creation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Once the token is created, key parameters such as name, symbol, and supply cannot be changed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-4.-where-can-i-view-the-purchased-tokens)

4\. Where can I view the purchased tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** After successful creation, the tokens will automatically appear in your wallet, and you can also view them on the Solana block explorer.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-buy#id-5.-do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-use-it)

5\. Do I need coding knowledge to use it?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, the entire process is no-code, making it easy for anyone to quickly launch a token project.

# New Address Buy (↑Holders) Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The New Address Buy (↑Holders) feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

🆚 **Difference Between New Address Buy (↑Makers) and New Address Buy (↑Holders)**

Type

Main Increase

Focus

**↑ Makers**

Number of active trading addresses

Activity and trading engagement

**↑ Holders**

Number of holding addresses

Distribution consensus and long-term holders

circle-check

**Pump New Address Buy (↑Holders)：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/newaddr-buyers-holdersarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/newaddr-buyers-holders)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#how-to-perform-a-new-address-buy-holders)

🆕 **How to Perform a New Address Buy (↑Holders)？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FPdfETMFXCqJvzzQLgvje%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D664f3335-ea0e-4c87-8e07-d959ddef9c27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1c3ba15&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-2.-open-the-new-address-buy-holders-interface)

**2\. Open the New Address Buy (↑Holders) Interface**

*   Navigate to the **New Address Buy** operation page.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FMPviCmLDgkYi5OkZGmQ2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e1edf0e-a69f-4332-ac67-1390b1e02a61&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19b9b6a5&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

*   **Select Token:** Manually paste the token contract address.
    
*   **Set Number of Buy Addresses:** Up to 1,000 new wallets; can be entered manually.
    
*   **Set Buy Amount (SOL):** Can set a random range; minimum per address is **0.00001 SOL**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FnmQfuj3IhjVP90Yfp8Hn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7dbd84e6-ab67-4864-9531-82ce518d4773&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bd9aa76&sv=2)

*   **Import Main Wallet Private Key:** Check wallet addresses and balances.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FuSMOl8dypttYdeLxFNMW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6690d26b-7909-4422-a9ee-a87d9e053893&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=711a7591&sv=2)

> 1.  All on-chain fees and platform service fees generated during the buy are paid by the **main wallet**. The estimated required balance will be shown at the bottom of the page—please ensure the main wallet balance exceeds this amount to avoid transaction failure.
>     
> 2.  The fee-paying wallet is the main wallet, but you must still connect a wallet before using the feature. If the **main wallet** differs from the **connected wallet**, fees will be deducted from the main wallet; if they are the same, simply ensure sufficient balance.
>     

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-4.-set-jito-mev-tip)

**4\. Set Jito MEV Tip**

*   Choose a recommended route or enter a custom tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FdTYyK0fa5rdTw8dQtBr6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd11b1b26-1720-44fe-bec8-ee8cea0420e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=95ff08d3&sv=2)

circle-info

Click **“Start”** to execute the purchase.

triangle-exclamation

⚠️ **Note:**

*   The main cost for a New Address Buy is **transaction fees**.
    
*   Do **not refresh** the page after starting; refreshing will interrupt the service.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-1.-what-is-holders-new-address-buying)

1\. What is “↑Holders” new address buying?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It refers to automatically creating multiple new wallet addresses and executing small real purchases for these addresses after launch, thereby increasing the number of on-chain token holders.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-2.-why-is-increasing-the-number-of-holders-beneficial-for-a-project)

2\. Why is increasing the number of holders beneficial for a project?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** The Pump platform’s ranking algorithm considers “number of token holders” as a key metric for project popularity and ranking; the higher the number, the easier it is to get recommended.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-3.-how-to-batch-create-new-addresses)

3\. How to batch-create new addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** In CiaoTool, click “One-Click Generate Addresses” to quickly create multiple unused new wallet addresses and automatically set them as purchase targets.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-4.-will-these-addresses-actually-complete-transactions)

4\. Will these addresses actually complete transactions?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. The system injects a small amount of SOL into each address and initiates real on-chain purchase operations to ensure transactions are indexed and counted on-chain.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/new-holders#id-5.-can-i-control-the-purchase-amount-and-number-of-addresses)

5\. Can I control the purchase amount and number of addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. You can set the purchase amount per address (e.g., 0.001–0.01 SOL) and the number of addresses to generate, and the system will execute automatically based on your settings.

# Solana 一键冷换仓教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana 一键冷换仓**：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/changeWarehouseZone/one-click-coldChangeWarehousearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/changeWarehouseZone/one-click-coldChangeWarehouse)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#gong-neng-jian-jie)

📁 功能简介

CiaoTool 提供的「**一键冷换仓**」工具，帮助您将持有的代币从指定钱包地址中，**快速迁移至多个新生成地址**，从而：

*   降低单地址持仓比例，分散风险
    
*   防标签、清洗地址历史
    
*   为换仓后钱包提供干净操作起点
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#ru-he-jin-xing-solana-yi-jian-leng-huan-cang)

🔗 如何进行Solana 一键冷换仓？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

1\. 绑定钱包

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FevHAgUU9qr7TNhFK5Lgy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2571739-6619-442e-8f33-2d8ab4659ca1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4d8d854&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-2.-xuan-ze-zhuan-zhang-dai-bi)

2\. 选择转账代币

*   可选择当前连接钱包中的代币，或手动输入代币合约地址。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F7EdRS73P8XD4VM0qDA8m%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46dc14cb-4b48-43e9-9aea-9b6f7b67cdb6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78161fad&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-3.-dao-ru-zhuan-zhang-qian-bao-jiu-di-zhi)

3\. 导入转账钱包（旧地址）

*   批量导入钱包（支持文件类型:Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON），或者手动输入粘贴私钥。
    
*   刷新导入钱包余额，检查SOL的余额是否足够，避免换仓失败。
    
*   设置转账数量（统一输入转账金额；按金额、百分比、保留数量、全部设置）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F8h6cIAru18aK3xy4r0Ty%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da03a3122-586c-4a52-b743-edf578322c28&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88803dd4&sv=2)

*   批量操作删除资金不足的钱包
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FL1wDoYDmTNl30L6VCkOH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4164294-82b2-49a4-a00b-9a5000db1250&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b421d895&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-4.-she-zhi-mei-ge-di-zhi-de-huan-cang-shu-liang)

4\. 设置每个地址的换仓数量

在界面中选择你希望分散到每个地址的代币数量，支持以下快速选项：

*   `1` `4` `40` `100` `200` `自定义数量`
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FoXDAUJ3fMeC0ofZG8D3p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8df47226-ef9d-40b9-a0a2-52fe1d764748&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f70cca6d&sv=2)

circle-info

举例：如果你导入了一个持有 1000 枚代币的钱包，并选择每个地址分配 10 枚，系统将自动生成 100 个地址来接收资产。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-5.-sheng-cheng-mu-biao-jie-shou-di-zhi-xin-qian-bao)

5\. 生成目标接收地址（新钱包）

*   点击【**生成钱包**】，系统会自动创建所需数量的新地址，作为换仓目标地址。所有钱包密钥将在本地生成，并可导出备份。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-6.-she-zhi-jito-mev-xiao-fei)

6\. **设置Jito MEV 小费**

*   选择适合的线路或自定义金额。
    

circle-info

注：所有转账的手续费均由当前转账的钱包支付，包括平台费用。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FEOsYWWREwlxP9DNr4t6i%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81b48ca8-bea8-443f-94fc-105b70f8d63e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7e67ad5&sv=2)

*   点击下方 **确认转账** 按钮即可完成操作。
    
*   费用概览：**例：**转账钱包数\*换仓钱包数\*0.0001875 SOL+ Gas费+Jito费
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fv01mXpe3JUVryehmp0iE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daccd52f2-8a8f-43cc-ab79-daf7e7b3eef2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=91acb54a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-1.-yi-jian-leng-huan-cang-de-zuo-yong-shi-shen-me)

1\. 一键冷换仓的作用是什么？

*   check
    
    答： 冷换仓可将代币从当前地址分散转移至大量新地址，降低单一地址持仓比例，优化链上分布结构，增强项目安全性和隐蔽性。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-2.-wei-shen-me-huan-cang-hou-yao-shi-yong-xin-sheng-cheng-de-qian-bao-di-zhi)

2\. 为什么换仓后要使用新生成的钱包地址？

*   check
    
    答： 新地址无历史交易记录，可避免被链上工具标记为“关联钱包”，更适合用于策略重建和分散操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-3.-huan-cang-guo-cheng-zhong-shi-fou-hui-xie-lou-si-yao)

3\. 换仓过程中是否会泄露私钥？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。CiaoTool 所有交易均在本地浏览器完成签名，**不会上传或存储私钥**，确保资产安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-4.-shi-fou-ke-yi-zi-ding-yi-huan-cang-di-zhi-he-zhuan-zhang-jine)

4\. 是否可以自定义换仓地址和转账金额？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可以选择系统自动生成钱包，也可以上传自定义地址列表；每笔转账金额可选固定值或输入自定义数量。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/fragmentation/solana#id-5.-huan-cang-guo-cheng-zhong-wang-luo-zhong-duan-hui-ying-xiang-cao-zuo-ma)

5\. 换仓过程中网络中断会影响操作吗？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。CiaoTool 支持断点恢复机制，系统会在中断后记录未完成的地址，并允许你重新发起剩余部分的换仓任务。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Market Making Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The Market Making feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

circle-check

**Here, using Pump as an example, Pump Market Making：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/market-makingarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/market-making)

circle-info

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#how-to-perform-market-making)

🧩 **How to Perform Market Making?**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#swap-settings)

**Swap Settings**

**Value Token:**

*   **Pump, PumpSwap, Bonk, and Meteora** currently support **Solana only**
    
*   **Bonk-USD1** supports **World Liberty Financial USD**
    
*   **Raydium** supports **Solana, USDT, and USD Coin**
    

**Market-Making Token:** You can select a token from the connected wallet or manually enter the token contract address to proceed.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F3fv2kuDJohrYoBUlm5nM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd20d3ec-5e99-4369-8e03-f5cd386f7f8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a081921e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#market-making-bot-settings)

🤖 **Market Making Settings**

circle-check

**Three operational modes are available:** Pull Up，Drop and Traffic Bot

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-1.-pull-up-continuously-executes-buy-orders)

**1\.** Pull Up：Continuously executes buy orders.

**Single Transaction Volume:** The buy size per transaction. If the min and max values are the same, the amount is fixed; if different, the amount is randomized within the range.

**Condition Parameters:** Includes **Target Price**, **Total Maximum Transaction Amount**, and **Duration(Minutes)**.

*   If none are set → the task runs continuously
    
*   If any is set → the task stops automatically once the condition is met
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FrdVKvacfM35vOAQxssIa%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc87ee80-f3bd-4d1d-b675-7479bca7344d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7040fe07&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-2.-drop-continuously-executes-sell-orders)

**2\. Drop:** Continuously executes sell orders.

**Single Transaction Volume:** The token sell size per transaction. If the min and max values are the same, the amount is fixed; if different, the amount is randomized within the range.

**Condition Parameters:** Includes **Target Price**, **Total Maximum Transaction Amount**, and **Duration(Minutes)**.

*   If none are set → the task runs continuously
    
*   If any is set → the task stops automatically once the condition is met
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FCnHKnae9VIR1v6myV9iG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62ebf320-7bfd-421a-816f-aff23bbde3f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9b6fcdb1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-3.-traffic-bot-continuously-executes-random-buy-and-sell-actions)

**3\.** Traffic Bot**:** Continuously executes **random buy and sell** actions.

**Single Transaction Volume:** The token amount per buy or sell. If the min and max values are the same, the amount is fixed; if different, the amount is randomized within the range.

**Condition Parameters:** Includes **Max Cumulative Volume (SOL)**, and **Duration(Minutes)**.

*   If none are set → the task runs continuously
    
*   If any is set → the task stops automatically once the condition is met
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F1TYb1dKlu9GJLu3YETqf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b6d1bb2-d49b-450b-ab83-e861e24f0c01&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9be43eb0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#general-settings)

⚙️ **General Settings**

*   **Task Execution Interval:** The interval between transactions executed by each wallet. To ensure a high success rate, the minimum interval must currently be set to at least **5 seconds**.
    
*   **Slippage Setting:** For small transaction amounts requiring fast execution, select **Auto**.
    
*   **Jito EVM Fee:**
    
    *   Jito is an alternative Solana transaction packaging service provider. The higher the Jito fee, the faster the transaction is confirmed on the blockchain.
        
    *   For lower transaction costs or if Jito mode has a low success rate, you can set the Jito fee to **0** and opt for standard transaction routes to retry.
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FLcGIIxds5szSKXux8sr3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D466a31d6-7fc4-428b-9a06-cebe5496e723&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a8ad363&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#wallet-settings)

🔐 **Wallet Settings**

*   **Import Private Keys:** You can manually input private keys (used only for local signing) or select them from batch wallet management (stored locally with encryption). After importing, wallets will be automatically selected, and balances will refresh automatically. You can manually adjust the wallets to operate.
    
*   **Real-Time Statistics:** During task execution, transaction results are updated in real-time, and wallet balances are refreshed continuously.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FuX7wGb60Ekllcg1wAxlg%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38559019-650f-4236-a899-014ce17c0056&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d928fe2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#transaction-logs)

📜 **Transaction Logs**

*   The entire process logs transaction details in real-time.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FPzxKkjEjT9oo0k2e4HFn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f444498-0306-4583-867f-e13ea454e9f0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a6c5f2ba&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-1.-what-is-market-cap-management)

1\. What is market cap management?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Market cap management involves maintaining the token’s market price and performance through strategic buying, selling, and trade control to avoid abnormal fluctuations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-2.-why-is-market-cap-management-important)

2\. Why is market cap management important?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It prevents extreme price spikes or drops during the early phase of a project, helping keep charts stable and boosting investor confidence.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-3.-how-can-new-addresses-be-used-in-market-cap-management)

3\. How can new addresses be used in market cap management?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** By rotating buys or sells across multiple addresses, you create **real but distributed trading activity**, reducing the risk of detection.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-4.-can-market-cap-operations-be-executed-in-bulk)

4\. Can market cap operations be executed in bulk?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes — with **CiaoTool's batch trading and address distribution tools**, fine-grained market cap control can be executed efficiently.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/market-making#id-5.-does-market-cap-management-involve-illegal-or-manipulative-behavior)

5\. Does market cap management involve illegal or manipulative behavior?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** As long as the goal is to **stabilize early chart performance** without misleading users, it's considered strategic control, not market manipulation.

# 「多转多」教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC多对多转账**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**Base多对多转账：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**X Layer多对多转账：**[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**IoTeX多对多转账：**[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 **操作步骤**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-1.-xuan-ze-dai-bi-di-zhi)

**1\. 选择代币地址**

*   输入或选择需要发送的代币合约地址。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FgD5FEZlKcauwwpyIKuFn%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50da0a89&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-2.-shang-chuan-fa-song-si-yao)

**2\. 上传发送私钥**

*   上传包含多个私钥的钱包文件（xls、xlsx格式），系统将识别来源钱包。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FEF41y8aHvR2FeHCoTBXK%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c601e0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-3.-shang-chuan-jie-shou-di-zhi)

**3\. 上传接收地址**

*   上传接收地址列表，确保发送方和接收方数量一致（如10个地址发给10个接收地址）。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FHeK6LGgnDpFDh5LgIX2U%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=468a9ea6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-4.-she-zhi-zhuan-zhang-can-shu)

**4\. 设置转账参数**

1.  全部数量
    
2.  固定数量
    
3.  固定留存
    
4.  自定义(点击输入)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FIAdK1T4tsHPkiJ0bjGVB%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ff51f52&sv=2)

*   自定义输入转账数量可上传文件或手动换行输入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FW2qhRAwRxX26i9mAYugV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d618ff8d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-5.-zhi-xing-pi-liang-zhuan-zhang)

**5\. 执行批量转账**

*   一键确认操作并签名，系统将自动完成所有多对多交易。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang)

**1\. 什么是多对多转账？**

*   check
    
    答：指多个发送地址向多个接收地址批量发送代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-2.-mei-ge-di-zhi-ke-yi-she-zhi-bu-tong-jinema)

**2\. 每个地址可以设置不同金额吗？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可在上传文件中自定义每笔交易的金额。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-3.-xi-tong-shi-fou-bao-cun-wo-de-si-yao)

**3\. 系统是否保存我的私钥？**

*   check
    
    答：不会。所有签名操作仅在本地浏览器完成，保障私钥安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-4.-zhi-chi-duo-shao-zu-di-zhi-jin-xing-zhuan-zhang)

**4\. 支持多少组地址进行转账？**

*   check
    
    答：没有数量限制，适合中大型批量操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-5.-shi-fou-ke-yi-dao-ru-xlsxlsx-ge-shi-wen-jian)

**5\. 是否可以导入** xls、xlsx格式**文件？**

*   check
    
    答：可以。发送私钥和接收地址都支持xls、xlsx格式导入，提高效率。

# Solana Fragmentation Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Fragmentation**：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/changeWarehouseZone/one-click-coldChangeWarehousearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/changeWarehouseZone/one-click-coldChangeWarehouse)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/fragmentation/solana#feature-overview)

📁 Feature Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CiaoTool’s **One-Click Cold Change Warehouse** tool helps you quickly redistribute tokens from a designated wallet to multiple newly generated addresses in order to:

*   Reduce holding concentration and distribute risk
    
*   Prevent tagging, and clean wallet history
    
*   Provide clean starting points for post-reallocation wallets
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/fragmentation/solana#solana-fragmentation-steps)

🔗 Solana Fragmentation Steps


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Step 1: Select the token to reallocate** From the token list, choose the Solana token you want to distribute (SPL or Token2022). The system will automatically detect your token balance.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fd4EtWnaBdgikrUnGBBcd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5efb797-33e8-4445-ae25-5f309d643309&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d03d7d23&sv=2)

**Step 2: Import the source wallets (Old Address)** Import the wallets holding the token using one of the following:

*   Manually input private keys
    
*   Upload a CSV file (format: address, private key)
    
*   Paste JSON content (multiple wallets)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F9YKI3cKj8z4JRDUCTB8h%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da48ab5d6-c00f-4825-b3fd-f1878178cde4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=807e1757&sv=2)

Only wallets with token balances will be included in the reallocation.

**Step 3: Set the amount per destination address** Choose how much of the token each new wallet should receive. Quick presets available:

`1 4 40 100 200` or **Custom value**

circle-info

**Example:** If a wallet holds 1000 tokens and you select “10 per address,” 100 new addresses will be generated.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fiqgy4BzDTJ3xFCt3Jj3z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D16bfe716-ca1f-4d21-9246-73542b431c39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a03b943b&sv=2)

**Step 4: Generate target addresses (new wallets)** Click **Generate Wallets** to create the exact number of required addresses. All private keys are generated locally and can be exported as a backup.

Alternatively, use **"Upload Address List"** or **"Paste Addresses"** if you have pre-generated wallets.

**Step 5: Confirm & Execute** After previewing total transactions and address distribution:

*   Click **"Start Reallocation"**
    
*   Tokens will be transferred in batches
    
*   Real-time transaction status will be displayed
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fb19ti0b7qrkGgBCnTWkL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db5947acb-9666-43eb-849c-e47e1997f644&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ecb1aee&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/fragmentation/solana#export-results-optional)

📁 Export Results (Optional)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can export a CSV file containing the new addresses and their balances for later management or recovery.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/fragmentation/solana#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

**1\. What is the purpose of Fragmentation?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Cold reallocation spreads tokens from a single address across multiple new ones, improving token distribution and reducing on-chain centralization risk.
    

**2\. Why use new wallet addresses for reallocation?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Fresh wallets have no transaction history, reducing the risk of chain wallet labeling. Ideal for clean strategic resets.
    

**3\. Are private keys exposed during this process?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. All signing is done locally in your browser. CiaoTool does not upload or store your keys.
    

**4\. Can I customize target addresses and transfer amounts?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. You can either auto-generate wallets or upload your own list. Transfer amounts can be fixed or customized per transaction.
    

**5\. What happens if the network connection is interrupted?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** CiaoTool supports recovery. Unfinished addresses are recorded and you can resume the reallocation at any time.

# SOL 中转转账教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**SOL 中转转账：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/relay-transferarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/wallet/manage/relay-transfer)

复制

    注意：转出钱包数量需要和目标钱包数量一致！
    中转转账仅支持 SOL 转账。开启转账前请务必保存好已生成的中转地址信息。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#ru-he-jin-xing-zhong-zhuan-zhuan-zhang)

🧩 **如何进行**中转转账？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FIo3dELFLz4B23XpNTxNK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9545a6f2-9171-46f1-b64c-dda95b32150a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a9f6a2df&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-2.-xuan-ze-zhuan-zhang-dai-bi)

2\. 选择转账代币

*   中转转账仅支持 SOL 转账
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FjXxRvNl2TVObVLHprF6r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D393fa7af-0445-4ad6-bf8c-51518ea3a0dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f04efa15&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-3.-xuan-ze-zhuan-zhang-qian-bao)

3\. 选择转账钱包

*   可选择手动粘贴多个私钥（支持多个钱包）
    
*   上传包含私钥的 `Excel/CSV/TXT/JSON` 文件。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fzf758qK8ddYKK3Rm6yos%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddc763410-c1f5-4305-9204-532aabe1bd48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbb71d54&sv=2)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F77oO2zGR2kL0f5jUUUt7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De2946727-0383-4297-a217-55cf086b6e39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16da077c&sv=2)

circle-info

注意：确保转出钱包有足够的SOL

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-4.-xuan-ze-jie-shou-di-zhi)

4\. 选择接收地址

*   输入目标钱包地址（数量必须与转出钱包一致）。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fxss0zJZwt1zHc7HD3m5I%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9ee835a6-08da-4537-991f-b52f7e281e4d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=93e6c2ae&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-5.-mei-ge-di-zhi-zhong-zhuan-shu-liang)

5\. 每个地址中转数量

*   选择分配方式：每个地址中转数量
    
    *   固定值（如每个地址 1/4/10 ）
        
    *   或自定义填写地址中转数量。
        
    
    ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F4FG0xqcMxOQZOgyQQP09%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D77be444a-6801-480e-af3e-2808f2429c6b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=52934625&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-6.-sheng-cheng-zhong-zhuan-qian-bao)

6\. 生成中转钱包

*   系统自动生成中间跳转地址，用于中转操作（隐藏转账路径）。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-7.-que-ren-zhuan-zhang)

7\. 确认转账

*   核对信息无误后，点击「确认转账」
    
*   系统将依次执行中转逻辑，完成资金分发。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FGAd61nWEQhd4OlDR72IG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1d964520-8861-4db4-8588-05e2d43f6b3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b3a962e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-1.-zhong-zhuan-zhuan-zhang-he-pu-tong-zhuan-zhang-you-he-qu-bie)

1\. 中转转账和普通转账有何区别？

*   check
    
    答： 中转转账通过在发送者和接收者之间插入一组中间钱包，实现多条转账路径，从而提升隐私性，防止链上追踪。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-2.-wei-shen-me-zhuan-chu-di-zhi-shu-liang-bi-xu-he-jie-shou-di-zhi-shu-liang-yi-zhi)

2\. 为什么转出地址数量必须和接收地址数量一致？

*   check
    
    答： 每一个转出地址将映射至一个目标地址，保持一一对应关系是确保资金精确分发和逻辑正确执行的关键。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-3.-wo-xu-yao-wei-mei-ge-zhong-zhuan-qian-bao-dan-du-zhun-bei-sol-ma)

3\. 我需要为每个中转钱包单独准备SOL吗？

*   check
    
    答： 不需要，系统自动生成中转钱包并执行转账，但你的手续费钱包需预留足够 SOL 用于支付每一笔转账的手续费。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/wallet-manage/relay-transfer#id-4.-zhong-zhuan-guo-cheng-an-quan-ma-wo-neng-kong-zhi-zhong-zhuan-qian-bao-ma)

4\. 中转过程安全吗？我能控制中转钱包吗？

*   check
    
    答： 所有中转钱包私钥将提供给用户保存，整个过程在本地或可信环境中执行，CiaoTool 不保留用户密钥，确保安全可控。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Token 流动性该如何配置？ | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana 发币：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/create)

**Pump：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buy)

**Base 发币：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#wei-shen-me-liu-dong-xing-hen-guan-jian)

📈 为什么流动性很关键？

*   **交易顺畅度：**流动性直接影响滑点大小。流动性越低，单笔交易对价格的冲击越大，交易越不顺畅。
    
*   **价格稳定性：**更高的流动性能有效吸收买卖波动，提升价格稳定性，但同时也会带来更高的资金占用成本。
    
*   **操纵风险与匹配度**：流动性不足时，池子更容易被操纵；但流动性并非越多越好，过高的流动性还会放大潜在的无常损失。关键在于流动性配置是否与项目所处阶段相匹配。
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#xian-que-ding-ni-de-liu-dong-xing-deng-ji)

📊 先确定你的流动性等级

无论在哪条链上发币，你都需要先判断项目所处的流动性等级，这会直接影响投资者预期和价格行为。

*   **极低流动性：**实验性项目或低成本 Meme，滑点高，极易被 bot 操纵。
    
*   **低流动性：**初期项目，有少量社区，但价格仍不稳定。
    
*   **中等流动性：**已有一定用户和交易频率，价格相对可控。
    
*   **高流动性**：成熟项目阶段，市场信任度明显提升。
    
*   **极高流动性：**资金雄厚或已验证成功的项目，几乎不易被操纵。
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#bu-tong-qu-kuai-lian-de-liu-dong-xing-can-kao-qu-jian)

🔗 不同区块链的流动性参考区间

*   下表基于实际市场情况整理，用于帮助你快速定位合理区间（非硬性标准）：
    

流动性等级

Solana (Raydium)

Solana (PumpSwap)

BSC (BNB)

Base

极低

1 – 100 SOL

1 – 25 SOL

0.15 – 15 BNB

0.1 – 5 WETH

低

101 – 500 SOL

26 – 125 SOL

15 – 75 BNB

6 – 25 WETH

中等

501 – 2,000 SOL

126 – 500 SOL

75 – 300 BNB

26 – 100 WETH

高

2,001 – 10,000 SOL

501 – 2,500 SOL

300 – 1,500 BNB

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FtLGXpKtBfoP1NuxWA1bj%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=261b0d5d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#liu-dong-xing-bu-zu-hui-dai-lai-na-xie-zhi-jie-wen-ti)

⚠️ 流动性不足会带来哪些直接问题？

*   **流动性不足的影响：**当流动性不足时，滑点会被显著放大，直接影响交易体验；同时，池子也更容易成为 bot 抢跑和拉砸的目标，增加市场风险。
    
*   **流动性管理的必要性：**即便通过提高流动性可以在一定程度上缓解上述问题，仍需关注无常损失，尤其是在价格波动剧烈的阶段。因此，流动性需要进行动态管理，而不是一次性投入。
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#shi-fou-ying-gai-ba-quan-bu-token-dou-fang-jin-chi-zi)

🔎 是否应该把全部 Token 都放进池子？

*   通常不建议。更合理的做法是将 **40%–70%** 的 Token 用于流动性，其余部分留作**质押激励、生态奖励、社区运营或未来空投。**
    
*   这种结构既能保证交易深度，也能为项目后续发展保留空间。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fu4ZWnh1DG4rsIgk00oDW%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66854c8d&sv=2)

Token Allocation 示例

* * *

流动性是 Token 的基础设施。在不同公链上，区间虽有差异，但核心逻辑一致：

> 足够的流动性 = 更稳定的价格 + 更高的市场信任 + 更低的操纵风险

提前规划流动性等级与 Token 分配，是避免项目在早期阶段“死在起跑线”的关键一步。

* * *

# Pump Bundled Buy and Snipe Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump Bundled Buy and Snipe：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/snipe/bundled-buy-snipearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/snipe/bundled-buy-snipe)

*   Bundling supports a single address, but for single-address operations, it is recommended to use the Market Making feature instead.
    
*   When performing bundled buys or sells, do not leave blank lines between addresses, as this will trigger an error.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#how-to-pump-launch-to-bundled-buy-and-snipe)

🧩 **How to** Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe**？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-connect-your-wallet-phantom-recommended)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet (Phantom Recommended)**

*   Open the **Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe** interface.
    
*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FokVYrE18cr2FMknQeTme%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc58c86e3-d452-4e50-aede-134bc286611b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f66987b0&sv=2)

circle-info

_Make sure you have enough SOL to cover estimated purchase costs._

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-select-token)

**2\.** Select Token

*   Enter or paste the token address of the upcoming project on Pump.fun.
    
*   The system will automatically fetch the bonding curve information. (It is recommended to prepare sufficient SOL balance to meet the estimated purchase amount.)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FwtwykQOUq485pUS0Fu0h%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc6d35d2-c764-4326-ad7d-5cf04e1cdadb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=16316373&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-bundled-buy-wallet-setup-up-to-12-wallets)

**3\.** Bundled Buy Wallet Setup (Up to 12 Wallets)

You can import bundled wallets in three ways:

*   **Manual Input:** Paste private keys one by one.
    
*   **Upload File:** Batch import private keys via **CSV / JSON**.
    
*   **Auto-Generate:** Use CiaoTool to generate wallet addresses with one click (remember to securely back up the private keys).
    

💡 **Tip:** The more wallets you use, the higher the chance of successful sniping. Ensure sufficient SOL allocation across wallets. In addition to service fees, each new address requires **0.00203928 SOL** as account rent.

circle-exclamation

Make sure buy wallets have enough funds and gas to avoid failed transactions. A maximum of **12 wallets** can participate simultaneously.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FD6e7xxHjchYD12CPt5a9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D013825cb-8b1e-4606-a0a6-13becf18fe48&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e2e5d91&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-swap-buy-wallet)

**4\. Swap Buy Wallet**

*   This wallet will be used for subsequent swap operations. Setup method:
    
*   Import the private key
    
*   Enter the estimated amount of SOL to be used by this wallet (_the actual buy amount depends on the selected purchase ratio_)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FCiGeGN3PSuSPOItutp63%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9a4822ed-7ad7-4e63-a53a-8c1dd7df67a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aacda32a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-jito-tip-settings)

**5\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the Jito MEV tip to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority in block ordering.
    
*   After configuration, click **“Pump Bundled Buy and Snipe.”**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FCUwK5JLaqHt5sC8LwxIG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dba281e88-bc56-4281-a5ef-4c031f810e7c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54d070a3&sv=2)

> ⚠️ _Jito tip is charged only once—not per address._

circle-info

*   Ensure every wallet has enough SOL for purchases and fees
    
*   All transactions are signed locally in-browser; **CiaoTool never uploads or stores your private keys**
    
*   Bundled buys improve speed, but can still face slippage in volatile markets—adjust slippage tolerance accordingly
    
*   If network congestion or failure occurs, you can retry or refresh the task
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-what-is-a-bundled-buy-wallet-group)

1\. **What is a Bundled Buy Wallet Group?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** A set of up to 16 wallets that execute a buy in a single bundled transaction at the Pump.fun launch, reducing the risk of being front-run.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-what-is-the-purpose-of-the-swap-buy-wallet)

2\. **What is the purpose of the Swap Buy Wallet?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** This wallet is used for post-launch buy operations—ideal for market-making, re-entry, or liquidity control.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-is-setting-jito-mev-tips-required)

3\. **Is setting Jito MEV tips required?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Not required but highly recommended. Jito boosts priority in transaction sorting pools—critical for beating bots.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-will-ciaotool-upload-or-store-my-private-keys)

4\. **Will CiaoTool upload or store my private keys?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Never. All keys are handled locally for signing and are never transmitted or saved by the platform.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-what-if-the-bundled-buy-fails)

5\. **What if the bundled buy fails?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Your SOL stays in your wallet. You can retry the transaction and tweak slippage or Jito tip settings to improve success.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/bundled-buy-snipe#need-help-contact-us-anytime)

💬 Need Help? Contact Us Anytime

*   **Telegram:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)
    
*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Blog**: [https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blog)
