# Bonk-USD1 Launch And Buy Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Bonk** **Launch And Buy：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/letsbonkZone/USD1/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/letsbonkZone/USD1/launch-and-buy)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#how-to-create-and-buy-on-bonk-usd1)

🧩 How to Create and Buy on Bonk USD1？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-1.-connect-your-wallet-phantom-recommended)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet (Phantom Recommended)**

*   Open the **Bonk USD1 Create & Buy** interface.
    
*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FrwrIEV6xCqF0r662GXtD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da22504e8-a2ec-4437-8eae-46b39330658c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67f54a81&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-2.-fill-in-basic-token-information)

**2\. Fill in Basic Token Information**

*   You may manually enter token details or click **“Clone”** to copy information from another token.
    
*   **Social media links are optional.**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FIv239catv6Q2Wx35n9io%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0418bb07-bff6-484f-939a-dd1ccfcd95a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1beb478d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-3.-customize-contract-address)

**3\. Customize Contract Address**

*   Create your personalized token address.
    
*   Paste your pre-generated private key (store it securely).
    
*   The system will deploy the token using this address to ensure the contract matches your expectation.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FYeU3SJNe3sziibTG1oWO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D287cf45b-70f7-4236-8dc3-9f4209775403&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=841313a9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-4.-dev-wallet-settings)

**4\. Dev Wallet Settings**

*   If the dev wallet does **not** set a buy amount, no service fee is charged.
    
*   If it participates in buying, the same service fee as other buy wallets applies.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FqAvoElfLZBllwcp3pp6r%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f13e46a-744a-4fea-9395-d62a2bbbc057&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fe19a35a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-5.-bundled-buy-wallet-setup-up-to-8-wallets)

**5\. Bundled Buy Wallet Setup (Up to 8 Wallets)**

*   Bundled buy follows a **tiered pricing model**—the more wallets you use, the lower the service fee per wallet.
    
*   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
    
*   Set buy amount: fixed amount / percentage / all (maximum purchasable amount per wallet)
    
*   In addition to service fees, each new address requires **0.00203928 SOL** as account rent.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FINxEUGv37q7QUpsAv2kG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da383b392-82e4-444d-bd8d-4d84f14b4afb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=896f07ce&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note:** Bundled buys may be identified as bots by the platform.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-6.-pre-generate-token-contract)

**6\. Pre-Generate Token Contract**

*   Supports generating the token contract address in advance—useful for pre-launch marketing or integrations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F9CAtru4q5As70Ikszuae%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a3dba4f-f246-45d2-b7b5-eceb5401eff5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac47946&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** If you have customized the contract address, there is no need to pre-generate the token contract again.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-7.-jito-tip-settings)

**7\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the **Jito MEV tip** to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority.
    
*   After configuration, click **“Bonk USD1** **Launch & Buy.”**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FFb4V8kyleV2rkS7Wjdpn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50b17b38-94eb-4f07-adf4-6d4692612430&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=421baa62&sv=2)

circle-info

This feature relies on **Jito bundling**. Due to network conditions, Jito nodes, RPC nodes, and block engine factors, the failure rate may be relatively high.

If the operation fails:

*   The launch will not succeed
    
*   No fees will be charged
    

You may try switching RPC nodes or block engines, increasing the Jito tip (**recommended: 0.01 SOL**), or retrying during lower on-chain activity periods.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-8.-process-display)

**8\. Process Display**

*   Once the task begins, a log pop-up will provide real-time progress updates.
    
*   After a successful transaction, you will receive both the **transaction link** and **token link** for direct viewing.
    
*   If any issue occurs at any stage, clear feedback will be provided. **No fees will be charged for failed operations.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-1.-what-is-the-bonk-usd1-create-and-buy-feature)

1\. What is the Bonk-USD1 “Create and Buy” feature?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It’s a one-click tool that allows you to quickly create and automatically buy a new token on Lets Bonk-USD1.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-2.-do-i-need-to-connect-a-wallet)

2\. Do I need to connect a wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, you need to connect your Solana wallet and have enough SOL to cover the fees.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-3.-can-i-modify-the-token-information-after-creation)

3\. Can I modify the token information after creation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Once the token is created, key parameters such as name, symbol, and supply cannot be changed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-4.-where-can-i-view-the-purchased-tokens)

4\. Where can I view the purchased tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** After successful creation, the tokens will automatically appear in your wallet, and you can also view them on the Solana block explorer.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/usd1-launch-buy#id-5.-do-i-need-coding-knowledge-to-use-it)

5\. Do I need coding knowledge to use it?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, the entire process is no-code, making it easy for anyone to quickly launch a token project.

# Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe**：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/snipe/launch-buy-snipearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/snipe/launch-buy-snipe)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning by video, check out this tutorial for a step-by-step guide on how to buy at launch and snipe on Solana.

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#how-to-pump-launch-to-bundled-buy-and-snipe)

🧩 **How to** Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe**？**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-connect-your-wallet-phantom-recommended)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet (Phantom Recommended)**

*   Open the **Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe** interface.
    
*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F5XYqYQG7Gvz6QYWzUWSj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e39ebf0-39ba-47af-bab3-e699d9db5575&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=506db133&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-fill-in-basic-token-information)

**2\. Fill in Basic Token Information**

*   You may manually enter token details or click **“Clone”** to copy information from another token.
    
*   Click **\[Show more options\]** to add website and other contact information.
    
*   You can set **auto-sell all tokens when price increases by X%**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F7xEeNH2e4AJKxAiKrNoy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debfafd62-afd4-4438-a2d7-d251dcc1dd16&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4884a46f&sv=2)

circle-info

If auto-sell is enabled, it is recommended **not to use the dev wallet for buying**, or provide the dev wallet’s private key below to participate. Otherwise, manual signature may be required during selling, which could cause delays.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-custom-contract-address)

**3\. Custom Contract Address**

**Two Methods for Setting Custom Contract Addresses：**

1.  Create a personalized token address and choose whether it ends with **“pump”**.
    
    *   Check ☑️ **pump** and confirm in your wallet
        
    
2.  Select **“Import Private Key”**
    
    *   Paste your pre-generated private key (**The address must be a new one that has never paid SOL rent**)**.**
        
    *   The system will deploy the token using this address, ensuring the contract matches your expectation.
        
    

circle-exclamation

**Note:** Selecting either option will immediately require wallet signature and payment of the platform fee (0.01 SOL).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fmzpnj1NT3bmQGUqWFySH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19af14a6-55f6-4273-bf41-a7de593a2184&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c70aee3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-dev-wallet-settings)

**4\. Dev Wallet Settings**

*   If the dev wallet does **not** set a buy amount, no service fee is charged.
    
*   If it participates in buying, the same service fee as other buy wallets applies.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FwKkF79cUF43v8JztdiRC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41db5a10-1c61-409f-88e9-c59ee787abd8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa1b2424&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-bundled-buy-wallet-settings)

**5\. Bundled Buy Wallet Settings**

*   Bundled buy uses a **tiered pricing model**—the more wallets you add, the lower the service fee per wallet.
    
*   **Batch import wallets** (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
    
*   **Set buy amount:** fixed amount / percentage / all (maximum purchasable amount per wallet)
    
*   In addition to service fees, each new address requires **0.00203928 SOL** as account rent.
    

circle-exclamation

For **Pump.fun Launch and Bundled Buy,** ensure buy wallets have sufficient funds and gas to avoid failure. Maximum **9 wallets** can participate simultaneously.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FURyjUwIY2E21jJwzmYuS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fa11be0-886d-486f-9040-a108cb301f32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60780083&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note:** This might be detected by Pump as bot behavior.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-6.-swap-buy-wallet)

**6\. Swap Buy Wallet：**

This wallet will be used for subsequent swap operations. Setup method:

*   Import the private key
    
*   Enter the estimated amount of SOL to be used by this wallet (_the actual buy amount depends on the selected purchase ratio_)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F9WdPvmzAQjf57dBp9fqC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd97630f-04b7-4c4b-9e6c-b40081ba08d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc360b83&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-7.-pre-generate-token-contract)

**7\. Pre-Generate Token Contract**

Supports generating the contract address in advance—useful for pre-launch marketing or integrations.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FPipqMSsubVBZQuH9xiM8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f82e4b9-f5c0-418b-bda1-32350f1e1aef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4189f76&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-8.-jito-tip-settings)

**8\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the Jito MEV tip to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority in block ordering.
    
*   After configuration, click **“Pump Launch and Buy Snipe.”**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FzzfO5BjuWHuME9ae9oTu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ab0affb-ec60-4f81-b84a-b29af852b774&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9c7f11f&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

This feature relies on **Jito bundling**. Due to network conditions, Jito nodes, RPC nodes, and block engine factors, the failure rate may be relatively high.

If the operation fails:

*   The launch will not succeed
    
*   No fees will be charged
    

You may try switching RPC nodes or block engines, increasing the Jito tip (**recommended: 0.01 SOL**), or retrying during lower on-chain activity periods.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-8.-process-display)

8\. Process Display

*   Once the task starts, a log pop-up will display real-time progress updates.
    
*   After a successful transaction, you will receive both the **transaction link** and **token link** for direct viewing.
    
*   If any issue occurs at any stage, clear feedback will be provided. No fees will be charged for failed operations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fz3wWK61c5hIYKRqOunzD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc1576d6-68ea-42a4-b010-1b219b0f747e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ab158eb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-what-is-a-bundled-buy-wallet)

1\. What is a Bundled Buy Wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** This is a group of wallets used to simultaneously execute buy transactions at the moment a Pump project launches. You can set up to 12 wallets.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-whats-the-difference-between-a-dev-wallet-and-a-swap-wallet)

2\. What’s the difference between a Dev Wallet and a Swap Wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** The Dev Wallet is used to deploy the token contract; the Swap Wallet is used to buy tokens on the market after launch (typically for market-making or liquidity control).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-whats-the-advantage-of-pre-generating-the-token-contract)

3\. What’s the advantage of pre-generating the token contract?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It saves deployment wait time and ensures a smoother sniping process without delays — especially useful for short-term opportunities.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-is-paying-the-jito-tip-required)

4\. Is paying the Jito tip required?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It’s not required, but enabling it greatly improves transaction priority and helps avoid being front-run or missing the launch.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-will-the-system-store-my-private-key)

5\. Will the system store my private key?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. All signing processes are done locally in your browser. CiaoTool never uploads or stores private keys, ensuring your security.

# Solana Tax Token2022 Creation Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Tax Token Creation：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/taxToken/create-token-2022arrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/taxToken/create-token-2022)

*   Token2022 Token Documentation: [https://spl.solana.com/token-2022arrow-up-right](https://spl.solana.com/token-2022)
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#how-to-use-the-solana-tax-token-token2022-creation-tool)

🛠️ How to Use the Solana Tax Token (Token2022) Creation Tool


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Connect Your Solana Wallet**
    
2.  **Enter the Full Name and Abbreviation for Your Project Token**
    
3.  **Upload the Token's Logo Image** (recommended size 1000\*1000 pixels)
    
4.  **Set the Token's Precision** (decimal places) and Total Supply
    
5.  **Fill in the Description for Your Project Token**
    
6.  **Set the Transaction or Transfer Fee Rate and the Maximum Fee per Transaction**
    
7.  **Set the Token Authority Address and Fee Withdrawal Wallet Address** (default is the current wallet)
    
8.  **Add Project's Social Links** (optional)
    
9.  **Advanced Settings for Authority Delegation and Interest Rate** (optional)
    
10.  **Set Token Metadata Modification Permissions, Freezing Permissions, and Minting Permissions**
    
11.  **Create the Token, Sign the Transaction, and Wait for the Token Creation to Complete**
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#preparation)

📋 **Preparation:**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A computer or a mobile phone
    
*   Solana wallet (Phantom wallet installation tutorial)
    
*   At least 0.15 SOL in the wallet
    
*   Token logo and related information
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#specific-steps)

🔁 Specific steps:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Connect Your Solana Wallet**
    
    *   CiaoTool currently supports various popular Solana wallets such as Solflare, Phantom, OK Wallet, etc. This tutorial uses the Phantom wallet as an example.
        
    *   Solana Tax Token (Token2022) Creation: [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/taxToken/create-token-2022arrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/taxToken/create-token-2022)
        
    *   Enter the CiaoTool Token2022 token creation page, and you can switch the language in the upper right corner.
        
    *   Click the "Select Wallet" button in the upper right corner, then choose the wallet you are using in the pop-up window. The wallet should have 0.15 SOL for payment.
        
    *   After connecting, you can see the wallet address displayed in the upper right corner.
        
    
    ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FykdfdUe9JTehlVWRuLx5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52b48cc0-4165-4b81-9b26-82f9849abe35&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b75b2d1a&sv=2)
    
2.  **Fill in the token-related information and upload the logo**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FtAIBzaFi8QVsrTlJBrDu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De84dab74-1d07-4b61-8f60-859ae8de76b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1074325d&sv=2)

1.  **Set the token's precision (decimal places) and total supply.**
    

*   **About Token Precision:** Token precision defines how small a unit the token can be divided into. The maximum precision for SPL tokens is 9. Common precision settings are 6 (utility tokens) and 9 (high precision applications), while 0 precision is typically used for NFTs.
    

1.  **Fill in the description for your project (token). This is the most straightforward place to introduce your project.**
    
    ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FlQD5LAxVrpbcq2Dez39F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc1d97e1a-a2e3-4a10-8f57-5858f91466cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a23f9997&sv=2)
    
2.  **Set the token's mechanism parameters:**
    
    *   **Fee Rate %**: The transaction or transfer fee rate, in percentage.
        
    *   **Maximum Fee**: The maximum fee for a single transfer or transaction.
        
    *   **Authority Wallet Address**: The wallet address with all permissions for this token, defaulting to the currently connected wallet address.
        
    *   **Withdrawal Wallet Address**: The address authorized to withdraw the fees generated by the token, defaulting to the currently connected wallet address.
        
        ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FvNYD0263akomG65KRkdO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0df2556-4ee9-4d9c-923f-264b9d72aad9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfe147e5&sv=2)
        
    
3.  **Add social links for your project (optional).**
    
    If you want users to join your community or learn about your project, this information is the most straightforward way to do so.
    
    ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FeW0hYOaf8x4r71LYppno%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee80cd58-7e52-4636-80f5-c8d22292c131&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a829b1e8&sv=2)
    
4.  **Token Metadata Modification Permission, Freezing Permission, and Minting Permission Settings:**
    

*   **Token Metadata Modification Permission**: "Renounce Authority" means you will no longer be able to modify the token metadata.
    
*   **Freezing Permission**: If you renounce freezing permission, it means you will no longer be able to freeze tokens in the holder's wallet.
    
*   **Minting Permission**: "Renounce Minting Authority" is necessary for making investors feel more secure and ensuring the success of the token. If you renounce minting authority, it means you will no longer be able to mint additional token supply.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FClNOk9NW67k8zfXV9VWT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0761fc77-0938-4f89-8950-a1a030b6a773&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8b3aa71&sv=2)

1.  **Create the token, sign the transaction, and wait for the token creation to complete**
    

> After clicking "Create Token," a source data file (Metadata) for the token information will be generated.
> 
> The generation process takes about 10 seconds. After that, your wallet will be prompted for a signature to complete the on-chain token creation.

1.  After creation is complete, you can view and copy the contract address of the created token at the bottom of the page.You can also open your wallet and view the token information in the Phantom wallet.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#id-1.-what-is-a-token2022-fee-token)

1\. What is a Token2022 fee token?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Token2022 is an upgraded Solana token standard that supports features like **customizable transaction fees**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#id-2.-how-can-i-set-the-transaction-fee-rate)

2\. How can I set the transaction fee rate?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** During token creation, simply enter the fee parameters in the interface — **multiple flexible configurations** are supported.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#id-3.-what-custom-features-does-token2022-support)

3\. What custom features does Token2022 support?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It supports **transaction fees**, **custom authorities**, **cold wallet management**, and more.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-token2022#id-4.-what-are-the-benefits-of-using-token2022-tokens)

4\. What are the benefits of using Token2022 tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** They offer **greater flexibility** for project strategies and help **enhance token ecosystem security**.

# Bundled Buy Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-exclamation

The bundled buy feature now supports multiple ecosystems, including **Pump, PumpSwap, Raydium (AMMv4, CPMM, CLMM), Bonk, Bonk-USD1, and Meteora**, making it adaptable to various launch and market-making scenarios.

*   Bundling supports single-address operations, but for a single address, it’s recommended to use the market-making feature instead.
    
*   When performing bundled buys or sells, do not leave blank lines between addresses, as this may trigger an error.
    

circle-check

**Here’s an example using Raydium for a bundled buy**: [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/raydium/bundled-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/raydium/bundled-buy)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#how-to-perform-a-bundled-buy)

🧩 How to Perform a Bundled Buy？


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve the authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FytWo9OXhwVllWwAO5DuB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe364a22-66b8-4fc5-b3b6-31f0789b8345&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54de54b8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-2.-open-the-bundled-buy-interface)

**2\. Open the Bundled Buy Interface**

*   Navigate to the bundled buy operation page for your selected platform.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FaGwYowat5Uwkf3MIxj6G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deda94c4b-22c7-4389-be80-04728e0dbc4f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2d47a07&sv=2)

circle-info

When selecting **Meteora**, this also applies to **Bags** and **Believe**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

**Token to Buy:** You can choose a token from the currently connected wallet or manually enter the token contract address.

*   **Bundled Buy Wallet Setup:**
    
    *   Batch import wallets (supported formats: **Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
        
    *   Refresh imported wallet balances
        
    *   Set buy amounts
        
    *   Batch remove wallets with insufficient f
        
    

circle-exclamation

**Note:** When selecting **Bonk**, the wallet quantity rules for bundled buying differ.

*   If **Send Type = JITO** → Maximum **9 wallets per group**
    
*   If **Send Type = RPC** → Maximum **10 wallets per group**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F2v45ZSlAtXWxuyJxG0CR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De7e517cc-bb33-47bf-8dc3-191db29636ca&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=45062e7a&sv=2)

circle-info

**Designated Receiving Wallet (Optional):** Purchased tokens will be sent to the specified wallet address by default (**Raydium only**).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fm0nu8gDvjxycuRtwFL4d%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db11e1e04-b780-4ae5-95d9-ae3ac52f6963&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56b66d17&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-4.-configure-jito-parameters)

**4\. Configure Jito Parameters**

*   Choose a recommended speed setting or customize the tip amount.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FRy7aetEXvyx5HzKmfw0f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0d9d77f-0530-4885-a827-446c0a77038f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f6ac893&sv=2)

*   Click the **“Bundled Buy”** button at the bottom to execute the purchase.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#important-notes)

⚙️ **Important Notes**

*   Bundled buying supports multiple wallet groups participating simultaneously.
    
*   **Service Fee:** Paid by the **first imported wallet**.
    
*   **Jito Tip:** Paid by the **last wallet in the group**.
    
*   **SOL Balance Requirement:** Ensure all participating wallets have sufficient SOL.
    

circle-info

If any step fails, clear feedback will be provided. **No fees are charged for failed transactions.**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-1.-what-is-bundled-buying)

1\. What is bundled buying?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** A bundled buy packages multiple wallet addresses or transaction instructions into a single submission, improving execution efficiency and priority.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-2.-how-is-bundled-buying-different-from-normal-buying)

2\. How is bundled buying different from normal buying?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Bundled buying is **faster**, more resistant to slippage, and can leverage **Jito** for higher front-running success.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-3.-what-role-does-jito-play-in-bundled-buying)

3\. What role does Jito play in bundled buying?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Jito inserts your transaction into the **MEV priority queue**, accelerating confirmation and increasing your chance of buying at a lower price.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-4.-do-i-need-multiple-wallets-to-use-bundled-buying)

4\. Do I need multiple wallets to use bundled buying?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No — it also supports **multiple trades from a single wallet**, executed in batch.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bundled-marketcap/bundled-buy#id-5.-does-bundled-buying-increase-gas-fees)

5\. Does bundled buying increase gas fees?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Slightly higher than normal trades, but **usually worth it** in front-running scenarios due to the higher potential return.

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-zhuan-yi)

**1\. 什么是 多转一？**

*   check
    
    答：指将多个钱包中的代币统一转账至一个主地址的操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-2.-xi-tong-shi-fou-zhi-chi-gui-ji-bu-tong-jine)

**2\. 系统是否支持归集不同金额？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可设置全部转出或为每个地址自定义转账数额。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-3.-si-yao-shi-fou-an-quan)

**3\. 私钥是否安全？**

*   check
    
    答：安全。所有私钥仅用于本地签名，不上传任何服务器。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-4.-ke-yi-gui-ji-na-xie-dai-bi)

**4\. 可以归集哪些代币？**

*   check
    
    答：支持你选择链的所有代币，只需输入合约地址即可。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-dao-ru-da-liang-di-zhi)

**5\. 是否支持导入大量地址？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可通过xls、xlsx格式文件导入地址。

# Pump Launch And Bundled Buy Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump Launch And Bundled Buy：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/launch-and-buy)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#how-to-pump-launch-and-bundled-buy)

🧩 **How to** Pump **Launch and Bundled Buy？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-1.-connect-your-wallet-phantom-recommended)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet (Phantom Recommended)**

*   Open the **Pump Launch and Bundled Buy** interface.
    
*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FQoxnvrxcIDgCTZ1bRs3Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7920f842-23ab-476d-8afd-8644784c75dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=67cfa26a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-2.-fill-in-basic-token-information)

**2\. Fill in Basic Token Information**

*   You may manually enter token details or click **“Clone”** to copy information from another token.
    
*   Social media links are optional.
    
*   You can set **auto-sell all tokens when price increases by X%**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F2IqD8WZvn9XXGKMEHxHG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc407093-60c6-46ac-be2a-02f756442ca3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ee0917f&sv=2)

circle-info

If auto-sell is enabled, it is recommended **not to use the dev wallet for buying**, or provide the dev wallet’s private key below to participate. Otherwise, manual signature may be required during selling, which could cause delays.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-3.-customize-contract-address)

**3\. Customize Contract Address**

**Two Methods for Setting Custom Contract Addresses：**

1.  Create a personalized token address and choose whether it ends with **“pump”**.
    
    *   Check ☑️ **pump** and confirm in your wallet
        
    
2.  Select **“Import Private Key”**
    
    *   Paste your pre-generated private key (**The address must be a new one that has never paid SOL rent**)**.**
        
    *   The system will deploy the token using this address, ensuring the contract matches your expectation.
        
    

circle-exclamation

**Note:** Selecting either option will immediately require wallet signature and payment of the platform fee (0.01 SOL).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FVcNg9aV0aJXulFq1IQ46%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e64baef-f7cf-4d6e-89be-8ee2e7c573cc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5867fe74&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-4.-dev-wallet-settings)

**4\. Dev Wallet Settings**

*   If the dev wallet does **not** set a buy amount, no service fee is charged.
    
*   If it participates in buying, the same service fee as other buy wallets applies.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FI5kbTWXHNIGFe2T3B1Zi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Decf152cb-81ed-44f4-a7f8-3115ccecb147&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=807d97e7&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-5.-bundled-buy-wallet-settings)

**5\. Bundled Buy Wallet Settings**

*   Bundled buy uses a **tiered pricing model**—the more wallets you add, the lower the service fee per wallet.
    
*   **Batch import wallets** (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
    
*   **Set buy amount:** fixed amount / percentage / all (maximum purchasable amount per wallet)
    
*   In addition to service fees, each new address requires **0.00203928 SOL** as account rent.
    

circle-exclamation

For **Pump.fun Launch and Bundled Buy,** ensure buy wallets have sufficient funds and gas to avoid failure. Maximum **12 wallets** can participate simultaneously.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FKQn8qFxbUAEtITvltoeW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46cc38c1-dd47-4da7-b061-453c56d6ded9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea3dbccd&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

**Note:** Bundled buys may be identified as bots by the Pump platform.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FceNLLyR0NKJxJdRkzr18%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc57b990-5109-4557-8c09-5cda39871e11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c704c124&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-6.-pre-generate-token-contract)

**6\. Pre-Generate Token Contract**

*   Supports generating the contract address in advance—useful for pre-launch marketing or integrations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fn8JPSiUbdarxF8YGGavx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3efd4f58-9154-4430-adf8-9aa5f2bc389c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7d8d7354&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** If you have customized the contract address, there is no need to pre-generate the token contract again.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-7.-jito-tip-settings)

**7\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the Jito MEV tip to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority in block ordering.
    
*   After configuration, click **“Pump Launch & Buy.”**
    

circle-exclamation

This feature relies on **Jito bundling**. Due to network conditions, Jito nodes, RPC nodes, and block engine factors, the failure rate may be relatively high.

If the operation fails:

*   The launch will not succeed
    
*   No fees will be charged
    

You may try switching RPC nodes or block engines, increasing the Jito tip (**recommended: 0.01 SOL**), or retrying during lower on-chain activity periods.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-8.-process-display)

**8\. Process Display**

*   Once the task starts, a log pop-up will display real-time progress updates.
    
*   After a successful transaction, you will receive both the **transaction link** and **token link** for direct viewing.
    
*   If any issue occurs at any stage, clear feedback will be provided. No fees will be charged for failed operations.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252F7DHCBczZYxka1ZfcoI6B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd467cec2-88e7-4fcb-ae65-30f5f1b27d6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f15c9a6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-1.-what-is-pump-launch-and-bundled-buy)

1\. What is Pump Launch and Bundled Buy?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It refers to buying tokens simultaneously with multiple wallets at the exact moment of launch on Pump.fun, aiming to secure lower-priced allocations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-2.-the-maximum-bundle-is-12-addresses.-does-this-include-the-deployer-wallet)

2\. The maximum bundle is 12 addresses. Does this include the deployer wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. The 12 bundled wallets do not include the deployer wallet. In total, up to **13 wallets** (including the deployer) can participate at launch.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-3.-can-token-information-be-modified-after-launching-on-pump.fun)

3\. Can token information be modified after launching on Pump.fun?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. Tokens launched on Pump.fun have no special permissions—no minting, blacklisting, or metadata modification is allowed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-4.-will-my-token-contract-address-end-with-pump)

4\. Will my token contract address end with “pump”?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** This is optional and depends on whether you select the “ends with pump” option.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-5.-do-i-need-to-manually-add-liquidity-on-pump.fun)

5\. Do I need to manually add liquidity on Pump.fun?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. After users start buying, a bonding curve liquidity pool is automatically formed. No manual liquidity addition is required.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-6.-what-condition-must-be-met-for-a-pump.fun-token-to-launch-on-pumpswap)

6\. What condition must be met for a Pump.fun token to launch on PumpSwap?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** When the bonding curve pool reaches **85 SOL**, Pump.fun will automatically migrate the token to PumpSwap.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-and-buy#id-7.-what-is-the-initial-launch-price-on-pump.fun)

7\. What is the initial launch price on Pump.fun?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. After users start buying, a bonding curve liquidity pool is automatically formed. No manual liquidity addition is required.

# How to Create Liquidity on Raydium？ | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Create Raydium Liquidity:** [https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/arrow-up-right](https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-is-raydium)

🌊 What Is Raydium?

*   Raydium is an **Automated Market Maker (AMM)** built on the **Solana blockchain**. It leverages a **central limit order book** to enable lightning-fast trades, shared liquidity, and new yield-generating opportunities.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#raydium-pool-types-explained-cpmm-clmm-ammv4)

🧩 Raydium Pool Types Explained: CPMM / CLMM / AMMv4

Below is a comparison of the three common pool types on Raydium and their typical use cases.

Type

Model & Features

Advantages

Best Use Case

⚙️ **CPMM (Constant Product AMM)**

Uses the (x \* y = k) model

Supports Token-2022, multiple fee tiers, stable capital efficiency

General trading pairs, first-time pool creation

🏛️ **AMMv4 (Legacy AMM)**

Raydium’s historical AMM version

Mature, stable, compatible with OpenBook

Legacy projects, users requiring backward compatibility

🎯 **CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity)**

LPs define price ranges for liquidity

Deeper liquidity, lower slippage, flexible yield

Advanced LPs, market makers, strategy-driven users

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#how-to-add-liquidity-on-raydium-create-a-pool)

🛠️ How to Add Liquidity on Raydium (Create a Pool)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-1-connect-your-wallet)

1️⃣ Connect Your Wallet

Open Raydium [(Liquidity page)arrow-up-right](https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/)
 and click **Connect Wallet** to connect your Solana wallet (e.g. Phantom).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FY7RRttarmU1HsPYoWjIB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D817c15cd-f38c-4b7a-b787-71ce029fea28&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ec870bc&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-2-go-to-pool-creation)

2️⃣ Go to Pool Creation

Navigate to **Liquidity → Create**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F82VFi1V05c0g3lW1Awx3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22cb4eff-0f51-4c16-9281-54c66f135777&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4f6b5bb&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-3-choose-pool-type)

3️⃣ Choose Pool Type

You can select one of the following:

*   **CPMM (Standard AMM)**
    
*   **CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity)**
    
*   **AMMv4 (Legacy AMM)**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FgtNJkauJOGRKeqIc95ja%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6859dcf-45db-4b19-b885-446abe13e5a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b8e4c0f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-4-configure-pool-parameters-clmm-example)

4️⃣ Configure Pool Parameters (CLMM Example)

**1.Select Base & Quote Tokens**

*   The **base token** is the first token displayed in the trading pair.
    
*   The **quote token** is the token used to price the base token.
    

circle-info

For example, the quote token represents how much of it is required to buy **1 unit of the base token**. Common quote tokens include **SOL, USDC, or other stablecoins**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FPs2S0eXxgiU20VxeUgwJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabeeada0-68bf-408d-9751-7e696eca8c2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8014ded5&sv=2)

**2.Select Fee Tier**

The selected fee is paid by traders. Liquidity providers receive:

*   **100% of token emission rewards**
    
*   **84% of trading fees**, while:
    
    *   **12%** goes to RAY buybacks
        
    *   **4%** goes to the project treasury
        
    

**Available fee tiers (selectable by pool creator):**

*   **0.01%** – Very stable assets
    
*   **0.05%** – Pegged assets and high-volume pairs
    
*   **0.25%** – Most token pairs
    
*   **1%** – Exotic or highly volatile pairs
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fmfusv80dY3NryBEV1koL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd81fd204-568b-4aff-b091-7c4ddcec4b7e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=961341f6&sv=2)

**3.Set Initial Price**

The **initial price** defines how much quote token is required to purchase **1 base token** at pool creation.

The pool creator may view the price in either base token or quote token terms.

circle-exclamation

Once the pool is confirmed and initialized, the **initial price, fee tier, and initial liquidity cannot be edited**. However, the pool creator can add additional liquidity within any chosen price range at a later time.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Flc5orqAB7g7RhyovcM6f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd945b863-ddea-43e5-9fa3-e51d5516ad17&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee2f7e88&sv=2)

**4.Choose Position Price Range**

When selecting the initial price range, you are only defining **your first liquidity position**.

After the pool is created:

*   Other users may add liquidity at **any price range**
    
*   You can withdraw or create new positions at any time
    

circle-info

By default, the system suggests a range of **±50% around the initial price**, but you may customize it.

**In CLMM:**

*   If the market price **falls below your lower bound**, your position becomes **100% base token** (accumulating at lower prices)
    
*   If the market price **exceeds your upper bound**, your position becomes **100% quote token** (selling at higher prices)
    

circle-info

This differs from **CPMM**, where liquidity is distributed automatically across the entire price range (from 0 to ∞).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FlUhp9dHrLmGAJmlMhMFJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8012d1b4-fb76-4494-9a4e-b912661b3683&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8775dfc&sv=2)

**5.Deposit Amount**

*   The deposit amount represents the quantity of base and quote tokens used to initialize the pool.
    
*   Based on your previous settings, the system will automatically calculate the deposit ratio. The pool creator may manually adjust the amount of base and quote tokens.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FCDFL4urZmT9Wd16ZbEpK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86b77f96-d07d-482d-ad04-93e83f532868&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fdb72ad&sv=2)

**6.Preview & Confirm**

*   After setting the deposit amount, preview the pool configuration.
    
*   Click **Confirm Deposit** and approve the transaction.
    
*   🎉 Congratulations! You have successfully created a **concentrated liquidity pool on Raydium**.
    

circle-exclamation

Due to pool initialization, **network gas fees will be higher than usual**

Once the transaction is approved and the pool is live:

1.  The initial price and initial liquidity **cannot be modified**
    
2.  The pool creator may still manage positions or add liquidity within any preferred price range
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhat Are the Benefits of Providing Liquidity in Raydium Traditional AMM Pools (CPMM)?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-the-benefits-of-providing-liquidity-in-raydium-traditional-amm-pools-cpmm)

**Earn Trading Fee Revenue：**A **0.25% trading fee** is charged on swaps within the pool, of which:

*   **0.22%** is distributed to the LP pool
    
*   **0.03%** is allocated to the **RAY single-sided staking pool**
    

**Earn OpenBook Market-Making Revenue：**

*   Raydium AMM automatically provides liquidity on the **OpenBook order book**.
    
*   Market-making revenue generated on OpenBook is distributed proportionally to liquidity providers.
    

**Receive LP Tokens as Proof of Liquidity：**After adding liquidity, you will receive **LP tokens** representing your share of the pool.

**Example:** Deposit **RAY + USDC** → receive **RAY-USDC LP**

As trading occurs, fees accumulate in the pool, and the **value of LP tokens increases accordingly**.

chevron-rightWhat Are LP Tokens?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-lp-tokens)

LP tokens represent your **proportional ownership** of assets in a liquidity pool.

**Example:** Add liquidity to the **SOL-RAY** pool → receive **SOL-RAY LP**

You may redeem LP tokens at any time to withdraw your corresponding share of the pool’s assets.

chevron-rightWhat Are Ecosystem Farms?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-ecosystem-farms)

*   **Ecosystem Farms** are a new type of **permissionless farming mechanism** designed for Raydium traditional AMM pools.
    
*   Any project team or user can create a farm to distribute rewards for a specific pool, further enhancing liquidity across the Solana ecosystem.
    

chevron-rightWhat Are the Benefits of Providing Liquidity in Raydium CLMM Pools?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-the-benefits-of-providing-liquidity-in-raydium-clmm-pools)

**CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity Market Maker)** is designed for more advanced liquidity providers.

**Concentrated Liquidity and Higher Capital Efficiency：**LPs can choose a **custom price range** in which their liquidity is active.

This results in:

*   More concentrated liquidity
    
*   Higher fee efficiency
    
*   Lower trading slippage
    

**More Flexible Risk Management：**By selecting different price ranges, LPs can express different market views, such as **bullish, bearish, or neutral** strategies.

circle-info

**Note:** Impermanent Loss (IL) risk is higher, especially when the market price moves outside the selected range.

circle-check

**Learn more about Raydium liquidity pools and rules：**[https://docs.raydium.io/raydiumarrow-up-right](https://docs.raydium.io/raydium)

circle-check

**Create a Standard AMM Pool:** [https://docs.raydium.io/raydium/zhong-wen/chuangjian-chi-zi/chuang-jian-biao-zhun-amm-chiarrow-up-right](https://docs.raydium.io/raydium/zhong-wen/chuangjian-chi-zi/chuang-jian-biao-zhun-amm-chi)

# Pump Micro Trading Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump Micro Trading**：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/micro-tradingarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/micro-trading)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#how-to-perform-pump-micro-trading)

🧩 **How to Perform Pump Micro Trading？**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-1.-connect-your-wallet)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet**

*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FnaI6ZIg1UbbWijcW7dkA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6109f0b4-c7a9-4889-ae2e-d9f399d5f42f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b20d974&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-2.-open-the-pump-micro-trading-interface)

**2\. Open the Pump Micro Trading Interface**

*   Navigate to the **Pump Micro Trading** operation page.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-3.-fill-in-the-trade-details)

**3\. Fill in the Trade Details**

*   **Select Token:**Manually enter the token contract address.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fa4PkaHpIhE1Q38Y7Mdt2%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbaee0ca0-935b-4378-a8c3-701e1d1071fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee3949c8&sv=2)

*   **Trading Wallet Setup:**
    
    *   Batch import wallets (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
        
    *   Refresh imported wallet balances and token balances
        
    *   Remove wallets with insufficient funds
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FyuGI5OfcOzTNm617VgPy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45b66bad-ae85-46af-ba27-927e44bb6eb4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dbbbe53b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-4.-micro-trading-settings)

**4\. Micro Trading Settings**

*   **Per-Trade Amount:** The minimum order displayed on the Pump homepage is **0.01 SOL**. Larger trade amounts increase the probability of being displayed.
    
*   **Task Interval:** Choose between **random** or **fixed interval** (seconds).
    
*   **Wallet Execution Order:** Sequential execution or random execution.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZE2tr8OVA3fNVkzieNbj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d7fcdbb-d23b-4ed8-9486-ef515b151671&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1691caaf&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-5.-jito-tip-settings)

**5\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the **Jito MEV tip** to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F2etAOHPdoKKU5RDG6uUr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D026b77bb-5a43-4652-9739-4f7f8472475a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78c93c98&sv=2)

*   Click **“Start Micro Trading”** to begin.
    

circle-info

Note: Each buy or sell counts as one trade. Service fees apply separately for buying and selling, and fees are displayed at the bottom of the trading page.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-1.-what-is-pump-micro-trading)

1\. What is Pump Micro Trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Micro trading refers to using very small buy and sell amounts to continuously keep the project exposed on the Pump homepage without significantly affecting the token price.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-2.-what-is-the-purpose-of-micro-trading)

2\. What is the purpose of micro trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Micro trading increases project activity metrics, boosts visibility on the homepage or popular lists, and attracts more real users to click and follow.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-3.-does-the-trade-amount-affect-the-effectiveness)

3\. Does the trade amount affect the effectiveness?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It is generally recommended to use small amounts between 0.001–0.01 SOL; frequent repeated executions achieve better volume boosting, as the system reads trade frequency rather than total amount.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-4.-will-micro-trading-cause-chart-abnormalities-or-market-impact)

4\. Will micro trading cause chart abnormalities or market impact?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. CiaoTool has optimized micro trading with a default "hide chart impact" mode to avoid noticeable price swings or sharp spikes in trades.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/micro-trading#id-5.-can-multiple-addresses-be-set-for-batch-micro-trading)

5\. Can multiple addresses be set for batch micro trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. The system supports batch importing multiple wallet addresses and will automatically rotate small trades to increase naturalness and anti-detection capability.

# BSC 中转转账教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC 中转转账**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/relay-transferarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/relay-transfer)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 **操作步骤**

triangle-exclamation

**转出钱包数量需要和目标钱包数量一致！**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-1.-xuan-ze-dai-bi-di-zhi)

**1\. 选择代币地址**

*   输入或选择需要发送的 BSC 代币合约地址。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FgD5FEZlKcauwwpyIKuFn%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50da0a89&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-2.-shang-chuan-fa-song-si-yao)

**2\. 上传发送私钥**

*   上传包含多个私钥的钱包文件（xls、xlsx格式），系统将识别来源钱包。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FEF41y8aHvR2FeHCoTBXK%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c601e0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-3.-shang-chuan-jie-shou-di-zhi)

**3\. 上传接收地址**

*   上传接收地址列表，确保发送方和接收方数量一致（如10个地址发给10个接收地址）。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FHeK6LGgnDpFDh5LgIX2U%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=468a9ea6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-4.-she-zhi-zhuan-zhang-can-shu)

**4\. 设置转账参数**

1.  **全部数量**：把地址中持有的**全部代币数量**一次性转出。
    
2.  **固定数量**：为每个目标地址**分配相同数量**的代币。
    
3.  **固定留存：**在操作时**保留钱包中一定数量**的代币，不全部转出。
    
4.  **自定义数量(点击输入)：**手动输入每个地址应获得的具体数量，可**灵活设置不同分配比例**。
    
5.  **中转次数：**在一次完整转账过程中，**资金经过多少次中间地址转移**后，才到达最终接收地址。
    

triangle-exclamation

中转次数越多，代表资金路径越复杂

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FaTokpxrjiSH2rxhyMEe4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cad0719&sv=2)

*   自定义输入转账数量可上传文件或手动换行输入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FW2qhRAwRxX26i9mAYugV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d618ff8d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-5.-sheng-cheng-zhong-zhuan-qian-bao)

**5\. 生成中转钱包**

*   系统自动生成中间跳转地址，用于中转操作（隐藏转账路径）。
    
*   查看钱包资金状态
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F2yacbeUozHwk8WVzqPAP%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d96c115f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-6.-zhi-xing-fa-song)

**6\. 执行发送**

*   一键确认操作并签名，系统将自动完成中转转账交易。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-1.-shen-me-shi-bsc-zhong-zhuan-zhuan-zhang)

**1\. 什么是 BSC** 中转转账**？**

*   check
    
    答：为用户提供一种更隐蔽和安全的转账方式。用户可以有效隐藏转账路径，从而提高资金转账的隐私性和安全性。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-2.-mei-ge-di-zhi-ke-yi-she-zhi-bu-tong-jinema)

**2\. 每个地址可以设置不同金额吗？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可在上传文件中自定义每笔交易的金额。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-3.-xi-tong-shi-fou-bao-cun-wo-de-si-yao)

**3\. 系统是否保存我的私钥？**

*   check
    
    答：不会。所有签名操作仅在本地浏览器完成，保障私钥安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-4.-zhi-chi-duo-shao-ge-di-zhi-jin-xing-zhong-zhuan-zhuan-zhang)

**4\. 支持多少个地址进行**中转**转账？**

*   check
    
    答：地址越多，中转消耗的时间就越久，但是隐私和安全性久越高，理论上没有数量限制，取决于网络以及服务器，适合中大型批量操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-5.-shi-fou-ke-yi-dao-ru-xlsxlsx-ge-shi-wen-jian)

**5\. 是否可以导入**xls、xlsx格式**文件？**

*   check
    
    答：可以。发送私钥和接收地址都支持 xls、xlsx格式导入，提高效率。

# CiaoTool · EVM | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

![Page cover](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252F68dq0AiOX5ixAY8KvvPq%252F423954199%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6334858-8c51-4149-ad5d-644dcbc0f039&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2ffd37a&sv=2)

*   CiaoTool integrates token creation, project management, liquidity deployment, airdrops, and market-making tools into one powerful platform.
    
*   It provides a complete one-stop solution to help users efficiently launch projects, optimize liquidity structures, and build successful tokens.
    

circle-check

Currently, CiaoTool supports major EVM networks including **BSC, IoTeX, Base, and X Layer**, with more chains and features continuously being added. Stay tuned.

[![Logo](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fbsc.ciaotool.io%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92b0cc9b&sv=2)https://bsc.ciaotool.io/bsc.ciaotool.iochevron-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/)

🚀 From Token Launch to Management — All in One Place

*   CiaoTool integrates essential tools such as **one-click token launch**, **MultiSender**, **Asset Fragmentation**, **anti-MEV protection**, and **liquidity control**. From creation and deployment to distribution and permission management, users can execute complex on-chain operations **without writing any code**. Even Web3 newcomers can quickly master token issuance and operations through CiaoTool’s intuitive **visual interface**.
    
*   We value every user’s needs and feedback. The platform will continue expanding its feature modules based on community input.

3.  All users must ensure they comply with their local laws while using the platform. CiaoTool is **not liable for any legal consequences** resulting from user violations.
    

###

Why Choose CiaoTool ?

1️⃣ **Visual No-Code Operations：**Intuitive contract creation and configuration process. Deploy and set up critical parameters with zero code, empowering even beginners to launch tokens independently.

2️⃣ **Optimized for PancakeSwap：**Easily create, add, or remove liquidity with real-time price and slippage display.

3️⃣ **Batch Tools：**Handle multi-transfer, batch collection/sending, failed transaction retry, and gas budgeting with ease.

4️⃣ **Multi-chain, multi-scenario support:** Covering BSC (**Four.meme**, **Flap**, **Binance Alpha**), **IoTeX (Robot Pump**), as well as Base and X Layer, meeting diverse token issuance and operational needs across ecosystems.

# EVM 多链通用操作说明（必读） | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/evm-duo-lian-tong-yong-cao-zuo-shuo-ming-bi-du#wei-shen-me-jiao-cheng-shi-tong-yong-de)

💡 **为什么教程是通用的？**

*   教程截图可能以 **BSC (BNB** **Smart** **Chain)** 为示例，方便演示（交易速度快，Gas 费低）。
    

实际操作中：

*   **界面一致**：Base、IoTeX、X Layer 等链上的发币界面与 BSC 完全相同。
    
*   **功能一致**：发币、空投、归集等逻辑完全相同。
    
*   **唯一区别**：需要在钱包中切换网络，并准备对应链的 Gas 代币（如 BNB、IOTX、ETH）。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/evm-duo-lian-tong-yong-cao-zuo-shuo-ming-bi-du#he-xin-bu-zhou-qie-huan-wang-luo-guan-jian)

⚙️ **核心步骤：切换网络（关键）**

1.  **选择目标网络**：在页面 选择 BSC、IoTeX、Base 或 X Layer
    
2.  **连接钱包：**点击右上角 **Connect Wallet**
    
3.  **自动刷新与状态同步**：
    
    *   当前链标识自动更新
        
    *   Gas 代币符号自动更新（如 BNB → IOTX / ETH）
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/evm-duo-lian-tong-yong-cao-zuo-shuo-ming-bi-du#xuan-ze-nin-de-lian-yi-jian-jin-ru-zhuan-shu-ru-kou)

🌐 **选择您的链：一键进入专属入口**

链名称

状态

入口链接

🔶 BNB Chain (BSC)

✅ 稳定

[进入 BSC 中心页arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/)

🟠 IoTeX

✅ 稳定

[进入 IoTeX 中心页arrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/)

🔵 Base Chain

✅ 稳定

[进入 Base 中心页arrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/)

⚫ X Layer

✅ 稳定

[进入 X Layer 中心页arrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/)

> 新链上线后，CiaoTool 会自动添加工具中心页，无需等待教程更新。

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 创建/添加流动性「v3」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-v3)

**添加流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3)

circle-exclamation

创建前必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB）**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#chuang-jian-tian-jia-liu-dong-xing-v3-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 创建/添加流动性v3详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8AhGayayJ4AHNtEmNeFz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c71d944&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-2-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

**2️⃣ 选择加池的两种代币**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FFcslP8CSH9YAcMnLGWH2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfbe1cf&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

添加流动性时：输入币对地址即可

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6liyVtfSkXWNzxboeJnH%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7747f57d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-3-xuan-ze-shou-xu-fei-ji-bie)

**3️⃣ 选择手续费级别**

*   V3 的 LP 手续费不同于V2，不再是复利。
    
*   交易费用不同：V3有四种不同的交易费等级，最多可降低25倍交易费用；V2每一笔交易将支付0.25%手续费。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Ftz5TOEaoz0lzKBQ28oPb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7365aa6&sv=2)

circle-info

Swap v3创建流动性滑点设置默认为1%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-4-she-zhi-chu-shi-jia-ge-yu-jia-ge-qu-jian)

**4️⃣ 设置初始价格与价格区间**

1.区间大小決定收益高低 (LP 手续费收益、CAKE 收益皆适用)

*   越窄收益越高，无常损失越大
    
*   越宽收益越低，无常损失越小
    
*   全区间设置则类似于 V2 运作，收益将非常少
    

2.超出区间时

*   无收益
    
*   流动性仓位将变为单币
    
*   可以移除流动性并重新添加，或是等待价格重新回到区间内
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FKCiVPNtRpqyauuZgXEGX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4e7a943&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-5-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

**5️⃣ 填写加池数量**

*   输入代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8Zlmc9TNOTG6lH0PxPBv%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36fa8fc7&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-6-shou-quan-dai-bi)

6️⃣ **授权代币**

*   第一次操作时，需要授权合约使用你的代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-7-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

7️⃣ **开始交易**

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
