# 创建流动性并捆绑买入「v2」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性并捆绑买入 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#ru-he-shi-yong-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

✅ 如何使用**创建流动性并捆绑买入**？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

1\. **连接钱包**

circle-info

创建前必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB）**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FIVf4IOZk63OZDweTKe3R%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=559b5673&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FhhD5AaWP8Y7YT8jwiWOO%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e47026b4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-2.-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

2\. 选择加池的两种代币

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FNbjzC96pyAMUXmkhDzO0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8a0bba5&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-3.-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

3.**填写加池数量**

*   输入两种代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FikIxiIOzzvrI5QKRnLxd%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85cc50a&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-4.-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

4\. 导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以手动粘贴多个私钥，也可以 上传包含私钥的表格文件（xlsx / xls）。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额、From余额、To余额。
    

circle-exclamation

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个地址**。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-5.-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

5\. 设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

*   为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
*   可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
*   系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

circle-info

注意：买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FylaxJvYLIARyXhf9k0Pp%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d05af914&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-6.-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

6\. 开始交易

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    
*   交易速度会受到链上拥堵情况影响，链上拥堵时可能交易速度较慢，还请您耐心等待。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-1.-wei-shen-me-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru-hui-shi-bai)

**1\.** 为什么创建流动性并捆绑买入会失败？

*   check
    
    答：请确认钱包内 BNB / WBNB 余额是否充足，以覆盖加池，捆绑买入所需资金及 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-2.-jia-chi-de-dai-bi-shu-liang-he-bi-li-you-yao-qiu-ma)

**2\.** 加池的代币数量和比例有要求吗？

*   check
    
    答：没有强制限制。你可以根据 代币经济模型、预期初始价格及市值目标 灵活调整加池数量与比例。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-3.-yu-gu-jia-ge-hui-yi-zhi-gu-ding-ma)

**3\.** 预估价格会一直固定吗？

*   check
    
    答：不会。预估价格仅代表 上线初始价格，随着用户持续买卖，价格会实时变化，交易越活跃，价格越真实。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-4.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-you-na-xie-xian-zhi)

**4\.** 什么是多地址捆绑买入？有哪些限制？

*   check
    
    答：多地址捆绑买入是指 多个钱包同时执行买入操作，实现更合理的筹码分布。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 「批量一转多」教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC 批量一转多：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

**Base 批量一转多：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

**X Layer 批量一转多：**[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

**IoTeX 批量一转多：**[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#pi-liang-yi-zhuan-duo-jiao-cheng)

📘 批量**一转多**教程

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FAwpCURdJp3FX3HWNWvj9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=756da39b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#id-2.-dian-ji-tian-jia-ye-mian-wei-mei-yi-zu-yi-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang-ren-wu-chuang-jian-yi-ge-ye-mian-ke)

**2\. 点击「添加页面」**：为每一组一对多转账任务创建一个页面（可自定义转账地址与数量）。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPcocfbFio9UXBk3UUhzz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=380fb103&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#id-3.-tian-xie-mei-ge-ye-mian-de-can-shu-xuan-ze-dai-bi-di-zhi-tian-xie-jie-shou-di-zhi-ji-jine)

**3\. 填写每个页面的参数**：选择代币地址，填写接收地址及金额。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FJpDYR1SnFUU37ac07QmV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6498c7c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#id-4.-dian-ji-shua-xin-yue-cha-kan-dang-qian-qian-bao-zai-ge-ye-mian-zhong-suo-xu-de-dai-bi-yue)

**4\. 点击「刷新余额」**：查看当前钱包在各页面中所需的代币余额。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F5mj5q1arjlvS00kVGNrh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22e9c5c7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#id-5.-dian-ji-yi-jian-zhi-xing-xi-tong-jiang-zi-dong-zhu-ye-chu-li-pi-liang-zhuan-zhang-cao-zuo-ti-shen)

**5\. 点击「一键执行」**：系统将自动逐页处理批量转账操作，提升执行效率。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FaLCGYQOnaoHr1FrZsVze%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8d227a3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many-multi#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题（FAQ）

**1\. 什么是批量一转多？**

*   check
    
    **答**：批量一转多是将多个一对多转账任务组合在一起统一执行的方式，适合复杂资金分发场景。
    

**2\. 一次最多能添加几个页面？**

*   check
    
    **答**：系统默认支持添加多个转账页面，具体数量取决于设备性能与页面复杂度。
    

**3\. 每个页面是否可以使用不同的代币？**

*   check
    
    **答**：可以。每个页面可设置独立的代币和接收地址。
    

**4\. 点击「一键执行」后可以暂停或取消吗？**

*   check
    
    **答**：执行过程中不可中断，请在确认参数无误后再操作。
    

**5\. 是否支持导入接收地址文件？**

*   check
    
    **答**：支持。每个页面都可上传接收地址xls、xlsx格式文件，便于快速导入大批量地址。

# 移除流动性「v3」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**移除流动性 v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/remove-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/remove-liquidity-v3)

circle-exclamation

必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB）**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#yi-chu-liu-dong-xing-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 移除流动性详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FNdlNqKeYrPleFWqlKF40%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2eccfc14&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-2-shu-ru-yong-yu-yi-chu-liu-dong-xing-de-si-yao)

**2️⃣** 输入用于移除流动性的私钥

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-3-she-zhi-yi-chu-bi-li)

**3️⃣ 设置移除比例**

*   输入移除的流动性比例：自定义，最大为100%，点击Max即可。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FGLudfjoVp0YLIM2kwWZ9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f43d49cc&sv=2)

circle-info

**关于比例：**假设池子都是您一个人加的， 那么这个百分比=池子的百分比。如果池子是多个人加的，就需要另外算的。比如，您本身占有池子份额的20%。那么您即便选择100%，整个池子也只是锁了20%的流动性而已。如果您选择20%，那么整个池子也就是锁了4%的流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-4-gou-xuan-xu-yao-yi-chu-de-liu-dong-xing)

**4️⃣ 勾选需要移除的流动性**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-5-yi-chu-liu-dong-xing)

**5️⃣ 移除流动性**

*   确认信息无误后，点击开始交易。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#faq)

**FAQ**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-1.-wei-shen-me-che-chi-hui-shi-bai)

**1\. 为什么撤池会失败？**

*   check
    
    钱包内 BNB / WBNB 是否足够。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-2.-che-chi-hou-dai-bi-hai-neng-jiao-yi-ma)

**2\. 撤池后代币还能交易吗？**

*   check
    
    如果全部移除是不能交易的，只是移除添加一部分是还能交易的。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-3.-yi-chu-hui-shou-qu-fei-yong-ma)

**3\. 移除会收取费用吗？**

*   check
    
    会的，移除流动性是按次收费，每次0.024BNB
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 多地址捆绑买入教程「v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**多地址捆绑买入v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-buy-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-buy-v2)

**多地址捆绑买入v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-buy-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-buy-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-jiao-cheng)

🪜 多地址捆绑买入教程

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-1.-dao-ru-si-yao)

1\. 导入私钥

*   将用于支付市值操作手续费的钱包私钥导入。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FvVtAMFWuGgoNnCvYfjQj%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74f8652&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-2.-dao-ru-bi-dui-di-zhi-huo-xuan-ze-bi-dui)

2\. 导入币对地址或选择币对

*   **v2-**在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fgjluf7csT7zet2lhBxMc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=385d8099&sv=2)

*   **v3-**在币对输入框中 **粘贴目标币对**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F2GyM9wN3dNywtprGN3hu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=573b97e5&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#di-er-bu-cao-zuo-zhong-v2-he-v3-de-qu-bie-zai-yu-v2-shou-dong-xuan-ze-liang-zhong-dai-bi-v3-shu-ru-b)

第二步操作中v2和v3的区别在于：v2手动选择两种代币，v3输入币对地址。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-3.-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

3\. 导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（**xls、xlsx格式**）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额、TokenA余额、TokenB余额。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个地址**。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-4.-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

4\. 设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FA0vQi2nE1C5RnB0jCbZO%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7042b87&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-5.-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

5\. 开始交易

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑买入操作。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fa4AbPzlrGYNhEhe3VOXX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebc8f5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时买入同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步买入。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-ru-di-zhi-de-bnb-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 BNB 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-ru-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义买入金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定买入金额，也可以统一设定同样的买入数额。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)

*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# The Beginner Guide to Token Creation | CiaoTool

*   The blockchain world can look complicated: tons of jargon, different chains, fee mechanisms, permission settings…
    
*   But in reality, creating a token isn’t mysterious at all. With smart one-click token-creation platforms like CiaoTool, you don’t need to write any code or stress about security and deployment. In just a few minutes, your token can be ready.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-1-preparations-and-basic-concepts-before-creating-a-token)

🧩 **Part 1: Preparations and Basic Concepts Before Creating a Token**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#what-is-creating-a-token)

🔹 **What is “creating a token”?**

*   **Creating token** means deploying a token contract on an existing blockchain. You define its name, symbol, total supply, and functions — in short, you are its creator.
    

> **Example:** Bitcoin is an independent blockchain (produced through mining), whereas what you’re creating is a “token” deployed on an existing blockchain, such as generating your own token on BSC or Solana.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#choosing-a-blockchain-where-to-launch-your-token)

🔹 **Choosing a Blockchain: Where to Launch Your Token?**

circle-info

Different blockchains have varying rules and costs, so this is something you should plan ahead. BSC and Solana are currently among the most popular choices.

*   The mainstream options are as follows:
    

Blockchain

Features

Suitable For

BSC (Binance Smart Chain)

Mature and stable, low transaction costs

Beginners / project teams

Solana

Fast, active ecosystem

Users creating Meme or light projects

Base / X Layer / IoTeX

Emerging chains, flexible operations

Developers exploring new ecosystems

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZUxKuEHs2EGjWMsVLi5F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45cead28-7e14-4795-9073-a9d1d4f8b1b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5d78269&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#how-to-create-a-token)

🔹 **How to Create a Token?**

Normally, issuing a token requires a developer to write a smart contract and deploy it on the blockchain. But if you’re not technical, you can skip the coding step entirely by using a one-click token creation tool like **CiaoTool**. By paying a small service fee, you can have your own token ready in just a few minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#how-much-does-it-cost-to-create-a-token)

🔹 **How Much Does It Cost to Create a Token?**

The cost varies depending on the blockchain and is generally paid in the chain’s native token. You can check the official pages for real-time fees:

*   **Solana** ➜ Paid in SOL, fees: [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/pricearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/price)
    
*   **BSC** ➜ Paid in BNB, fees: [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bsc/pricearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bsc/price)
    
*   **Base** ➜ Paid in ETH，fees: [https://base.ciaotool.io/arrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **IoTeX** ➜ Paid in IOTX，fees: [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/iotex/pricearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/iotex/price)
    
*   **OKX Chain**（X Layer) ➜ Paid in OKB，fees: [https://xlayer.ciaarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/)
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#what-can-you-do-after-creating-a-token)

🔹 **What Can You Do After Creating a Token?**

You can:

*   Transfer or airdrop it to others
    
*   Create a liquidity pool for trading
    
*   Track your token’s market data on DEX platforms
    

⚠️ **Note:** To enable **trading**, assign a **price**, and have your token appear on platforms like **GMGN** and **DexScreener**, you must create a **liquidity pool**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#launch-vs.-one-click-token-creation)

🔹 **Launch vs. One-Click Token Creation**

Type

Features

Note

Launch

No liquidity pool, tokens must be purchased, limited control by the project team

Suitable for lightweight applications

One-Click Token Creation

Tokens are received directly, liquidity can be added independently, functions are configurable

The project team has full control over the token logic

> CiaoTool supports both modes: you can either use the **one-click token creation** feature or connect to internal platforms like PumpFun, BonkFun, Fourmeme, and Flap to create and purchase tokens within their ecosystems.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#token-creation-prep-checklist)

⚙️ **Token Creation Prep Checklist**

Tools

Purpose

Computer / Phone

Using a computer is recommended for more stable and convenient operations

VPN or internet access tool

Access on-chain resources and tutorials

Wallet (MetaMask / Phantom / OKX)

Store blockchain assets

Assets Preparation

Have BNB, SOL, or other tokens ready to pay gas fees in your wallet

Telegram

Join the official CiaoTool Telegram group for support: [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

circle-exclamation

*   Don’t know how to use a wallet ❌ Not recommended to create a token
    
*   Wallet has no funds ❌ Not recommended to create a token
    
*   Don’t understand basic concepts ❌ Not recommended to create a token
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-2-practical-guide-to-creating-a-token)

💥 **Part 2: Practical Guide to Creating a Token**

Ready? In this section, we dive into hands-on steps! Whether you’re making a community token, a Meme coin, or an experimental project, the process is largely the same.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#fill-in-basic-information)

Fill in Basic Information

Parameters and recommendations:

*   **Name:** Full token name, can be in Chinese or English. Example: SolDog
    
*   **Symbol:** Short code, usually 3–5 letters. Example: DOG, MEOW
    
*   **Supply:** Maximum token amount, recommended as an integer (no decimals)
    
*   **Decimals:** Smallest divisible unit, default 6 or 9
    
*   **Logo:** Supported on Solana; for other chains, uploads may not display. (On Solana, you can replace freely; for other chains, contact official support)
    

2

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#optional-feature-configuration)

Optional Feature Configuration

Features and suitable users:

*   **Burn:** Destroy part of the tokens to increase scarcity. Suitable for deflationary projects
    
*   **Blacklist:** Freeze specific addresses to prevent malicious wallets
    
*   **Mint:** Dynamically increase supply, mainly for testing purposes
    
*   **Standard Token:** No special permissions, recommended for beginners, fully green in safety checks
    

> Beginners are recommended to create a **Standard Token** — simplest functionality, highest security, and most friendly for risk-control checks.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#choose-a-blockchain)

Choose a Blockchain

*   **EVM-based chains (BSC / Base / X Layer):** Powerful features, high compatibility, slightly higher cost
    
*   **Solana:** Fast, logo displays nicely, simpler functionality
    

4

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#payment-and-creation)

**Payment and Creation**

After confirming all parameters, the system will prompt you to pay the token creation fee. Once paid, the token will be automatically generated and sent to your connected wallet.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-3-managing-and-maintaining-your-token)

💼 **Part 3: Managing and Maintaining Your Token**

Congratulations! You now officially own your token. But the next crucial step is how to operate and maintain your token ecosystem.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#quick-faq-and-liquidity-pool-faq)

💡 **Quick FAQ and** Liquidity Pool FAQ

chevron-right**Q1：Where is my token? Why doesn’t it show in my wallet?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q1-where-is-my-token-why-doesnt-it-show-in-my-wallet)

All tokens are in the wallet you connected. If it doesn’t appear, manually add the token address.

chevron-right**Q2：How can I trade it?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q2-how-can-i-trade-it)

Create a liquidity pool, for example:

*   **BSC:** PancakeSwap → [https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/poolsarrow-up-right](https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/pools)
    ?
    
*   **Solana:** Raydium → [https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/arrow-up-right](https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/)
    
*   **Base:** PancakeSwap → [https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/poolsarrow-up-right](https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/pools)
    ?
    
*   **X Layer:** PotatoSwap → [https://potatoswap.finance/swaparrow-up-right](https://potatoswap.finance/swap)
    

chevron-right**Q3: How is the token price determined?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q3-how-is-the-token-price-determined)

Price = ratio of the two assets in the liquidity pool. For example: 100 USDT + 100 TOKEN → initial price 1 USDT/TOKEN

chevron-rightQ4：Why does risk detection show red?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q4-why-does-risk-detection-show-red)

Adding features like “Mint” or “Blacklist” flags high risk in checks. It’s recommended to use a **Standard Token** to keep the green status.

chevron-rightQ5：If someone buys my token, where does the money go?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q5-if-someone-buys-my-token-where-does-the-money-go)

The purchase funds go into the liquidity pool. To withdraw earnings, use the “Remove Liquidity” function.

chevron-rightQ6: Who can create a liquidity pool?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q6-who-can-create-a-liquidity-pool)

Anyone with tokens and assets can create one.

chevron-right**Q7: How much should I invest in the pool?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q7-how-much-should-i-invest-in-the-pool)

There’s no fixed minimum; even a few dozen USD can work.

chevron-right**Q8: Can the pool’s tokens be completely bought out?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q8-can-the-pools-tokens-be-completely-bought-out)

In theory, no. The price will rise gradually as demand increases, approaching but never reaching zero.

chevron-right**Q9: How can I stabilize the token price?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q9-how-can-i-stabilize-the-token-price)

Using CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity Market Maker) or adding single-token liquidity can help make the price more stable.

chevron-right**Q10: Does Solana require a Market ID?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q10-does-solana-require-a-market-id)

Only in AMM mode is creating a Market ID necessary.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-4-recommended-tools-after-creating-a-token)

🧰 **Part 4: Recommended Tools After Creating a Token**

*   Creating a token is just the beginning. To manage it effectively, you need the right tools. CiaoTool offers a complete suite of features:
    

Feature

Use Case

Description

Batch Transfer

Airdrop to hundreds of addresses at once

Supports uploading spreadsheets or importing

Snapshot Export

Export token holder list

Useful for airdrops, governance, or rewards

Market Making

Operate multiple addresses for trading

Helps control the price curve

Batch Create Wallets

Generate hundreds of addresses at once

Supports Solana and BSC

Batch Collection

Recover assets from multiple addresses

Convenient for fund management

Vanity Wallets

Custom prefix wallet addresses

Suitable for branding projects

*   **Tutorials:** [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool)
    
*   **Telegram:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)
    

* * *

✅ With CiaoTool, creating a token no longer requires coding or running a node. As long as you have your wallet and assets ready, you can complete the full cycle from **“Idea → Token → Market.”**

> 🚀 The barrier to creating a token is getting lower, but the barrier to managing it is getting higher. The real competition isn’t about “who launches first,” but “who can operate it best.” May your first token on-chain become your key to the Web3 world.

# 创建/添加流动性「v2」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2)

**添加流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/add-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/add-liquidity-v2)

circle-info

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

circle-exclamation

创建前必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB**）

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#chuang-jian-tian-jia-liu-dong-xing-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 创建/添加流动性详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8AhGayayJ4AHNtEmNeFz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c71d944&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-2-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

**2️⃣ 选择加池的两种代币**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FW7W59pBfNoSt8Uw6eOR4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e408dd41&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-3-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

**3️⃣ 填写加池数量**

*   输入两种代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FH7IlbzsmUqJZYYVZMFX5%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2568d044&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

*   添加流动性时：会出现已经有的流动池详细，且价格固定，只需要输入TokanA的数量即可。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F4sWWKGzF5KAuJ4ekH62p%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c17ff827&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-4-shou-quan-dai-bi)

**4️⃣ 授权代币**

*   第一次操作时，需要授权合约使用你的代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-5-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing)

**5️⃣ 创建流动性**

*   检查无误后，点击“**开始交易”**按钮。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题**FAQ**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-1.-wei-shen-me-jia-chi-hui-shi-bai)

**1\. 为什么加池会失败？**

*   check
    
    钱包内 BNB /WBNB是否足够。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-2.-wo-chuang-jian-de-shi-wbnb-jiao-yi-dui-yong-hu-ke-yi-yong-usdt-mai-bi-ma)

**2\. 我创建的是 WBNB 交易对，用户可以用 USDT 买币吗？**

*   check
    
    可以的，即使你创建的是 WBNB 池：仍可用 USDT → BNB → 你的代币 链上交易是自动路由的，结果是相通的。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-3.-jia-chi-de-dai-bi-shu-liang-you-yao-qiu-ma)

**3\. 加池的代币数量有要求吗？**

*   check
    
    没有强制要求,你可以根据代币经济模型、想要的初始价格、市值目标、来灵活决定加池比例。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-4.-yu-gu-jia-ge-hou-mian-hui-bian-ma)

**4\. 预估价格后面会变吗？**

*   check
    
    会的，预估价格 = 上线初始价格，随着用户不断买卖，价格会实时变化，交易越多，价格波动越真实。
